viii 

 
CHAPTER I. GENERAL PROVISIONS 

§1. Purpose   

The purpose of these Enforcement Rules shall be to stipulate the matters referred by and the 
matters  necessary  for  the  enforcement  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Business  Regulation 
(hereinafter referred to as "the Regulation"). (Amended on February 3, 2009; July 31, 2009) 

§2. Definitions   

(1) The meanings of terms used in these Enforcement Rules shall be as follows. (Amended 
on February 3, 2009; April 12, 2023) 

1. “Issue using the first trading price as the base price” refers to an issue whose the first 
trading price determined in accordance with [§22] of the Regulation becomes the base 
price of the day within the range of quotations within the minimum quotation price and 
the maximum quotation price noted in [Annex 1], and it is classified as follows: 

(a)  Relisted issue and issue with listing change;   

(b) Issue  whose  paid-in  capital  is  reduced  (refers  to  the  case  where  paid-in  capital 
amount is  reduced according  to  reverse stock  split  or stock retirement of stocks 
held by minority shareholders); and 

(c)  Issue  that  resumes  trading  after  trading  has  been  halted  or  suspended  for  thirty 

(30) trading days or more. 

2.  “Relisted  issue”  refers  to  stocks  that  are  relisted  in  accordance  with  [§39]  of  the 
KOSDAQ  Market  Listing  Regulation  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “Listing 
Regulation”),  as  stocks  issued  by  corporations  noted  in  [§2(1)1c]  of  the  Listing 
Regulation. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

3. “Issue with listing change” refers to stocks that are issued by corporations (excluding 
corporations surviving after carving out noted in Article 530-12 of the Commercial Act) 
surviving after split-off or merger after split-off of a corporation listed on the KOSDAQ 
market  and  then  relisted  in  accordance  with  [§44]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Listing 
Regulations. (Amended on March 16, 2026) 

4.  “Issue  listed  after  merger”  refers  to  stocks  that  are  issued  by  a  corporation 
incorporated  according  to  the  merger  between  a  special  purpose  acquisition  company 

1 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
noted in  [§2(1)36] of the KOSDAQ Market  Listing  Regulation and a corporation  that 
has not listed its stocks on the stock market, and that are listed in accordance with [§76] 
of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation. 

(2) “Prices set by the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(6)3] of the Regulation shall refer to each 
of the following prices: (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

1. In the case of immediately executable offer limit quotation   

The price of the highest bid quotation (excluding bid quotation submitted at mid-price 
quotation; the same hereinafter in this Article) at the time of receipt of the relevant offer 
quotation. Provided that, in cases where there are no bid quotations, it shall be the price 
(the  lower  price  change  limit  shall  be  the  minimum)  which  is  one  (1)  quotation  price 
unit lower than the lowest offer price (excluding offer quotation submitted at mid-price 
quotation;  the  same  hereinafter  in  this  Article),  and  in  cases  where  there  is  no  bid  or 
offer  quotation,  it  shall  be  the  most  recent  market  price  (when  such  price  does  not 
match the quotation price unit, it shall be the closest price to such price among prices 
that  are  lower  than  such  price  and  match  the  quotation  price  unit).  (Amended  on 
February 27, 2025) 

2. In the case of immediately executable bid limit quotation   

The  price  of  the  lowest  offer  quotation  at  the  time  of  receipt  of  the  relevant  bid 
quotation.  Provided  that,  in  cases  where  there  are  no  offer  quotations,  it  shall  be  the 
price which is one (1) quotation price unit higher than the highest bid price (the upper 
price change limit shall be the maximum), and in cases where there is no bid or offer, it 
shall  be  the  most  recent  market  price  (when  such  price  does  not  match  the  quotation 
price unit, it shall be the closest price to such price among prices that are higher than 
such price and match the quotation price unit). (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(3) “Prices set by the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(6)4] of the Regulation shall refer to each 
of the following prices: (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

1.  In  the  case  of  best  limit  offer  quotation:  The  lowest  offer  price.  Provided  that,  in 
cases where there are no offer quotations, it shall be the most recent market price (when 
such price does not match the quotation price unit, it shall be the closest price to such 
price among prices that are higher than such price and match the quotation price unit). 
(Amended on February 27, 2025) 

2. In the case of best limit bid quotation: The highest bid price. Provided that, in cases 
where there are no bid quotations, it shall be the most recent market price (when such 
price does not match the quotation price unit, it shall be the closest price to such price 
among  prices  that  are  lower  than  such  price  and  match  the  quotation  price  unit). 
(Amended on February 27, 2025)   

2 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(4)  “Price  set  by  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§2(6)7]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  the 
simple arithmetic average of the best offer quotation price and the best bid quotation price 
at the time of continuous auction (anything less than KRW 1 is rounded down; hereinafter 
referred to as “mid-price”). [February 27, 2025]] 

(5)  “Conditions  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§2(6)8]  of  the  Regulation  shall 
refer to conditions in each of the followings: [February 27, 2025]] 

1. In the case of stop-limit sell quotations 

    The previous transaction price (if there is no previous transaction price, the base price is 
used; the same hereinafter in this Article) shall be equal to or lower than the stop price 
noted in [§2(6)8] of the Regulations (hereinafter referred to as the “stop price”). 

2. In the case of stop-limit buy quotations 

    The previous transaction price shall be equal to or higher than the stop price. 

[February 27, 2025] 

(6) “An index specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(8)1] of the Regulation shall refer 
to an index falling under any of the following subparagraphs (hereinafter referred to as the 
“index  for  index  arbitrage  trading”):  (Amended  on  October  14,  2005;  August  16,  2007; 
February 3, 2009; October 27, 2015; February 28, 2017; December 7, 2018; July 11, 2019)   

1. KOSDAQ 150 (referring to a market capitalization weighted stock price index based 
on 150 issues listed on the KOSDAQ Market, which is calculated by the Exchange using 
the base index of 1,000 on the base date of January 4, 2010; the same hereinafter);   

2.  KRX  300  (referring  to  a  market  capitalization  weighted  stock  price  index  based  on 
300 issues, from among the stocks listed on the KOSPI Market and the stocks listed on 
the  KOSDAQ  Market,  which  is  calculated  by  the  Exchange  using  the  base  index  of 
1,000 on the base date of January 4, 2010; the same hereinafter); and 

3.  KOSDAQ  Global  (referring  to  a  market  capitalization-weighted  stock  price  index 
calculated  by  the  Exchange,  based  on  the  shares  of  corporations  designated  by  the 
Exchange  in  accordance  with  [§3]  of  the  Guidelines  on  the  Designation  of  Global 
Companies  in  the  KOSDAQ  Market,  setting  the  index  of  1,000  on  the  base  date  of 
November 18, 2022). [January 15, 2026] 

(7) “A form set by the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(8)1] of the Regulation shall refer to any 
of the followings, and it shall include the case where a trade is carried out after splitting an 
order into two (2) or more orders. (Amended on June 28, 2005; February 3, 2009; March 21, 

3 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2018; December 7, 2018) 

1.  A  trade  in  which  the  sale  (including  the  final  settlement  of  a  buying  contract)  of 
futures contracts on an index for index arbitrage trading (including synthetic stock price 
index futures) is carried out at the same time or immediately after/before the purchase of 
a basket of stocks linked to the same index (hereinafter referred to as “a basket of stocks” 
in this Article); and   

2. A trade in which the purchase (including the final settlement of a selling contract) of 
futures  contracts  on  the  same  index  (including  synthetic  stock  price  index  futures)  is 
carried out at the same time or immediately after/before the sale of a basket of stocks.

index  put  options  while  selling  index  call  options  in  trading  of  options  on  an  index  for 
index  arbitrage  trading  of  the  domestic  index  options  market  noted  in  [§3(2)1]  of  the 
Derivatives  Market  Business  Regulation  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “trading  of  index 
options”), and the "purchase of synthetic stock price index futures" shall refer to selling of 
index put options while buying index call options in the trading of index options. [March 
21, 2018] (Amended on December 7, 2018; February 27, 2025)

the Regulation shall be classified based on the trust assets of each fund and the proprietary 
assets. (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 7, 2018) 

(10)  “Specific  number  set  forth  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§2(8)2]  of  the  Regulation 
shall  refer  to  ten  (10)  or  more  (calculated  including  issues  traded  at  multilateral  trading 
companies). In such cases, the number of stocks shall be calculated separately for each of 
buy  and  sell.  (Amended  on  February  3,  2009;  December  7,  2018;  January  24,  2019; 
February 27, 2025)

(m), this shall not apply to the case where it is otherwise specified in the market-making 
agreement. (Amended on January 15, 2026)

refer to the case where the price of different classes of stock of the day exceeds one point 
five (1.5) times of the price of common stock concerned. [January 14, 2010] (Amended on 
April 20, 2012; September 21, 2020) 

CHAPTER II. OPERATION OF THE MARKET   

§3. [Deleted on March 3, 2011] 

§4. Change of trading hours   

(1) “Case where it deems it necessary for market management” in [§4(4)] of the Regulation 
shall  refer  to  any  of  the  following  cases:  (Amended  on  June  28,  2005;  June  1,  2007; 
February 3, 2009; December 29, 2009) 

1.  In  the  case  of  failures  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  systems  and  member  systems,  and 
other computer system that are known to perform similar functions thereof (hereinafter 
referred to as “the computer system failure”);   

2. In the case of the first trading day of the year; and 

3. In addition, other cases where the Exchange deems it necessary to change the trading 
hours.   

(2) In the case of falling under paragraph (1)1, the trading hours in regular session shall, in 
principle, be extended for the duration of computer system failure,  but the market closing 
time may be extended to the time that Exchange deems it necessary. Provided that, if the 
system is not fully recovered by the market closing time, it shall be deemed that the trading 
was closed at the time the system failure occurred. (Amended on June 28, 2005; February 3, 
2009)   

(3) Failure of the member systems mentioned in paragraph (1)1 shall refer to the case when 
the sum  of the trades  executed by the members  who are experiencing  a  computer system 
failure  (referring  to  the  cases  where  members  are  unable  to  transmit  quotations  to  the 
Market through the member computer system, but excluding computer system failures that 
are  limited  to  specific  offices  of  the  members  or  specific  regions;  the  same  hereinafter) 
amounts to or exceed 75% of the total trading volume( based on the total volume of trades 

5 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
executed during twelve (12) months prior to the last day of the month preceding the month 
to which the day the system failed belongs and the cases of admission of new members as 
well  as  the  membership  withdrawal  shall  take  into  account.;  the  same  hereinafter).   
Provided that, in the case of total volume of trades of the members with the occurrence of 
system error being under 75% of the total volume of trades, pursuant to paragraph (1), the 
Exchange may regard it as an error of member system when the Exchange deems necessary 
considering  market  circumstances  of  each  following  subparagraphs:  [June  28,  2005] 
(Amended on February 3, 2009; December 18, 2013) 

1. Case of total  volume of trades  of the member with  the occurrence of  system error 
per member being over 75% of the total volume of trades in the KOSPI Market; and   

2.  Case  of  normal  market  operation  being  troubled  due  to  the  occurrence  of  member 
system error.   

§4-2. Designation of Trading Types   

“Case stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§7-2(4)] of the Regulation shall refer to the 
case of trading noted in any of the following subparagraphs: 

1. As a stock trade conducted pursuant to [§10(4)1 & 2] of the Regulation, when both 
the bid and offer quotations are submitted by a single member (in the case of member 
who  received  multiple  member  IDs  pursuant  to  [§7(3)],  it  shall  be  limited  to  the 
quotations placed under the same member ID; the same hereinafter in [§24(2)]) and the 
relevant member has submitted the application for cash settlement to the Exchange in 
accordance with the [Annex: Form No. 14] three (3) days before placing the quotations, 
the trade the Exchange deems it necessary; and 

2.  The  trade  according  to  buy-in  by  the  Exchange  pursuant  to  [§22]  of  the  Securities 
Market Clearing and Settlement Business Regulation. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(Wholly amended on December 30, 2011) 

§4-3. Guideline for Connection to Member System, etc. 

(1) “Matters stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§7-3(1)] of the Regulation shall refer 
to the matters noted in each of the following subparagraphs: 

1. Network connection method between the members and the Exchange; 

2.  Method  of  applying  for  and  allotting  the  communication  lines  and  the  sessions 
between the member and the Exchange;     

6 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
3. Prerequisites of security device noted in [§39(2)] of the Regulation; 

4. Criteria for allocation and operation of member session; and 

5.  In  addition,  the  matters  that  the  Exchange  deems  necessary  for  the  efficient  and 
reliable system operation.   

(2)  “Communication  line”  noted  in  paragraph  (1)  shall  refer  to  the  physical  line  used  to 
transmit  and  receive  the  quotations  and  trade  details  etc.  between  the  members  and  the 
Exchange,  and  “session”  shall  refer  to  the  logical  circuit  that  electronically  transmit  and 
receive the quotations and trade details etc. (Amended on February 28, 2014) 

[December 28, 2011] 

CHAPTER III. TRADING   

§5. [Deleted on December 4, 2007] 

§6. Quotation Receiving Hours   

(1)  “Quotation  receiving  hours  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§9(1)]  of  the 
Regulation  shall  refer  to  each  of  the  following  hours:  (Amended  on  February  3,  2009; 
March 19, 2009;  December 29, 2009;  July  29, 2010;  December 30, 2010;  June 24, 2014; 
May 19, 2015; June 21, 2016; April 3, 2019) 

1.  In  the  case  of  regular  session,  the  hours  noted  in  each  of  following  items  for  each 
trading type:   

(a) In the case of trading types other than those under items (b) and (c): From thirty 
(30) minutes before the  opening of trading  hours of the  regular session (hereinafter 
referred to as “market opening”) to the closing of trading hours (hereinafter referred 
to as “market closing”).   

(b)  Regular  session  block  trade  &  regular  session  basket  trade:  From  the  market 
opening to the market closing.   

(c) Regular session auction-based block trade: From the market opening to thirty (30) 
minutes before the market closing 

7 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2. In the case of off-hours sessions, each of the following hours:   

(a) For the pre-hours sessions, the hours classified for each trading type as follows:   

(i) Off-hours closing price trade: From 07:30 a.m. to 08:30 a.m.; and 

(ii) Off-hours block trade, off-hours basket trade and off-hours auction-based block 
trade: From 08:00 a.m. to 09:00 a.m. 

(b) For the after-hours sessions, the hours classified for each trading type as follows: 

(i)  Off-hours  closing  price  trade:  From  the  closing  time  of  the  regular  session  to 
04:00 p.m.; 

(ii)  Off-hours  call  auction  trade:  From  04:00  a.m.  to  06:00  p.m.  (In  the  case  of 
determining  closing  prices,  it  shall  be  until  the  time  when  the  price  concerned  is 
determined.); and 

(iii) Off-hours block trade and off-hours basket trade: From 03:40 p.m. to 06:00 p.m. 

(2) The Exchange may change the quotation receiving hours mentioned in paragraph (1) in 
the case falling under any of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

1. Where the trading hours has been changed pursuant to [§4(1)]; and   

2.  In  addition  to  subparagraph  1,  the  cases  that  are  deemed  necessary  for  the  market 
management.

§7-2. Collective Quoting of Order Details Relating to Several Accounts   

(1) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§9(1)] of the Regulation 
shall  refer  to  any  one  of  the  following  subparagraphs:  (Amended  on  February  3,  2009; 
September 24, 2012; September 10, 2019; November 23, 2023) 

1.  Where  a  member  engaged  in  the  discretionary  investment  business  submits 
quotations  using  an  account  in  its  own  name  upon  receiving  entrustment  of  orders  in 
order  to  manage  individual  discretionary  investment  property  efficiently  pursuant  to 
Article  99(2)4  of  the  Enforcement  Decree  of  the  Financial  Investment  Services  and 
Capital Markets Act (hereinafter referred to as “the Enforcement Decree of the Act”). In 
such  cases,  the  person  responsible  for  the  discretionary  investment  business  shall  be 
clearly noticeable;   

1-2.  Where  a  member  engaged  in  the  trust  business  submits  the  quotations  using  an 
account  in  its  own  name  upon  receiving  entrustment  of  orders  in  order  to  manage 
individual  trust  property  (excluding  trust  property  intending  to  acquire  or  dispose  the 
treasury  stocks)  efficiently  pursuant  to  Article  109(1)5  of  the  Enforcement  Decree  of 
the  Act.  In  such  cases,  the  person  responsible  for  the  trust  business  shall  be  clearly 
noticeable;   

2. Case of quoting the order details using an account in the name of a foreign financial 
investment  company  or  a  representative  investor  or  an  account  in  the  name  of  an 
investment  broker  to  manage  the  investment  of  foreign  investor  groups  (excluding 
foreigners treated as citizens) prescribed in the Regulations on the Financial Investment 
Business of the FSC; and   

3. Additionally, cases where, according to the relevant statutes, it is deemed necessary 
to quote order details using such accounts as those in investment broker’s name. 

15 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) In the case of quoting order details relating to multiple accounts pursuant to paragraph 
(1), the member shall use a separate account. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

[August 16, 2007] 

§7-3. Quotation Types 

The  type  of  quotation  that  the  members  may  submit  according  to  the  type  of  securities 
pursuant to [§9(3)] of the Regulation shall be as follows:   

1.  Case  of  stocks,  DRs  of  foreign  stocks  and  collective  investment  securities  of  ETF 
collective investment vehicle;   

Limit  quotation,  market  quotation,  limit-to-market-on-close  quotation,  best  limit 
quotation,  immediately  executable  quotation,  quotation  for  auction-based  block  trade, 
mid-price quotation, or stop-limit quotation (Amended on February 27, 2025)   

2.  Case  of  subscription  warrant,  subscription  right  certificates,  and  collective 
investment securities of business development collective investment vehicle; 

Limit quotation (Amended on March 16, 2026) 

[December 29, 2009]

(3) In cases where the quotation for auction-based block trade or limit quotation falls under

2010] (Amended on June 24, 2014) 

1. Case of quotations for auction-based block trade 

(a) Case where the quotation is submitted for the regular session trade (excluding the

In cases where the quotation is submitted for auction-based block trade. 

(4)  In  cases  where  the  quotation  quantity  exceeds  the  quantities  specified  in  each  of  the 
following  subparagraphs,  no  member  shall  input  such  quotations.  Provided  that,  this 
provision shall not apply to the quotations for block trading, basket trading, auction-based 
block trading, or the quotations placed pursuant to [§22] of the Securities Market Clearing 
and Settlement Business Regulation. (Amended on February 3, 2009; March 19, 2009; July 
29, 2010; June 24, 2014; September 12, 2018; February 27, 2025)   

1. Where the amount calculated by the Exchange for every trading day  by multiplying 
the base price determined in [Annex 1-2] (referred to as the “base price for the date of 
quotation  placement”  hereinafter  in  this  Paragraph)  by  the  number  of  listed  securities 
(referred to as the “market capitalization for the date of quotation placement” hereinafter 
in this Paragraph) is KRX 10 trillion or more; the quantity calculated by dividing KRW 
100 billion by the base price for the date of quotation placement (the quantity less than 
the trading unit of the regular session shall be rounded off to the trading unit; the same 
hereinafter in this Paragraph); 

18 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2.  Where  the  market  capitalization  for  the  date  of  quotation  placement  is  KRX  100 
billion  or  more  but  less  than  KRW  10  trillion;  the  quantity  equivalent  to  1/100  of  the 
number of listed securities; 

3. Where the market capitalization for the date of quotation placement is KRX 20 billion 
or  more  but  less  than  KRW  100  billion;  the  quantity  calculated  by  dividing  KRW  1 
billion by the base price for the date of quotation placement; and 

4. Where the market capitalization for the date of quotation placement is less than KRW 
20 billion; the quantity equivalent to 5/100 of the number of listed securities. 

(5) In cases where the quantity of entrustment that a member has received from a customer 
falls  under  the  quantity  specified  in  paragraph  (3),  the  quotations  shall  be  placed  by 
splitting the order quantity. (Amended on February 3, 2009)

§8-2. Conversion of Limit-to-market-on-close Quotations   

(1) Limit-to-market-on-close quotations shall be deemed, in accordance with [§9(4)] of the 
Regulation,  to  have  been  converted  into  the  market  quotations  according  to  each  of  the 
following priority: (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 29, 2009) 

1.  Offer  quotation  at  lower  price  shall  have  priority  over  offer  quotations  at  higher 
prices and a bid quotation at higher price shall have priority over the bid quotations at 
lower prices; and   

2. In the case of the quotations at the same price, priority shall be assigned according to 
the time when the quotations were received, thus the quotation received earlier having 
priority over the ones received later.   

(2) In cases where a limit-to-market-on-close quotation is converted into a market quotation 
pursuant  to  paragraph  (1),  the  converted  market  quotation  shall  be  deemed  to  have  been 
received at the beginning of the quotation receiving hours pursuant to the front part of main 
clause of [§20(1)2]. Provided that, it shall be deemed to have been received at the relevant 
time of resumption in the case of the latter part of the main clause of [§20(1)2], and it shall 
be deemed to have been received 10 minutes before the market  closing in the case of the 
proviso of [§20(1)4]. (Amended on February 3, 2009; May 19, 2015) 

21 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(3)  Pursuant  to  [§9(4)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  priority  for  the  validity  of  stop-limit 
quotations as limit quotations shall be as follows: [February 27, 2025] 

    1.  In  stop-limit  sell  quotations,  a  stop-limit  quotation  with  a  higher  stop  price  takes 
precedence over a stop-limit quotation with a lower stop price; [February 27, 2025] 

    2.  In  stop-limit  buy  quotations,  a  stop-limit  quotation  with  a  lower  stop  price  takes 
precedence over a stop-limit quotation with a higher stop price; and [February 27, 2025] 

    3.  In cases  where stop prices  are the same, the stop-limit  quotation  received first takes 
precedence  over  the  stop-limit  quotation  received  later,  based  on  the  time  the  stop-limit 
quotation was received. [February 27, 2025] 

(4) In applying [§17(2)2] of the Regulations to the stop-limit quotation whose validity as a 
limit  quotation  is  triggered  pursuant  to  paragraph  (3),  the  time  at  which  the  stop-limit 
quotation triggers into a limit quotation shall be deemed as the time of receiving the stop-
limit quotation. [February 27, 2025] 

[June 28, 2005]   

§8-3. Matters for Inspection of Quotation Suitability, etc.

Listing  Regulation  or  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Disclosure  Regulation  (hereinafter 
referred to as “the Disclosure Regulation”). (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

3. With regard to quantity of quotation, the matters in each of the following items: 

(a) Trading quantity unit under [§18(1)]; 

22 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(b) Quotation quantity limit under [§8(4)];

and

of the Regulation.

§8-4. Methods of Verifying Covered Short Sale   

(1)  “Manner  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§9-2(3)3]  of  the  Regulation  shall 
refer to the preservation of the documents, tape recordings or electronic storage devices that 
validate the date and details of orders, which the member received from a customer, for a 
period of longer than three (3) years that is determined by the member.   

(2) [Deleted on February 28, 2017] 

[March 12, 2009] 

§8-5. Restrictions of Quotations for Covered Short Sale 

(1)  “Covered  short  sale  quotations  placed  to  conduct  the  trades  stipulated  in  the 
Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to the part other than subparagraphs of [§9-2(6)] of the 
Regulation  shall  refer  to  any  of  the  followings:  (Amended  on  March  12,  2009;  July  29, 
2010; December 18, 2013; February 28, 2017; March 12, 2021) 

1.  Quotations  falling  under  any  of  subparagraphs  5  through  7  of  [§9-3(2)]  of  the 
Regulation;   

2.  Liquidity  providing  quotations  pursuant  to  [§12-2(1)]  of  the  Regulation  and  market 
making quotations stipulated in [§12-7(1)] of the Regulation; or 

3. Other quotations placed for the trades that the Exchange deems necessary. 

24 

 
 
 
 
     
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2)  “Issues  falling  under  the  criteria  set  by  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§9-2(6)1]  of  the 
Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  issues  that  fall  under  any  of  the  following  requirements 
(limited to the stock certificates and the DRs of foreign stocks, and hereinafter referred to 
as the “overheated  short sale issues”). [September 24, 2012] (Amended  on December 18, 
2013; February 28, 2017; September 19, 2017; July 11, 2019; August 26, 2022; April 12, 
2023; February 27, 2025) 

1. Issues of which the stock price decline rate, the proportion of short sale trading value 
to the market, and the increase rate of short sale trading value meet all of the following 
Items: 

(a) The closing price of the day shall be not less than 90/100 and not more than 95/100 

of the base price of the day; 

    (b) The proportion of the trading value of covered short sale to the trading value of the 
day shall be at least three (3) times (if the value is greater than 0.2, it shall be set at 
0.2)  the  proportion  of  the  trading  value  of  covered  short  sale  (numbers  shall  be 
rounded  off  to  the  third  decimal  point)  of  the  quarter  immediately  preceding  the 
quarter  in  which  the  relevant  trading  day  falls  to  the  total  trading  value  of  the 
constituent stocks of KOSDAQ 150 index of the same period; and 

    (c) The trading value of covered short sale of the day shall be at least five (5) times 
the average of the trading value of covered short sale for the latest forty (40) trading 
days. 

    2. Issues of which the stock price decline rate and the increase rate of short sale trading 

value meet all of the following Items: 

    (a) The closing price of the day shall be 90/100 or lower of the base price of the day;   

and 

    (b) The requirement in Subparagraph 1(c) shall be satisfied. 

    3.  Issues  of  which  the  proportion  and  the  increase  rate  of  the  trading  value  of  covered 

short sale meet all of the following Items: 

(a)   The average proportion of the trading value of covered short sale for the latest 

                forty (40) trading days shall be 5/100 or more; and 

(b)   The requirement in Subparagraph 1(c) shall be satisfied. 

25 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
    4. Issues of which the stock price decline rate and the proportion and the increase rate of 

the trading value of covered short sale meet all of the following Items: 

(a)   The closing price of the day shall be 97/100 or lower of the base price of the day; 

(b) The proportion of trading value of covered short sale to trading value of the day is 

30% or more; and (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

        (c) The trading value of covered short sale of the day shall be at least two (2) times the 
average of the trading value of covered short sale for the latest forty (40) trading 
days. 

(3) When calculating the trading value of covered short sale, trading value of the day, and 
trading value of the constituent stocks of KOSDAQ 150 index in paragraph (2), the trading 
value at multilateral trading companies (limited to each trading value during trading hours 
when covered short sale is possible; the same hereinafter in the paragraph) shall be included 
in the calculation. Provided that, in cases where the Exchange cannot receive information 
on  the  trading  value  of  a  multilateral  trading  company  due  to  system  failure,  etc.,  it  may 
calculate it excluding the information. [February 27, 2025] 

(4)  Notwithstanding  paragraphs  (2)  and  (3),  stocks  falling  under  each  of  following 
subparagraphs shall be excluded from the overheated short sale issues: [February 27, 2025] 

    1. Issues using the first trading price as the base price; [February 27, 2025] 

    2. Newly listed issues noted in [§17(1)2(a)]; [February 27, 2025] 

    3. Issues for which trading is not established during the regular market hours of the day 
and  the  trading  hours  of  multilateral  trading  companies  corresponding  to  the  regular 
market hours of the Exchange. In this case, if the trading information of the multilateral 
trading company cannot be received due to system failure, etc., the stock is considered as 
one  for  which  no  transaction  has  been  concluded  at  the  multilateral  trading  company; 
[February 27, 2025] 

    4. Issues scheduled to be delisted; [February 27, 2025] 

5. Issues for which the number of trading days with executed trades during each trading 
hour,  where  covered  short  sale  is  possible  during  trading  hours  of  the  Exchange  and 
multilateral trading companies, is less than twenty (20) days within the latest forty (40) 
trading  days.  In  this  case,  if  transaction  information  from  the  multilateral  trading 
company cannot be received due to computer failure, etc., the stock is considered as one 
for  which  no  transaction  has  been  concluded  at  the  multilateral  trading  company; 

26 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[February 27, 2025] 

(5)  The  Exchange  may  restrict  the  quotations  for  covered  short  sale  issues  specified  in 
paragraph (2) for one (1) day of the next trading day. Provided that, if the closing price of 
the  relevant  issue  on  the  day  when  the  restriction  of  covered  short  sale  quotation  is 
terminated is 95/100 or less of the base price of the day, the restriction of covered short sale 
quotation shall be extended until the next trading day and applied repeatedly at the end of 
every extension period. [August 26, 2022]   

(6) Notwithstanding paragraphs (2) through (5), in cases where it is deemed necessary for 
the management of the market by the Exchange due to reasons including sudden changes in 
market  conditions,  the  Exchange  may  set  differently  the  criteria  of  overheated  short  sale 
issues  under  paragraph  (2)  and  restriction  period  for  quotation  of  overheated  short  sale 
issues under paragraph (5). [March 9, 2020] (Amended on August 26, 2022; February 27, 
2025) 

(7)  The  Exchange  shall  officially  announce  the  overheated  short  sale  issues  specified  in 
paragraph (2) immediately and notify it to the members. [February 28, 2017] (Amended on 
September 19, 2017; March 9, 2020; August 26, 2022) 

(8) The notification to the members noted in paragraph (7) shall refer to the methods falling 
under any of the following subparagraphs: [November 26, 2020] (Amended on August 26, 
2022; February 27, 2025) 

1.  Posting on the electronic media operated by the Exchange; 

2.  Posting on the securities information terminals; 

3.  Publishing in the Daily Stock Market Review; and 

4.  Notification in a written form   

§8-6. Index Arbitrage Trades, etc. 

(1) “Trade stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§9-3(2)1] of the Regulation shall refer 
to the trade falling under any of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Index arbitrage trades under [§2(8)1] of the Regulation; 

2.  A  trade  in  which  the  sale  (including  the  final  settlement  of  a  buying  contract)  of 
futures contracts on a sector index (referring to an index calculated by industrial group 
or  category  with  listed  stocks  on  the  KOSDAQ  market.  The  same  shall  applies 
hereinafter) is carried out at the same time or immediately before/after the purchase of 

27 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
a basket of stocks linked to the sector index; and 

3.  A trade in which the purchase (including the final settlement of a selling contract) 
of  futures  contracts  on  a  sector  index  is  carried  out  at  the  same  time  or  immediately 
before/after the sale of a basket of stocks linked to the sector index. 

(2) The provision of [§9(3)] shall apply mutatis  mutandis to the case of selling or buying 
pursuant to subparagraphs 2 and 3 of paragraph (1). 

[March 12, 2021] 

§9. Stock Arbitrage Trading 

(1)  “Trade  that  is  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§9-3(2)1-2]  of  the  Regulation 
shall  refer  to  the  trade  falling  under  any  of  the  following  subparagraphs:  (Amended  on 
December 27, 2018) 

1. A trade where the sale (including the final settlement of a buying contract) of single 
stock  futures  (including  the  synthetic  stock  futures)  based  on  the  relevant  underlying 
stocks  is  carried  out  at  the  same  time  or  immediately  after/before  the  purchase  of 
underlying stocks; and   

2.  A  trade  where  the  purchase  (including  the  final  settlement  of  a  selling  contract)  of 
single  stock  futures  (including  the  synthetic  stock  futures)  based  on  the  relevant 
underlying stocks is carried out at the same time or immediately after/before the sale of 
underlying stocks.   

(2) “Sale of synthetic stock futures” mentioned in paragraph (1) shall refer to the purchase 
of  a  put  option  while  selling  a  call  option,  and  the  "purchase  of  synthetic  stock  futures" 
shall refer to the sale of a put option while buying a call option. (Amended on December 27, 
2018)   

(3)  The  purchase  and  sale  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1)  shall  include  the  purchase  and  sale 
carried  out  through  a  single  order  or  those  carried  out  by  splitting  the  order  into  several 
smaller orders.   

[February 3, 2009] 

§9-2. [Deleted on March 12, 2021] 

28 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§9-3. Arbitrage Trading of DRs 

(1) “Trade stipulated in the Enforcement Rule” in [§9-3(2)3] of the Regulation shall refer to 
the trade that falls under any of the followings: (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

1. Trades where the sale of the underlying stocks of DRs is carried out at the same time 
or  immediately  after  or  before  the  purchase  of  the  relevant  DRs  (including  DRs  of 
foreign stocks: the same hereinafter in this Article); and   

2. Trades where the purchase of the underlying stocks of DRs is carried out at the same 
time or immediately after or before the sale of the relevant DRs.   

(2) The provisions of [§9(3)] shall apply mutatis mutandis to the purchase or sale pursuant 
to paragraph (1). (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

[June 28, 2005]   

§9-4. Restrictions on Quotation Prices for Covered Short Sale 

(1) Pursuant to [§9-3(3)] of the Regulation, the proviso to [§9-3(1)] of the Regulation shall 
not  apply  to  the  case  that  falls  under  any  of  the  following  subparagraphs:  (Amended  on 
December 30, 2010) 

1. Case where the opening price is not yet determined; and   

2. When the opening price is the same as the most recent market price [in the case of 
determining the opening price of the first trading day for the issue using the first trading 
price as the  base price, the  appraisal  price specified in  Annex 1 (the lowest  quotation 
price if  no  appraisal price is  available), and in any  other  cases, it shall be the  closing 
price  of  the  most  recent  trading  day,  but  if  the  base  price  is  available,  the  base  price 
shall be used], the case where no price that is different from the relevant price has been 
determined.   

(2) The provisions of [§9-3] of the Regulation shall not apply to the regular session block 
trade, regular session auction-based block trade, regular session basket trade and off-hours 
session (excluding the off-hours periodic call trade). (Amended on July 29, 2010; June 24, 
2014) 

[February 3, 2009] 

§9-5. Follow-up Management of Short Sale Quotations   

29 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(1) The member shall preserve the relevant records and relevant materials pursuant to [§9-
4(1)] of the Regulation for the period determined by the member, which is longer than three 
(3) years. (Amended on September 24, 2012) 

(2)  In  verifying  the  balance  of  securities  held  and  quantity  of  securities  to  be  settled 
pursuant  to  [§9-4(1)1]  of  the  Regulation,  if  the  customer  has  electronically  registered  the 
relevant securities through trust companies or depository institutions, members shall obtain 
a  notification  on  the  status  of  settlement  shortage  from  the  trust  companies  or  the 
depository  institutions  in  accordance  with  [Annex:  Form  No.  1],  by  12:00  noon  on  the 
settlement  date.  In  such  cases,  if  a  trust  company  or  a  depository  institution  notifies  the 
customer  of  the  information  on  settlement  shortage  via  the  information  network  of  the 
Korea Securities Depository (hereinafter referred to as “KSD”) (limited to the case where 
reasons for the settlement failure are stated according to the classifications in [Annex: Form 
No. 1]), it shall be deemed that such notification has been made in accordance with [Annex: 
Form No. 1]. (Amended on September 24, 2012; December 18, 2013; September 10, 2019) 

(3) “The latest six (6) months” in the part other than each subparagraph of [§9-4(4)] of the 
Regulation  shall  be  calculated  by  counting  from  the  day  when  the  Exchange  verified  the 
fact  that  the  customer  sold  the  securities  not  in  possession  or  securities  that  cannot  be 
settled by the settlement day. (Amended on September 24, 2012; March 16, 2026)             

(4)  When  the  entire  selling  securities  are  collected  as  the  entrustment  guarantee  money 
during the 120-day period  from  the trading day  following  the  settlement  date pursuant  to 
[§42(5)2],  each  item  under  [§9-4(4)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  not  apply.  [December  18, 
2013] (Amended on December 27, 2018; March 16, 2026) 

[March 12, 2009] 

§10.  Methods  of  Submitting  Quotations  for  Trading  of  Treasury  Stocks  of  Listed 
Corporations, etc. 

(1)  The  quotations  under  [§10]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  made  according  to  each  of  the 
following methods: (Amended on October 14, 2005; September 8, 2006; February 3, 2009; 
December 30, 2010; April 20, 2012; April 26, 2013; April 12, 2023)   

1.  The  quotations  shall  be  placed  at  the  price  that  is  consistent  with  [§10]  of  the 
Regulation. In such cases, for the issues whose closing price of the previous day does 
not match up with the quotation price unit and the issues that have gone ex-dividends, 
ex-rights,  and  stock  split  or  reverse  stock  split,  and  the  initially  listed  issues  falling 
under [§17(1)2a] on the day of placing such quotation, the base price of the day shall be 
deemed to be the closing prices of the previous day, and in the case of determining the 
first  price  of  the  first  trading  day  of  an  issue  using  the  first  trading  price  as  the  base 
price, the appraisal price noted in [Annex 1] (if no appraisal price is available, it shall 

30 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
be the lowest quotation  price) shall be deemed to be the closing price of  the previous 
day. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

2. In the case of placing quotations pursuant to [§10(1)] of the Regulation, the quotation 
quantity shall be within the larger quantity among the quantities specified in each of the 
following  items  (the  quantity  below  the  trading  unit  shall  be  rounded  down  to  the 
trading quantity unit; the same hereinafter in this Subparagraph). Provided that, in cases 
where such quantity exceeds 1/100 of the total number of shares issued, it should be the 
quantity within 1/100 thereof:   

(a)  Quantities  equivalent  to  10/100  of  the  number  of  stocks  intended  to  acquire 
(dispose), which the listed company reported to  the Financial Services Commission 
for the purpose of acquiring (disposing) its treasury stocks; and   

(b)  Quantities  equivalent  to  25/100  of  average  daily  trading  volume  for  one  (1) 
month  retroactive  from  the  day  before  the  date  when  the  listed  company  filed  the 
report on acquiring (or disposing) its treasury stocks with the FSC.   

3. In applying [§10(1)2] of the Regulation, if the higher price or lower price of the same 
subparagraph does not match the quotation price unit, the upper limit and lower limit of 
the same subparagraph shall be calculated according to the following items: [February 
27, 2025] 

          (a) In the case of higher limit: 

          Among the price that is lower than the last price and matches the quotation price unit, 
the price that is five (5) quotation price unit higher than the closest price to such price. 
[February 27, 2025] 

          (b) In the case of lower limit: 

          Among the price that is higher than the last price and matches the quotation price unit, 
the price that is five (5) quotation price unit lower than the closest price to such price. 
[February 27, 2025] 

(2) No member shall be allowed to cancel the quotation after placing a quotation pursuant 
to paragraph (1). (Amended on October 14, 2005; February 3, 2009)   

(3) “The manner stipulated in the Enforcement Rules within the period stipulated therein” 
in [§10(3)] of the Regulation shall refer to “the submission of the application for purchase 
of treasury stocks of Listed Company [Annex:  Form No.  1-2] during the period from the 
market closing time of the previous trading day to 18:00 hours” (Amended on December 4, 
2007; February 3, 2009; March 12, 2009)   

31 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(4) The application under paragraph (3) shall be submitted in a form of electronic document. 
Provided that, in cases where due to the computer system failure, the application cannot be 
submitted  in  a  form  of  electronic  document  or  the  details  to  be  submitted  cannot  be 
confirmed,  it  may  be  submitted  via  facsimile,  etc.  [December  23,  2005]  (Amended  on 
December 23, 2005; February 3, 2009) 

(5) In the case of the issues that have no record of trade execution in the regular session, the 
most recent execution price noted in [§10(1)2] of the Regulation shall be deemed the base 
price  of  the  day,  and  when  the  expected  best  quotation  price  is  announced  pursuant  to 
[§52(1)1], the best bid quotation and the best offer quotation in the same subparagraph shall 
be  construed  as  the  expected  best  bid  quotation  and  the  expected  best  offer  quotation, 
respectively.  [September  8,  2006]  (Amended  on  December  4,  2007;  February  3,  2009; 
March 19, 2009; May 19, 2015; February 27, 2025) 

(6)  In  the  case  of  the  off-hours  block  trade  pursuant  to  [§10(4)  &  (5)]  of  the  Regulation, 
paragraph (3) shall apply mutatis mutandis to the matters concerning the submission of the 
application for transaction of treasury stocks. [September 8, 2006] (Amended on December 
4, 2007; February 3, 2009) 

§11. Special Case of Bid Quotation Price for Acquisition of Treasury Stocks   

(1) When intending to acquire the treasury stocks of a listed company by way of the method 
stipulated  in  [§11(1)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  member  shall  place  the  quotations  in 
accordance  with  manner  noted  in  each  of  the  following  subparagraphs:  (Amended  on 
October 14, 2005; December 4, 2007; February 3, 2009; December 30, 2010)   

1.  The  quotations  shall  be  submitted  at  the  price  that  is  consistent  with  each 
subparagraph of [§10(1)] of the Regulation.  In such cases, the latter part of [§10(1)1] 
shall apply mutatis mutandis thereto; and   

2. Quotation quantity shall be equal to or less than the quantity decided by the board of 
directors.   

(2) The provisions of [§10] shall apply mutatis mutandis to the trading matters other than 
those mentioned in paragraph (1). (Amended on December 4, 2007; February 3, 2009)   

§12. Trading Methods of Treasury Stocks of Listed Corporations under Money Trust 
Contract   

Provisions  of  [§10]  and  [§11]  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis  to  the  case  where  a  member 
places  a  quotation  for  trading  of  treasury  stocks  under  money  trust  contract  using  the 
method  stipulated  in  [§12]  of  the  Regulation.  In  such  cases,  the  quotation  quantity  in 

32 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[§10(1)2] shall be equal to or less than 1/100 of the total number of shares issued; and the 
quotation  quantity  in  [§11(1)2]  shall  be  equal  to  or  less  than  the  maximum  acquirable 
quantity within the total money trust asset. (Amended on February 3, 2009)   

(Wholly amended on September 8, 2006) 

§12-2. [Deleted on March 25, 2013] 

§12-3. Notification of Employee Responsible for Liquidity Provision Task 

In  cases  where  the  employee  responsible  for  the  task  of  liquidity  provision  has  been 
designated pursuant to [§12-2(2)2] of the Regulation, the member shall notify the employee 
concerned  to  the  Exchange  without  delay  and  shall  do  the  same  when  the  employee 
responsible for liquidity provision task has been changed. [December 4, 2007] (Amended 
on February 3, 2009) 

§12-4. Agreement for Liquidity Provision 

(1) “Details stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§12-3(1)] of the Regulation shall refer 
to each of the following details: (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 30, 2010) 

1. Names of the member and the listed corporation;   

2. Matters about the quotation spread;   

3. Matters about the quotation quantity;   

4. Term of the agreement for liquidity provision;   

5. Matters about the service charge, etc. relating to liquidity provision; 

6.  In  the  case  of  including  a  clause  that  stipulates  when  the  daily  trading  volume 
resulting  from  the  liquidity  providing  quotations  placed  by  a  member  during  the  day 
reaches to a certain quantity, such member is exempted from the obligation to place the 
liquidly providing quotations, such quantity. In such cases, the quantity concerned shall 
satisfy any one of the following items:   

(a) It shall exceed 50/100 of the average daily trading volume of the previous month 
of  the  quotation  submission  day  (in  cases  where  the  number  of  days  when  the 
relevant issue was traded is less than 50/100 of the trading days of the Market, it shall 
be advanced in a sequential order); and   

33 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(b) It shall be at least 5/1000 of the total number of listed shares.   

6-2. In the case of stating that the requirement for submission of bid liquidity providing 
quotation  shall be exempted, in  the event  that  the quantity  of stocks  acquired through 
the liquidity providing quotations exceeds 2/100 of total listed shares (shall be based on 
the  settlement  date),  until  the  quantity  of  shares  exceeding  2/100  is  brought  down  to 
15/1000 of listed shares, the relevant details;   

7.  The  clause  stating  that,  in  conjunction  with  the  liquidity  provision,  the  securities 
related  laws  and  the  regulations  relating  to  the  business  of  the  Exchange  shall  be 
observed.   

(2) When entering  into an agreement for liquidity  provision pursuant  to  [§12-3(2)] of the 
Regulation, terminating the relevant agreement thereafter, or changing the material details 
of the agreement, such facts shall be notified to the Exchange in accordance with [Annex: 
Form  No.  6-2]  at  least  three  (3)  trading  days  before  the  relevant  agreement,  etc.  become 
effective. Provided that, in the case of unavoidable circumstance where the agreement for 
liquidity provision has to be terminated without delay, the Exchange may be notified at the 
time when such circumstance has occurred. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(3)  In  cases  where  more  than  two  (2)  members  enter  into  an  agreement  for  liquidity 
provision with a same listed company, the details specified in paragraphs (1)2 and(1)3 shall 
be the same. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

[December 4, 2007] 

§12-5. Exemption from Obligation to Submit Liquidity Providing Quotations 

The “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” stated in the proviso to [§12-4(1)] of the 
Regulation  shall  be  the  cases  falling  under  any  one  of  the  following  subparagraphs: 
(Amended  on  February  3,  2009;  March  19,  2009;  December  30,  2010;  March  3,  2011; 
March 25, 2013; April 3, 2019) 

1. Where the quotation spread ratio is within the limit specified in each subparagraph of 
[§12-4(1)] of the Regulation. In such cases, when only offer (or bid) quotation has been 
submitted,  the  lower  (upper)  limit  price  shall  be  deemed  to  be  the  best  bid  (offer) 
quotation;   

2.  Where  there  is  no  quotation  price  unit  that  could  reduce  the  quotation  spread  ratio 
within the range stipulated in each subparagraph of [§12-4(1)] of the Regulation;   

3. When the price is  determined by the  call auction pursuant  to  [§20(1)], cases  of the 

34 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
   
 
 
quotation receiving hours and within five (5) minutes immediately after the closing of 
such quotation receiving hours;   

4.  In  the  case  of  determining  the  opening  price  pursuant  to  [§27],  case  of  from  thirty 
(30) minutes before the opening of the regular session to the time that has not  passed 
five (5) minutes after the market opening;   

5. [Deleted on December 30, 2010] 

6. [Deleted on December 30, 2010]   

7. In the case of a stock for which the details specified in [§12-4(1)6] has been included 
in the agreement for liquidity provision, when the trading volume exceeds that quantity;   

7-2. As a case of stating the details noted in [§12-4(1)6-2] in the agreement for liquidity 
provision,  in  the  event  that  the  quantity  of  shares  acquired  through  the  liquidity 
providing quotations falls under the condition noted in the agreement, the bid liquidity 
providing quotation; and   

8.  Additionally,  in  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  them  necessary  for  the  market 
management  for  the  reasons  such  as  the  sudden  change  in  the  quotation  or  trading 
conditions.   

[December 4, 2007] 

§12-6. Methods of Submitting Liquidity Providing Quotations   

(1) Pursuant to the proviso to [§12-5(1)] of the Regulation, in cases where it is difficult to 
apply  the  price  in  each  subparagraph  of  [§12-5(1)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  quotation  price 
shall be determined in the manner noted in each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended 
on February 3, 2009; March 19, 2009; December 30, 2010;  March 3, 2011; February 28, 
2014) 

1.  During  the  quotation  receiving  hours  for  call  auction,  the  price  determined  in 
accordance  with  the  main  sentence  of  each  subparagraph  of  [§12-5(1)]  of  the 
Regulation  by  assuming  that  the  expected  best  offer  (bid)  quotation  price  is  the  best 
offer (bid) quotation price;   

2.  Where  there  is  no  quotation  on  both  sides,  the  most  recent  market  price  shall  be 
regarded  as  price  determined  in  accordance  with  each  subparagraph  (in  the  case  of 
trading  hours  for  call  auction,  only  the  main  sentence  of  each  subparagraph)  of  [§12-
5(1)] of the Regulation by assuming that the most recent market price is the best offer 
(bid) price. In such cases, when the most recent market price is different from the base 

35 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
price  during  the  quotation  receiving  hours  for  the  determination  of  opening  price,  the 
base price shall deem to be the most recent market price, and in the case of calculating 
the opening price of the first trading day of the issue using the first trading price as the 
base price, the appraisal price specified in Annex 1 (if no appraisal price is available, it 
shall be the lowest quotation price) shall deem to be the most recent price;   

3. Where only offer (bid) quotations have been placed, the price of bid (offer) quotation 
shall be the best offer (bid) price of issue concerned, and the lower (upper) price limit, 
which  is  the  price  [within  the  limit  of  lower  (upper)  limit  price],  shall  be  the  lowest 
(highest) price among the prices falling within the ratio pursuant to [§12-4(1)1] of the 
Regulation. Provided that, no quotation at the best bid (offer) price shall be submitted 
during the trading hours for continuous call auction if the liquidity providing quotation 
at best offer (bid) price (including the liquidity providing quotations submitted by other 
member) has already been submitted; and 

4.  When  the  expected  matching  price  is  not  published  during  the  quotation  receiving 
hours for determination of opening price, the price determined in accordance with the 
main  sentence  of  each  subparagraph  of  [§12-5(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  used  by 
assuming that the base price is the best offer (bid) quotation price. 

5. [Deleted on February 28, 2014] 

(2) [Deleted on March 25, 2013] 

(3) In cases where it is necessary to place a liquidity providing quotation on the other side 
immediately after placing a liquidity providing quotation on one side pursuant to the main 
sentence  of  [§12-5(3)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  quotation  shall  be  placed  at  the  price  that 
satisfy  the  range  specified  in  [§12-4(1)]  of  the  Regulation.  Provided  that,  if  there  is  no 
quotation price unit that makes possible the submission within the range specified in [§12-
4(1)] of the Regulation,  in  the case of  offer  quotation,  the quotation may be submitted at 
price that is one (1) quotation price unit higher than the best bid price; and in the case of bid 
quotation, the quotation may be submitted at the price that is one (1) quotation price unit 
lower than the best offer quotation. (Amended on February 3, 2009; March 19, 2009) 

(4) In cases where a member submits a liquidity providing quotation pursuant to [§12-5(2)] 
of  the  Regulation,  the  quantity  shall  be  higher  than  the  amount  specified  in  each  of  the 
following subparagraphs. Provided that, when providing the offer (bid) liquidity providing 
quotations at best bid (offer) quotation price, such liquidity providing quotations shall be of 
the  quantity  that  is  larger  than  the  quantity  specified  in  subparagraph  1  but  less  than  the 
sum  of  the  quantities  of  best  bid  (offer)  quotations  (shall  not  apply  to  the  liquidity 
providing  quotation  submitted  first,  if  both  the  offer  quotation  and  bid  quotation  are  not 
available): (Amended on February 3, 2009; March 3, 2011) 

1.  In  the  case  of  stocks,  the  quantity  that  the  listed  corporation  has  reported  to  the 

36 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Exchange, which is larger than ten (10) times the trading quantity unit.   

2. [Deleted on March 25, 2013] 

(5) In cases where pursuant to [§12-5(2)] of the Regulation, a member corrects the prices of 
the liquidity providing quotations which are not yet executed, the quotation quantity shall 
be larger than the smaller of the quantities specified in each of the following subparagraphs. 
Provided that, in the case of correcting the price of offer (bid) liquidity quotation for stocks 
to the best bid (offer) quotation price, the quantity shall be higher than the smaller of the 
quantities noted in each of the following subparagraphs, but less than the sum of quantities 
of bid (offer) quotations: (Amended on February 3, 2009; March 3, 2011) 

1. The quantity specified in each subparagraph of paragraph (4); and 

2. The entire unexecuted quantity. 

(6) When submitting liquidity providing quotations, a liquidity providing member shall not 
entrust it to another member. [May 7, 2021] 

[December 4, 2007] 

§12-7. Exceptions to Obligation to submit Quotations on Both Sides   

Pursuant to the proviso to [§12-5(3)] of the Regulation, in the case of falling under any one 
of the following subparagraphs, the liquidity providing quotations on the relevant side may 
not  be  submitted:  (Amended  on  February  3,  2009;  March  19,  2009;  December  30,  2010; 
March 25, 2013) 

1. Where either side of bid or offer quotations includes the liquidity providing quotation 
submitted by the relevant member, the case of placing a quotation on that side;   

2. [Deleted on March 25, 2013] 

3. Where the quotations fall under [§12-8(1-2)] or [§12-8(1-3)]; and   

4.  In  the  event  that  a  liquidity  providing  quotation  must  be  placed  on  the  other  side 
immediately after placing a liquidity providing quotation on one side, the case where a 
quotation price unit that would reduce the quotation spread ratio below the ratio noted 
in [§12-4(1)] of the Regulation is not available.   

[December 4, 2007] 

37 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§12-8. Restriction on Submission of Liquidity Providing Quotations   

Pursuant  to  [§12-5(4)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  members  shall  not  submit  a  liquidity 
providing  quotation  in  the  cases  falling  under  any  one  of  the  following  subparagraphs: 
(Amended on February 3, 2009; December 30, 2010; March 25, 2013; September 10, 2019) 

1. Case of falling under the conditions under Article 71(2) of the Financial Investment 
Services and Capital Markets Act (hereinafter referred to as “the Act”);   

1-2. Where the quantity held by the member company is less than the quantity specified 
in [§12-6(4)], the offer quotation;   

1-3. Where the quantity held by the member company exceeds the quantity obtained by 
subtracting the quantity  noted in each  subparagraph of [§12-6(4)] from the number of 
total listed shares, the bid quotation;   

2. Where quotations have been already submitted on any one side of offer or bid, the 
case of placing a liquidity providing quotation on such side.   

[December 4, 2007] 

§12-9. Assessment of Liquidity Providing Members   

(1) The Exchange may, pursuant to [§12-6(1)] of the Regulation, assess the members who 
provide a liquidity providing quotation  for stocks against the matters  specified in  each of 
the  following  subparagraphs  for  each  quarter  and  make  public  the  outcome  thereof; 
(Amended on February 3, 2009; December 27, 2018) 

1. The extent of obligation to submit liquidity providing quotation has been fulfilled;   

2.  The  extent  of  contribution  made  to  the  improvement  of  quotation  spread  ratio  of 
concerned issue following the submission of liquidity providing quotations; and   

3. The eagerness in submitting liquidity providing quotations.   

4. Compliance with the securities-related laws and regulations and the business-related 
regulations of the Exchange with respect to the liquidity provision. 

(2) In conducting an assessment pursuant to paragraph (1), in cases where a member did not 
submit  the  liquidity  providing  quotations  for  any  of  the  issues,  to  which  it  is  obliged  to 
submit liquidity providing quotations, for at least thirty (30) minutes on the average a day, 
the  lowest  rating  shall  be  given  to  such  member  regardless  of  the  performance  on  other 
issues. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

38 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(3)  Members  shall  notify  the  details  that  the  Exchange  requires  for  the  assessment, 
including  the  specifics  about  the  non-submission  of  liquidity  providing  quotations  during 
the relevant quarter as a result of falling under any of the following cases, by the end of the 
quarter concerned: (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 30, 2010) 

1. Any one of the cases in subparagraphs 7 through 8 of [§12-5]; and   

2. Any one of the cases in subparagraphs 1 through 1-3 of [§12-8].   

(4) In addition to paragraphs (1) through (3), the Exchange shall separately determine the 
assessment criteria, announcement methods and other matters necessary for the assessment 
of liquidity providing members. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

[December 4, 2007] 

§12-10. Methods of Submission of Market Making Quotations, etc. 

(1)  “Quotations  for  market  making  in  accordance  with  the  manner  stipulated  in  the 
Enforcement Rules” in the main sentence of [§12-7(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to the 
quotations  submitted  through  market  making  accounts  in  the  manner  of  meeting  all  the 
requirements of each of the following subparagraphs: 

1. The quotation shall be a limit quotation or a best limit quotation; 

2.  The  quotation  shall  be  submitted  during  the  quotation  receiving  hours  in  a  regular 
session; and 

3. In the case of a bid quotation, the quotation shall be submitted at a price lower than 
the price of the best offer quotation at the time of submission and in the case of an offer 
quotation, the quotation shall be submitted at a price higher than the price of the best bid 
quotation at the time of submission. Provided that, this provision shall not apply to the 
case where there is no residual quantity of quotations on the other side of the quotation 
to be submitted. 

(2) In cases where the quotations under paragraph (1) are submitted at a call auction under 
[§18] of the Regulation, “the best offer quotation” and “the best bid quotation” in paragraph 
(1)3  shall  be  construed  as  “the  expected  best  offer  quotation”  and  “the  expected  best  bid 
quotation”,  respectively,  which  are  publicly  announced  pursuant  to  [§52(1)1].  (Amended 
on December 7, 2018) 

(3)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1)3,  in  cases  where  a  market  maker  submits  an  offer 
quotation at a price lower than the price of the best bid quotation at the time of submission 

39 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
or a bid quotation at a price higher than the price of the best offer quotation at the time of 
submission, only the quotation that falls under any of the followings shall be deemed as a 
market making quotation: (Amended on November 28, 2019) 

1. The quotation that has not been executed after having been submitted; and 

2. An offer quotation of a stock which is  subject  to  the market  making agreement and 
meets all the requirements of each of the following items. In such cases, the quantity of 
quotations  of  a  market  maker  that  are  executed  in  excess  of  70/100  of  the  market 
maker’s  balance  held  {referring  to  the  daily  balance  held  specified  in  [§12-17(4)];  the 
same hereinafter in [§12-16]} on the previous day shall be excluded. 

(a) Single stock futures or single stock options of which underlying assets include the 
relevant stock shall not be listed on the market; and 

(b)  The  executed  price  of  the  quotation  shall  decrease  by  more  than  4/100  in 
comparison with the base price of the day. 

(4)  In  cases  where  a  market  maker  intends  to  open,  change  or  close  a  market  making 
account, he/she shall report the matters related to the account to the Exchange by no later 
than two (2) trading days prior to the date of opening, changing  or closing the account in 
accordance with [Annex: Form No. 6-3]. 

(5) “Issues specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to the main sentence of [§12-
7(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to the issues specified in [Annex 5]. 

(6) When submitting liquidity providing quotations as prescribed in paragraphs (1) through 
(3), a market maker shall not entrust it to another member. [May 7, 2021] 

[March 25, 2016] 

§12-11. Qualification of Market Maker 

(1)  “Other  requirements  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§12-7(2)3]  of  the 
Regulation  shall  refer  to  each  of  the  followings:  (Amended  on  March  12,  2021;  July  13, 
2022) 

1. In the case of falling under any of followings, one (1) year or more shall have passed 
since then: 

(a) Where the qualification of market maker has been suspended pursuant to [§12-19]; 
and   

40 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(b) Where a member has a record of having been subject to a criminal sanction, or any 
measures equivalent to or heavier than penalty surcharge, business suspension, trading 
suspension or member fine (limited to a fine amounting to KRW 10 million or more), 
on account of a violation of the relevant laws on securities businesses and the business 
regulations  of  the  Exchange  in  the  course  of  performing  the  tasks  of  market  making 
related  to  stocks  (referring  to  market  making  tasks  for  stocks  in  the  KOSPI  and 
KOSDAQ markets and equity derivatives in the derivatives market). 

2.  The  person  in  charge  of  market  making  tasks  shall  have  no  record  of  having  been 
subject  to  a  criminal  sanction  or  any  measures  equivalent  to  or  heavier  than  penalty 
surcharge  or  suspension  within  the  latest  one  (1)  year  on  account  of  violation  of  the 
relevant laws on securities businesses and the business regulations of the Exchange. 

3.  Two  (2)  or  more  persons  in  charge  of  market  making  tasks  shall  be  appointed  to 
perform market making tasks. 

4.  An internal control device shall be available to allow the quotations for covered short 
sales  under  [§9-2(2)]  of  the  Regulation  only  if  the  relevant  listed  securities  are 
borrowed. 

(2)  In  cases  where  a  market  maker  designates  or  changes  the  person  in  charge  of  market 
making tasks, he/she shall report such fact to the Exchange in advance in accordance with 
[Annex: Form No. 6-4]. 

[March 25, 2016] 

§12-12. Selection of Market Making Target Issues 

(1)  Pursuant  to  [§12-7(3)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  Exchange  may  assess  the  liquidity  of 
eligible  issues  based  on  the  criteria  specified  in  [Annex  5],  select  and  publish  the  low-
liquidity issues subject to market-making agreements (hereinafter referred to as the “market 
making target issues”). 

(2) The timing for selection and the effective period of market making target issues shall be 
determined in accordance with the manner stipulated in [Annex 5]. 

[March 25, 2016] 

§12-13. Selection of Market Makers and Allocation of Market Making Target Issues 

(1) Each member may apply to be selected as a market maker after the Exchange officially 
announces the list of market making target issues pursuant to [§12-7(3)] of the Regulation. 

41 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) The Exchange may determine the number of market makers by taking into account the 
number of  members applied pursuant  to  paragraph (1) and  the number of  market  making 
target issues. 

(3) The Exchange shall assess eligibility of the applicants noted in paragraph (1) based on 
the  criteria  specified  in  [Annex  5-2]  to  select  market  makers  and  the  selected  market 
makers may choose market making target issues by the order of priority. 

(4)  The  Exchange  shall  allocate  market  making  target  issues  in  accordance  with  the 
selections  made  by  the  market  makers  pursuant  to  paragraph  (3).  Provided  that,  in  cases 
where  it  is  deemed  necessary,  the  Exchange  may  change  the  allocation  method  in 
consultation with market makers. 

[March 25, 2016] 

§12-14. Conclusion or Termination, etc. of Market Making Agreements 

(1) A person who was selected by the Exchange as a market maker pursuant to [§12-13(3)] 
shall  enter  into  a  market  making  agreement  in  advance  with  the  Exchange  in  accordance 
with  [Annex:  Form  No.  6-5]  in  order  to  submit  the  market  making  quotations  for  the 
market  making  target  issues  that  have  been  allocated  pursuant  to  [§12-13(4)]  (hereinafter 
referred to as the “market making issues”). 

(2) The Exchange may terminate a market making agreement as determined in the market 
making agreement entered into with a market maker. 

(3) [Deleted on September 19, 2017] 

(4)  In  cases  where  the  market  making  for  a  market  making  is  terminated  according  to  a 
market making agreement, the market maker cannot submit quotations of the relevant issue 
through  the  market  making  account  after  the  date  of  termination.  Provided  that,  where  a 
market making agreement has newly been entered into for the same issue before the market 
making agreement expires, this provision shall not apply thereto. (Amended on November 
28, 2019) 

(5)  The  Exchange  may  newly  enter  into  a  market  making  agreement  with  other  market 
makers  for  an  issue  of  which  market  making  agreement  has  been  terminated  pursuant  to 
paragraph  (2)  or  for  an  issue  which  has  not  been  allocated  as  a  market  making  issue 
pursuant  to  [§12-1(4)],  as  stipulated  by  the  Exchange  separately.  Provided  that,  this 
provision shall not apply to the case where the remaining period from the effective date of 
the termination of the market making agreement to the expiry date of the previous market 
making agreement is shorter than two (2) months. (Amended on February 28, 2017) 

42 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(6)  The  Exchange  may  terminate  the  market  making  agreement  for  the  relevant  issue  in 
cases where any of the followings occurs: [March 12, 2021] 

1.  Case  where  the  average  daily  turnover  ratio  (excluding  the  last  seven  (7)  trading       
days of each quarter) is assessed every quarter pursuant to [Annex 5-3] and it exceeds 
15% for two (2) consecutive quarters. In such cases, the market making for the relevant 
issue shall terminate at the end of the concerned quarter; 

2.  Case where the relevant issue is delisted; 

3.  Case where the liquidity provision agreement pursuant to [§12-3] of the Regulation 
was concluded and is in force; and 

4.  Other cases that the Exchange deems necessary for market management. 

[March 25, 2016] 

§12-15. Obligation to maintain Market Making Quotations 

(1) Pursuant to [§12-8] of the Regulation, a market maker shall maintain the market making 
quotations  in  the  manner  of  satisfying  all  the  requirements  specified  in  each  of  the 
following subparagraphs. In such cases, the quotations that have been submitted during the 
hours  for  the  trading  by  the  method  of  continuous  call  auction  stipulated  in  [§19]  of  the 
Regulation  shall  be  deemed  as  having  been  submitted  to  perform  the  obligation  of 
maintaining market making quotations, notwithstanding [§12-10(2)]. 

1. Quotations shall be maintained on both of offer and bid sides; 

2.  The  figure,  which  is  obtained  from  dividing  the  difference  between  the  price  of  an 
offer quotation and the price of a bid quotation of a market maker by the quotation price 
unit  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “quotation  price  unit  spread”),  shall  be  within  the 
obligatory spread that is determined in the market making agreement. Provided that, in 
cases where the obligation to maintain market making quotations on either side of bid or 
offer is exempted and the quotation situation falls under any of the following items, the 
figure specified in the relevant item shall be deemed as the quotation price unit spread: 

(a) Where there is a quotation on one side: The figure that is obtained from dividing 
the difference between the price of the best quotation on one side and the price of the 
market making quotation on the other side by the quotation price unit; and 

(b) Where there is no quotation on one side: The figure that is obtained from dividing 
the difference between the price of the best quotation on the other side and the price 

43 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
of the market making quotation on the other side by the quotation price unit. 

3. The sum of the amount of offer market making quotations and the sum of the amount 
of  bid  market  making  quotations  shall  be  at  least  the  minimum  amount  for  quotation 
maintenance specified in the market making agreement, respectively. 

(2)  “Cases  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§12-8(1)]  of  the 
Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  cases  falling  under  each  of  the  following  subparagraphs: 
(Amended on November 28, 2019) 

1. Where it is within three (3) minutes after the market opening; 

2. Where it is the quotation receiving hours when the prices are determined by the call 
auction under [§18] of the Regulation; 

3. Where there are only the bid quotations at the upper price limit or the offer quotations 
at the lower price limit for the relevant market making issue; 

4.  When  the  value  of  the  relevant  market  making  issue  traded  by  the  market  making 
quotations during a day exceeds 50/100 of the average daily trading value {limited to the 
value of traded concluded during the trading hours of regular sessions by the methods of 
individual  auction  under  [§18(1)3  through  5]  of  the  Regulation  and  [§19]  of  the 
Regulation}  during  the  assessment  period  specified  in  [Annex  5],  case  where  it  is  the 
period from such time to the time of market closing of the day; 

5.  Where  the  relevant  market  making  issue  was  designated  as  an  investment  caution 
issue  pursuant  to  [§5-2] of  the  Market  Oversight  Regulation,  or  as  an  investment  alert 
issue or an investment risk issue; (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

6. Where the relevant market making issue was designated as an administrative issue or 
an investment precaution issue; 

7.  Where  it  is  from  the  time  when  a  cause  for  delisting  has  occurred  to  the  relevant 
market making issue to the time when the cause was resolved; and 

8.  Other  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  is  difficult  to  submit  the  market  making 
quotations due to the system failure, etc. 

[March 25, 2016] 

(3)  Notwithstanding  the  provisions  of  paragraph  (1),  in  the  case  of  sudden  changes  in 
market condition etc., where the Exchange deems necessary, the obligatory spread may be 
increased  pursuant  to  subparagraph  2  of  the  same  paragraph  or  the  minimum  amount  for 
quotation maintenance may be decreased pursuant to subparagraph 3 of the same paragraph. 

44 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[March 25, 2020] 

§12-16. Exceptions in Obligation to maintain Both-sided Market Making Quotations 

Pursuant to [§12-8(2)] of the Regulation, in cases when a market maker falls under each of 
the following  subparagraphs, the market  maker  may not  be obligated to  maintain either  a 
bid  or  offer  quotation  in  accordance  with  the  provisions  of  the  relevant  subparagraph: 
(Amended on November 28, 2019) 

1. In the case of a bid quotation that falls under any of the following items: 

(a)  Where  the  balance  held  (excluding  the  quantity  held  by  borrowing)  for  the 
relevant  market  making  issue  exceeds  2/1000  of  the  number  of  listed  stocks  or  the 
amount  of balance  held  (referring  to  the amount calculated by multiplying the most 
recent  price by  the balance held  excluding the quantity  held  by borrowing)  exceeds 
KRW 100 million; 

(b)  Where  the  quantity,  which  is  calculated  by  subtracting  the  balance  held  of  a 
market maker from the number of listed stocks of the relevant market making issue, 
falls short of the minimum quotation quantity (referring to the quantity that is needed 
to  meet  the  minimum  quantity  for  quotation  maintenance  specified  in  the  market 
making agreement pursuant to the criteria of [Annex 5-3]; the same hereinafter in this 
Article); and 

(c)  Where the  price difference between the best  offer quotation  and the lower price 
limit  of  the  day  is  within  the  scope  of  obligatory  spread  specified  in  the  market 
making agreement. 

2. In the case of an offer quotation that falls under any of the following items: 

(a) [Deleted on November 28, 2019] 

(b) Where the balance held of a market maker for the relevant market making issue 
falls short of the minimum quotation quantity; and 

(c)  Where  the  price  difference  between  the  best  bid  quotation  and  the  upper  price 
limit  of  the  day  is  within  the  scope  of  obligatory  spread  specified  in  the  market 
making agreement. 

[March 25, 2016] 

45 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§12-17. Management of Balance of Market Making Account 

(1) Pursuant to [§12-8(2)] of the Regulation, a market maker shall report to the Exchange 
the number of stocks of each market making issue held in the market making account as of 
the  day  before  the  starting  date  for  market  making  specified  in  the  market  making 
agreement, on the starting date for market making in accordance with [Annex: Form No. 6-
6]. Provided that, this provision shall not apply to the issue for which the market making 
agreement has been entered into for the first time. 

(2)  Market  makers  shall  report  the  changes  in  quantity  and  the  balance  held  in  market 
making accounts for each market making issue to the Exchange in accordance with [Annex: 
Form  6-6]  from  the  date  of  commencement  of  the  market  making  by  the  time  of  market
