opening on the following trading day. (Amended on November 28, 2019) 

(3) In cases where it needs to make corrections to the contents of the report made pursuant 
to  paragraph  (2),  market  makers  shall  report  the  corrections  by  12:00  noon  on  the  day 
which includes the reporting deadline. (Amended on November 28, 2019) 

(4) The Exchange shall manage the quantities reported by market makers for each market 
making issue pursuant to the provisions of paragraphs (1) through (3) as the daily balance 
held of the relevant market making issue. [November 28, 2019] 

[March 25, 2016] 

§12-18. Assessment, etc. of Market Makers 

(1)  Pursuant  to  [§12-9(2)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  Exchange  may  make  assessment 
(hereinafter referred to as the “assessment of market making performance”) of each market 
maker on a quarterly basis for each market making issue in accordance with the assessment 
criteria under [Annex 5-3] on the extent to which the obligation to maintain market making 
quotations was fulfilled and the activeness in market making activities, etc. Provided that, 
this provision shall not apply to the market making issues of which the number of days for 
obligatory market making is fewer than five (5) during the relevant quarter. 

(2)  The  Exchange  may  notify  the  market  maker  concerned  of  the  result  of  assessment  of 
his/her market making performance. 

(3)  The  Exchange  may  request  a  market  maker  to  submit  materials  that  are  deemed 
necessary  for  the  assessment  of  market  making  performance.  In  such  cases,  the  market 
maker shall comply with the request without delay. 

(4)  Notwithstanding  the  provisions  of  paragraph  (1),  in  the  case  of  each  of  the  following 
subparagraphs, the assessment of the market making performance may not be carried out. 

46 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[December 6, 2018] (Amended on December 21, 2022) 

1.  Where  it  is  necessary  to  be  excluded  from  the  assessment  of  the  market  making 
performance  for  a  certain  period  in  order  to  secure  a  preliminary  test  period  for 
participating  as  a  market  maker,  and  such  period  is  specified  in  the  market  making 
agreement; and 

2.  Where  a  market  maker  who  has  failed  to  submit  market  making  quotations  for  any 
reasons  that  are  not  attributable  to  the  market  maker’s  intent  or  negligence,  such  as 
compliance  with  related  statutes  and  internal  control  procedures,  computer  problems, 
market  fluctuation,  etc.  requests  the  Exchange  to  exclude  it  from  the  assessment  of 
market making performance by specifying the reason and the exclusion period, and the 
Exchange recognizes it necessary.   

[March 25, 2016] 

§12-19. Suspension of Market Maker’s Qualification 

(1) Pursuant to [§12-9(2)] of the Regulation, in cases where a market maker falls under the 
criteria  for  suspension  of  qualifications  stipulated  in  [Annex  5-3]  as  a  result  of  the 
assessment of market making performance, the Exchange may suspend the qualification of 
the relevant market maker. 

(2) The Exchange shall not designate the person whose qualification as a market maker has 
been suspended pursuant to paragraph (1) as a market maker for one (1) year period from 
the month following the month to which the suspension date belongs. 

[March 25, 2016] 

§12-20. Payments to Market Makers 

(1) Pursuant to §12-9(2)] of the Regulation, the Exchange may make payments to market 
makers (hereinafter referred to as the “payment for market making”) in accordance with the 
stipulation  in  [Annex  5-3]  differentially  reflecting  the  result  of  assessment  of  market 
making performance, within the scope of total revenue from fees (referring to the trading 
fees  and  clearing  fees)  of  the  market  making  issues  for  which  the  market  makers  have 
fulfilled  their  market  making  obligations  during  the  term  of  market  making  agreement. 
Provided that the criteria on the payments for market making may be set differently when 
the Exchange deems it necessary. (Amended on September 19, 2017) 

(2) The Exchange shall make the payments for market making in accordance with the time 
for  making  the  payments  specified  in  [Annex  5-3]  after  the  end  of  the  quarter  when  the 

47 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
assessment  of  market  making  performance  was  conducted.  (Amended  on  February  28, 
2017) 

[March 25, 2016] 

§13. [Deleted on December 21, 2022]   

§14. Prior Notice on Suspension of Validity of Program Trading Quotations, etc.   

(1)  The  Exchange  may,  when  the  price  of  a  contract  of  which  the  trading  volume  is  the 
largest  under  [§13(1)]  of  the  Regulation  (hereinafter  in  this  article  referred  to  as  “base 
contract”) rises (or falls) by 6/100 or more from the base price, and KOSDAQ 150 rises (or 
falls)  by  3/100  or  more  from  the  closing  value  of  the  previous  day,  issue  a  prior  notice 
about  the  fact  that  the  validity  of  bid  (or  offer)  quotations  for  program  trading  may  be 
suspended. (Amended on February 3, 2009; July 1, 2009; December 7, 2018) 

(2) In the case of falling under the case noted in any of the following subparagraphs after 
issuing the prior notice on the suspension of program quotation validity, the Exchange may 
withdraw  the  relevant  prior  notice  on  the  suspension  of  program  quotation  validity: 
(Amended on July 1, 2009; December 7, 2018) 

1.  Where  the  base  price  of  base  contract  has  recovered  to  within  ±  6/100  of  the  base 
price; 

2.  Where  KOSDAQ  150  has  recovered  to  within  ±  3/100  of  the  closing  value  of  the 
previous day; and   

3.  Where  the  trading  of  the  base  contract  is  halted  pursuant  to  the  Derivatives  Market 
Business Regulation. 

(3) In cases where the temporary failure of KOSDAQ system has occurred, the Exchange 
may suspend the validity of program trading quotation without issuing a prior notice on the 
suspension  of validity of  program  trading  quotation pursuant  to  paragraph (1). (Amended 
on February 3, 2009) 

§15. [Deleted on July 11, 2019] 

§16. [Deleted on December 28, 2011] 

48 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§17. Base Price 

(1) The base price noted in [§14(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to each of the following 
subparagraphs: (Amended on April 20, 2012; March 25, 2013; June 16, 2014; February 14, 
2022) 

1. For the issues other than those noted in subparagraphs 2 through 10, the closing price 
of  immediately  preceding  trading  day.  Provided  that,  if  the  price  does  not  match  the 
quotation price unit, it shall  be the price closest  to  that price among  the  prices that are 
higher than that price and match the quotation price unit, and if there is no closing price 
on the immediately preceding trading day, it shall be the base price of the immediately 
preceding trading day. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

2. For the initially listed issues, it shall be the price noted in each of following items: 

(a)  Case  of  stocks  and  DRs  of  foreign  stocks  [excluding  the  issues  noted  in 
subparagraph 2(e)]; 

Price calculated in accordance with [Annex 1-4]   

(b) [Deleted on March 25, 2013] 

(c) [Deleted on March 25, 2013] 

(d) [Deleted on March 25, 2013] 

(e) Case of issue transferred from the KOSPI Market; 

The closing price (if no closing price is available, it shall be the base price: the same 
hereinafter in this Paragraph) of last trading day in the KOSPI Market.   

      (f)  Case  of  collective  investment  securities  of  business  development  collective 

investment vehicle; 

The base price calculated in accordance with Article 238, Paragraph 6 of the Act (it 
shall be the mostly recently announced base price based on the listing date; in the 
case of an announcement on the day prior to the listing date, it shall be limited to 
that announce by 17:00) [March 16, 2026] 

3. For the issues using the first trading price as the base price, the price determined for 
the  first  time  pursuant  to  [§22]  of  the  Regulation.  In  this  case,  if  the  first  price  of  the 
issue  using  the  first  trading  price  as  the  base  price  is  not  determined  by  the  time  of 
market  closing,  the  lowest  offer  price  if  the  offer  prices  which  are  lower  than  the 
appraisal price (in case of no appraisal price, the lowest quotation price shall be regarded 

49 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
as  the  appraisal  price;  the  same  hereinafter  and  [§20(4)])  determined  according  to 
[Annex 1] are available, the highest bid price if the bid prices which are higher than the 
appraisal price are available, and the appraisal price in any other cases shall be the base 
price of the next trading day, respectively. 

3-2. In the case of listed issues after merger, the base price shall be as follows: 

(a)  In  the  case  where  the  special  purpose  acquisition  company  survives  the  merger 
pursuant to [§2(1)1(f)(i)], the base price shall be the stock price under subparagraph 1 
of the surviving special purpose acquisition company; and 

(b)  In  the  case  where  the  special  purpose  acquisition  company  does  not  survive  the   
merger pursuant to [§2(1)1(f)(ii)], the base price shall be the price obtained by dividing 
the stock price under subparagraph 1 of the non-surviving special purpose acquisition 
company by the merger ratio (the number of new shares issued per share of the non-
surviving  special  purpose  acquisition  company)  of  the  corporation  that  is  the 
counterpart to the merger in the report on completion of merger, etc. or the report on 
the issuance of securities submitted in connection with the merger. 

4. [Deleted on April 12, 2013]   

5. [Deleted on April 12, 2013]   

6.  Of  the  issues  having  gone  ex-dividend  or  ex-right,  those  issues  falling  under  any  of 
following items, it shall be the price determined using the formula noted in Annex 2, and 
if the formula noted in Annex 2 cannot be applied, among the formula noted in Annex 2, 
the  formula  applicable  to  the  issue  with  the  most  similar  specification  as  the  relevant 
issue shall apply mutatis mutandis thereto:   

(a)  The  issue  having  gone  ex-dividend  as  a  result  of  an  advance  notice  on  the  stock 
dividend for the relevant fiscal year;   

(b)  The  issue  having  gone  ex-dividend  following  the  capital  increase  without 
consideration; and 

(c)  As  an  issue  having  gone  ex-dividend  following  the  paid-in  capital  increase,  the 
issue whose closing price on the trading day before the  ex-dividend day exceeds the 
issue price of new stocks.   

7. [Deleted on March 25, 2013] 

8. [Deleted on March 25, 2013] 

9.  In  the  case  of  issue  to  undergo  the  stock  split  or  reverse  stock  split,  the  price 

50 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
determined by multiplying the closing price on the day immediately before by the split 
ratio or merger ratio.   

10. [Deleted on April 12, 2013]   

(2) [Deleted on March 25, 2013]   

(3) [Deleted on April 12, 2013]   

(4) In cases where the price (the amount less than KRW 1 shall be rounded down) pursuant 
to paragraphs (1)2(e and f), (1)3-2(b), (1)6 and (1)9 does not match the quotation price unit, 
it shall be the price closest to that price among the prices that are higher than that price and 
match the quotation price unit. (Amended on March 25, 2013; February 14, 2022; February 
27, 2025; March 16, 2026) 

(5)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1),  in  the  case  that  falls  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs, the base price may be determined differently.  In such cases, the Exchange 
shall make public such fact, calculation method of base price, etc. without delay. (Amended 
on March 25, 2013; June 16, 2014) 

1. Case of resuming the trade after closing of the market for a lengthy period; and 

2. [Deleted on June16, 2014] 

3. Where it is judged that application of base price pursuant to paragraph (1) is clearly 
problematic because of such reasons as no trading for a lengthy period, material change 
in right details or sudden change in market condition.   

(Wholly amended on December 30, 2010) 

§17-2. Price Limits   

(1) Among the amounts determined pursuant to [§14(2)] of the Regulation, the amount less 
than the quotation price unit corresponding to the base price range shall be rounded down, 
but  in  cases  where  the  relevant  amount  is  less  than  the  lowest  amount  of  quotation  price 
units,  it  shall  be  the  lowest  quotation  price  unit,  and  if  the  amount  determined  by  taking 
into  account  the  price  limit  of  base  price  cannot  apply  the  quotation  price  units  noted  in 
[§18], it shall be rounded up to the price to which the quotation price unit can be applied.   

(2) Pursuant to [§14(3)] of the Regulation, the case where the price limit range of quotation 
may  be  determined  differently  shall  be  the  case  falling  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs. In this case, the Exchange shall make public the fact without delay: (April 
12, 2023) 

51 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. Case of resuming the trade after closing of market for a lengthy period; 

2. Case where the market condition changes suddenly; and   

3. In addition, case where the Exchange deems it necessary for the market management. 

(3)  Pursuant  to  [§14(3)]  of  the  Regulation,  in  the  case  of  initially  listed  issues 
corresponding  to  stocks  and  DRs  of  foreign  stocks  falling  under  [§17(1)2a],  the  highest 
limit price and the lowest limit price on the date of new listing shall be in accordance with 
each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on April 12, 2023) 

1.  In  the  case  of  the  highest  limit  price;  The  price  obtained  by  adding  the  amount 
(amount  less  than  the  quotation  price  unit  of  the  base  price  from  the  relevant  amount 
shall be rounded down; the same hereinafter in this paragraph) produced by multiplying 
the base price by 3 to the base price; and 

2.  In  the  case  of  the  lowest  limit  price:  The  price  obtained  by  subtracting  the  amount 
produced by multiplying the base price by 0.4 from the base price. 

[December 30, 2010] 

§18. Quotation Units   

(1)  Quotation  quantity  unit  and  trading  quantity  unit  of  issues  shall  be  one  (1)  share  for 
stock  certificates,  one  (1)  DR  for  DRs  of  foreign  stocks,  one  (1)  warrantfor  subscription 
warrants  and  one  (1)  certificate  for  subscription  right  certificate,  one  (1)  share  for 
investment  company  of  business  development  collective  investment  vehicle,  and  one  (1) 
unit  for  investment  trust  beneficiary  certificates  of  business  development  collective 
investment vehicle. (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 29, 2009; March 25, 2013; 
March 16, 2026) 

(2) Quotation price unit pursuant to [§15] of the Regulation shall be those noted in each of 
the following subparagraphs: (Amended on August 16, 2007; February 3, 2009; December 
29, 2009; July 29, 2010; December 21, 2022) 

1. Issue with the price per share (including price per warrant, price per certificate, and 
price  per  unit;  the  same  hereinafter  in  this  Article)  is  less  than  KRW  2,000:  KRW  1 
(Amended on Marcy 16, 2026) 

1-2. Issue with the price per share is equal to or higher than KRW 2,000, but less than 
KRW 5,000: KRW 5   

52 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2.  Issue  with  the  price  per  share  is  equal  to  or  higher  than  KRW  5,000,  but  less  than 
KRW 20,000: KRW 10 

3. Issue with the price per share is equal to or higher than KRW 20,000, but less than 
KRW 50,000: KRW 50 

4. Issue with the price per share is equal to or higher than KRW 50,000, but less than 
KRW 200,000: KRW 100   

5. Issue with the price per share is equal to or higher than KRW 50,000, but less than 
KRW 200,000: KRW 100   

6. Issue with the price per share is equal to or higher than KRW 200,000, but less than 
KRW 500,000: KRW 500   

7. Issue with the price per share is equal to or higher than KRW 500,000: KRW 1,000.   

(3) [Deleted on March 25, 2013] 

§18-2. Validity of Quotations, etc.   

(1)  The  quotations  shall  be  valid  from  the  time  of  quotation  receipt  to  the  time  of  trade 
execution  per  trade  type  during  the  regular  session  and  off-hours  session,  within  the 
quotation receiving hours of the day pursuant to [§6] for each trading session (referring to 
the regular session, pre-hours session and after-hours session). Provided that, the validity of 
quotation  shall  not  be  acknowledged  if  the  quotation  falls  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs:   

1.  The  quotations  inputted  during  the  time  when  the  trading  has  been  halted  or 
suspended  pursuant  to  [§6(1)],  [§25(1)],  [§25-2]  and  [§26(1)]  of  the  Regulation 
(including the cases of the trading halt or suspension pursuant to the Listing Regulation 
and  the  Disclosure  Regulation).  Provided  that  the  cancellation  quotations  (including 
quotations that the mass order cancellation under [§18-4] is applied) inputted during the 
relevant period of the trading halt or suspension are recognized as effective;   

2. [Deleted on July 29, 2010]   

3. [Deleted on July 29, 2010] 

4. Among the quotations participated in the determination of the opening price of the 
first  trading  day  for  the  issue  using  the  first  trading  price  as  the  base  price,  the 

53 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
quotations  with  prices  that  exceed  the  upper  price  limit  or  are  below  the  lower  price 
limit after the determination of the opening price;   

4-2. Mid-price quotations received before the quotation receiving hours for call auction 
to determine the price at the time of market closing noted in [§18(1)2] of the Regulation, 
but  for which no transaction has  been concluded by  the quotation reception time;  and 
[February 27, 2025] 

5.  Other  quotations  that  the  Exchange  deems  unreasonable  to  accept  the  validity  of 
quotation.   

(2) The cancellation or correction of quotation pursuant to [§9(1)] of the Regulation shall 
be allowed only in the case of the unexecuted quotations among those received and shall be 
processed in the sequence of the receipt time of correction or cancellation quotations.   

(3) Pursuant to paragraph (2), a member may cancel or correct the quotations using any of 
the following methods: (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

1. Canceling the entire or a part of quantity quoted. Provided that, the entire or a part of 
quantity  of  quotation  for  auction-based  block  trade  shall  be  cancelled  only  in  cases 
where  the  quantity  after  cancellation  satisfies  the  quantity  requirements  specified  in 
[§22-3(3)] or [§24-2(3)];   

2. Correction of prices of entire or a part of quantity quoted into another price, if a limit 
quotation,  limit-to-market-on-close  quotation,  immediately  executable  limit  quotation 
and best limit quotation is corrected into the same type of quotation; and   

3. Correction of entire or a part of quantity quoted into another type of quotation, if a 
limit  quotation,  limit-to-market-on-close  quotation,  immediately  executable  limit 
quotation, best limit quotation and market quotation is corrected into a different type of 
quotation (excluding mid-price quotation and stop-limit quotation; the same hereinafter 
in this subparagraph). In such cases, if a limit quotation, immediately executable limit 
quotation  and  best  limit  quotation  are  corrected  into  one  another,  the  price  shall  be 
corrected into other price. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

4.  In  cases  of  correcting  a  stop-limit  quotation  to  a  quotation  of  the  same  type,  all  or 
part  of  the  quantity  of  the  quotation  shall  be  corrected  using  any  one  method  of  the 
following items: [February 27, 2025] 

        (a) If a stop-limit quotation is corrected before it triggers into a limit quotation, either 
the  price  of  quotation  before  the  correction  shall  be  different  from  the  price  of  the 
quotation after the correction, or the stop price before the correction shall be different 
from the stop price after the correction; or [February 27, 2025] 

54 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
     
 
 
        (b) If a stop-limit quotation is corrected after it triggers into a limit quotation, the price 

of the quotation shall be different. [February 27, 2025] 

(4) In the case of quotations affixed with the conditions under each item of subparagraph 17 
of [§40], among the quantities of such quotations, the quantity that has not been executed 
shall be construed as cancelled. 

(5)  A  quotation  falling  under  any  of  the  following  subparagraphs  shall  be  suspended  its 
validity  until  the  resumption  time  specified  in  the  relevant  subparagraph:  (Amended  on 
February 27, 2025)     

    1. In case of suspension of trading during the quotation receiving hours for call auction 
or  suspension  of  quotation  reception  in  accordance  with  [§25-2]  of  the  Regulation, 
quotations received before the relevant measures: When trading is resumed [February 27, 
2025] 

    2.  Mid-price  quotation  in  cases  where  there  is  no  quantity  of  quotation  other  than  the 
mid-price quotation on either the sell side or the buy side during the time of trading by 
means of continuous auction: When there is a quantity of quotation other than the mid-
price quotation on both the sell and buy sides; and [February 27, 2025] 

    3.  Mid-price  quotation  in  cases  where  no  transaction  is  made  during  the  quotation 
receiving hours for call auction: When the method of executing transactions is changed 
to continuous auction and there are quotations other than mid-price quotation on both the 
sell and buy sides. [February 27, 2025] 

[December 21, 2022] 

§18-3. Validity of Quotations with Self-match Prevention Condition 

(1)  In  the  case  where,  among  the  quotation  of  high-speed  algorithmic  traders,  the  high-
speed algorithmic trading numbers of quotations are the same and it is possible to execute 
transactions between such quotations affixed with the following conditions, the quantity of 
the relevant quotation shall be deemed to be cancelled according to each of the following 
subparagraphs based on the condition imposed on the quotation received later: 

    1. A condition to cancel all of the balance of previously received quotation;   

    2. A condition to cancel the entire quantity of quotation received later; and   

    3.  A  condition  to  cancel  each  quantity  that  can  be  executed  between  buy  and  sell 

quotations. 

55 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2)  Paragraph  (1)  shall  apply  only  to  the  case  of  continuous  trading  under  [§19]  of  the 
Regulation  during  the  regular  trading  session.  Provided  that  this  shall  not  apply  if  the 
relevant quotation is subject to the trading priority for simultaneous quotations pursuant to 
[§19(3)1]. 

(3)  In  the  case  of  quotations  to  which  both  the  self-match  prevention  conditions  under 
paragraph  (1)  and  the  condition  under  subparagraph  17(a)  of  [§40]  are  simultaneously 
affixed, the self-match prevention condition shall take precedence.   

[December 21, 2022] 

§18-4. Mass Order Cancellation   

(1)  Members  may  apply  to  the  Exchange  to  cancel  all  quotations  received  before 
application at once (hereinafter referred to as the “mass order cancellation”) by designating 
conditions  for  each  high-speed  algorithmic  trading  number  only  if  all  of  the  following 
subparagraphs are met. In such case, matters necessary for the application of the mass order 
cancellation, such as classification of securities, conditions for cancellation, etc. shall be as 
specified in the Annex 1-3: 

1.  Cases for managing risks; and 

2.  Cases  for  submitting  quotations  through  high-speed  algorithmic  trading  account 

reported pursuant to [§50-3(3)] of the Regulation. 

(2)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1),  the  Exchange  may  not  process  the  mass  order 
cancellation  in  case  of  a  system  failure  or  other  cases  when  it  is  deemed  necessary  for 
market management.   

(3) Members shall record and maintain data related to the mass order cancellation for ten 
(10) years and submit the data when the Exchange request for the relevant data for market 
management, etc. 

[December 21, 2022] 

§18-5. Methods to Apply for Cancellation of Disconnected Quotations, etc. 

(1)  The  “case  where  it  is  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§16-2(1)]  of  the 
Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  case  where,  as  a  case  in  which  the  connection  between  the 
member system and the Exchange system is disconnected during the regular trading session 
and  electronic  transmission  and  reception  does  not  occur,  there  is  a  determination  in 

56 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
advance between the member applying for the cancellation of disconnected quotations and 
the Exchange. 

(2)  Pursuant  to  [§16-2(1)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  range  of  cancellation  of  disconnected 
quotations shall be the number (excluding the number changed or cancelled through other 
sessions)  of  quotations  not  executed  among  quotations  submitted  through  the  session 
requested in advance pursuant to paragraph (3). 

(3) Pursuant  to  [§16-2(2)] of the Regulation, the methods  to  apply  for the cancellation of 
disconnected quotations and for the termination thereof shall be as specified in [§8(5)] of 
the Guidelines for Connection, etc. of Member System. 

(5)  The  Exchange  may  not  apply  the  cancellation  of  disconnection  quotations  in  case  of 
system failure or other cases where it deems necessary for market management. 

[December 21, 2022] 

§19. Priority of Simultaneous Quotations   

(1) Pursuant to the part other than each subparagraph of [§17(3)] of the Regulation, among 
the simultaneous quotations, the quotations with larger quantities shall have a priority over 
the quotations with smaller quantities (in the case of quotations with the same quantity, the 
quotation  received  earlier  by  the  KOSDAQ  computer  system  has  a  priority)  until  the 
quotation quantity reaches to the quantity under following subparagraph 1. In such case, for 
the  quotations  of  which  quantities  exceed  the  quantity  under  subparagraph  1,  the  priority 
shall be applied in a sequential order from subparagraph 2 in the same manner as stated in 
the former part:. (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 21, 2022) 

1. 100 times trading quantities unit;   

2.  Half  (1/2)  of  the  residual  quantity.  In  such  case,  the  quantity  less  than  trading 
quantity unit shall be rounded to the trading quantity unit; and   

3. The total residual quantity.   

(2) [Deleted on December 21, 2022]   

(3) The priority of simultaneous quotations pursuant to paragraphs (1) shall apply until the 
time  noted  in  each  of  the  following  subparagraphs.  In  such  cases,  in  cases  where,  in 
applying paragraphs (1) and (2) and the proviso to paragraph (3), while the entire quantity 
has not been executed pursuant to paragraph (1) until the time of determining the closing 
price of the market and the market was closed with the upper limit price or lower limit price 

57 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
as the closing price, the simultaneous quotations shall apply until the time when the closing 
price  is  determined.  (Amended  on  June  1,  2007;  February  3,  2009;  March  19,  2009; 
December 21, 2022)   

1.  In  the  case  of  a  bid  quotation  at  the  upper  limit  price  or  an  offer  quotation  at  the 
lower limit price pursuant to [§17(3)] of the Regulation, until the entire quantity thereof 
is executed;   

2. In the case of market quotations pursuant to [§17(3)] of the Regulation, until the time 
such quotation price is regarded as the price other than the upper limit price or the lower 
limit price; and   

3. In the case of the quotation at the highest or lowest price pursuant to [§17(3)] of the 
Regulation, until the opening price pursuant to [§27(2)] is determined. Provided that, if 
the price is determined to be a price falling under the lowest quotation price unit under 
[§18(2)],  until  the  entire  quantity  of  quotations  submitted  at  the  relevant  price  is 
executed.   

(4) At the time of determining the price pursuant to [§18(1)1, 3 & 4] of the Regulation, if 
such price is formed as the upper limit price or lower limit price at the time of determining 
the  closing  price,  the  quotations  at  the  price  noted  in  [§17(3)]  of  the  Regulation  that 
participated  in  the  determination  of  such  price  shall  be  construed  as  the  simultaneous 
quotation. [March 19, 2009] (Amended on March 30, 2009) 

§20. Range of Quotations Participating in Call Auction   

(1)  The  range  of  quotations  participating  in  the  call  auction  pursuant  to  [§18(2)]  of  the 
Regulation  shall  be  the  quotations  received  during  the  hours  specified  in  each  of  the 
following  subparagraphs  and  those  received  during  the  period  specified  by  the  Exchange 
randomly  within  thirty  (30)  seconds  since  then,  and  shall  include  the  quotations  received 
earlier,  but  not  yet  executed,  if  there  are  any:  (Amended  on  June  28,  2005;  February  3, 
2009; June 24, 2014; May 19, 2015; December 21, 2022)   

1.  In  the  case  of  determining  the  price  under  [§18(1)1]  of  the  Regulation,  from  the 
beginning  of  the  quotation  receiving  hours  of  the  regular  session  under  [§6]  to  the 
market opening. Provided that, in the case of being applied with [§23-3(1)2], it shall be 
until the time extended for two (2) minutes after the market opening;   

2. In the case of determining the price under [§18(1)2] of the Regulation, from ten (10) 
minutes before the market closing time to the market closing time, and if the time of the 
market reopening or the trading resumption pursuant to paragraph (1)3 is within the last 
twenty  (20)  minutes  immediately  before  the  market  closing  time,  from  such  point  of 
time to the market closing time. Provided that, in the case of being applied with [§23-

58 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
3(1)], it shall be until the time extended for two (2) minutes after the market closing;   

3. In the case of determining the price under subparagraphs 3 and 4 of [§18(1)] of the 
Regulation, for the first ten (10) minutes from  the time of reopening  of the market  or 
resumption of trading. 

4. In the case of determining the price under [§18(1)5] of the Regulation {excluding the 
case  where  the  relevant  price  falls  under  subparagraphs  1  and  2  of  [§18(1)]},  for  the 
first two (2) minutes from the time of changing the trade execution method. Provided 
that, in cases where the call auction to determine the price at the market closing under 
subparagraph 2 started before two (2) minutes have elapsed from the time of change of 
the  trade  execution  method,  etc.,  it  shall  be  until  ten  (10)  minutes  before  the  market 
closing,  but  the  quotations  received  during  the  time  shall  be  deemed  to  have  been 
participated in the price determination pursuant to [§18(1)2].   

(2) Pursuant to the proviso to [§18(1)] of the Regulation, in the case where the price of each 
subparagraph (excluding subparagraph 2) of the same paragraph is not determined with the 
quotations noted in paragraph (1), the price shall be determined by switching to continuous 
trading specified in [§19] of the Regulation.. (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 21, 
2022) 

(3) [Deleted June 28, 2005]   

(4) “Prices stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to the part other than each 
subparagraph  of  [§18(5)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  the  prices  in  each  of  following 
subparagraphs:  (Amended  on  December  29,  2009;  December  30,  2010;  March  25,  2013; 
April 12, 2023; February 27, 2025) 

1. Where there is a price that is equal to the base price noted in [§17(1)] [referring to the 
appraisal  price  specified  in  Annex  1,  in  the  case  of  determining  the  first  price  on  the 
first  trading  day  for  an  issue  using  the  first  trading  price  as  the  base  price;  the  same 
hereinafter  in  this  Subparagraph],  that  price.  If  there  is  no  such  equivalent  price,  the 
price that is closest to such base price; and   

2. In the case of determining the first price of initially listed subscription warrants and 
subscription right certificates, the price determined by averaging the highest and lowest 
prices. In such cases, if such price does not match the quotation price unit, it shall be the 
price  closest  to  such  price,  among  the  prices  that  are  higher  than  such  price  and  that 
match the quotation price unit. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

§21.  Range  of  Quotations  Restricted  to  Participate  in  Determination  of  Special 
Quotation Price   

59 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Pursuant  to  the  [§18(7)]  of  the  Regulation,  in  cases  where  the  trading  was  halted  or 
suspended during the quotation receiving hours noted in each subparagraph of [§20(1)], and 
the trading was not resumed by the end of the market closing time of the day, the quotations 
received  during  the  day  shall  not  be  included  in  the  determination  of  special  quotation. 
(Amended on February 3, 2009; March 19, 2009) 

§22 [Deleted on May 19, 2015] 

§22-2. Regular Session Block Trade   

(1) The regular session block trade pursuant to [§19-2(1)] of the Regulation shall be applied 
by  inputting  the  details  negotiated  by  the  selling  and  buying  parties,  such  as  the  issue, 
quantity, and price, in accordance with any of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on 
February 3, 2009; December 21, 2022) 

    1.  Method  in  which  details  of  negotiation  are  notified  to  the  member  system  and  the 
KOSDAQ  system  via  the  electronic  network  for  block  trading,  etc.  (referring  to  the 
electronic system operated by the Exchange for the purpose of notifying and confirming 
the  agreement  or  negotiated  details  of  block  trading  and  basket  trading;  the  same 
hereinafter)  and  the  member  places  the  quotations  in  accordance  with  the  negotiated 
details; or   

    2. Method in which the member places the quotations by inputting details of negotiation 

to the KOSDAQ system via the member system or the member securities terminal. 

(2) The details, which have been negotiated between the buying and selling parties pursuant 
to  paragraph  (1),  may  be  changed  only  when  there  has  been  an  agreement  between  the 
trading parties before placing quotations according to such details. (Amended on February 
3, 2009) 

(3) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), when it has been concluded that inputting the negotiated 
details  of  regular  session  block  trade  is  difficult  due  to  the  failure  to  connect  to  the 
electronic  network  for  block  trading,  etc.,  the  member  shall  notify  to  the  Exchange  the 
negotiated details via electronic mail, etc. and place the quotations according to the details 
notified. (Amended on March 19, 2009)   

(4) Notwithstanding paragraphs (1) and (3), when, due to the difficulties in connecting to 
the electronic block trading network, etc., it is not possible to notify the negotiated details 
to the KOSDAQ system, the regular session block trade shall not be executed. (Amended 
on March 19, 2009) 

(5)  The  provisions  of  [§24(2)  &  (3)]  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis  to  the  case  of  regular 

60 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
session block trade. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

[December 23, 2005]   

§22-3. Regular Session Auction-based Block Trade 

(1) The trading volume weighted average price pursuant to the latter part of [§19-3(1)1] of 
the  Regulation  shall  be  calculated  by  dividing  the  total  value  of  trades  (excluding  the 
regular session auction-based block trade and regular session block trade) executed during 
the period in the regular session after the execution of concerned auction-based block trade 
by  the  total  trading  volume  during  the  same  period.  In  such  cases,  if  the  relevant  price 
calculated is higher than the closing price, the amount less than KRW 1 shall be rounded 
down, but if the relevant price calculated is less than the closing price, the amount less than 
KRW 1 shall be rounded up to KRW 1 unit.   

(2) “The price stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” noted in [§19-3(1)2p] of the Regulation 
shall  refer  to  the  base  price  [if  no  base  price  is  available,  it  shall  be  the  appraisal  price 
specified  in  Annex  1  (if  no  appraisal  price  is  available,  it  shall  be  the  lowest  quotation 
price): the same hereinafter in this Article]. (Amended on December 30, 2010) 

(3) The quantity of quotation participating in the regular session auction-based block trade 
pursuant  to  [§19-3(3)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  higher  than  the  quantity,  where  the 
amount obtained by multiplying the relevant quantity by the base price of the day is higher 
than KRW 200 million. (Amended on December 30, 2010)   

(4) The trading unit of regular session auction-based block trade pursuant to [§19-3(3)] of 
the Regulation shall conform to [§18(1)].   

(5)  Pursuant  to  [§19-3(3)],  the  regular  session  auction-based  block  trade  shall  not  be 
utilized when trading the issue designated as administrative issue and issue scheduled to be 
delisted.   

[July 29, 2010] 

§22-4. Regular Session Basket Trade 

(1) The application for regular session basket trade under [§19-4(1)] of the Regulation shall 
be made by notifying the details negotiated by the selling and buying parties, including the 
issue,  quantity  and  price,  to  the  member  system  and  KOSDAQ  system  via  the  electronic 
network  for  block  trading,  etc.  during  regular  session  and  placing  of  the  quotation  by 
members in accordance with the negotiated details. 

61 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) In the case of applying for basket trades pursuant to paragraph (1), one of parties from 
bid quotation and offer quotation shall be submitted by a single member and the case of the 
counter party shall be the quotation of each single member by each issue forming basket. In 
such cases, when the case is trading between foreigners pursuant to provision of Article 6-
7(1)6 of the Regulations on Financial Investment Business, customers of buying and selling 
quotations shall be foreigners. (Amended on July 11, 2019) 

(3) The identical basket number shall be provided regarding the issues forming the identical 
basket,  and  the  number  shall  be  different  from  each  basket  in  the  case  of  on  member 
conducting two (2) or more basket trading quotation during regular session. 

(4)  Pursuant  [§19-4(3)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  number  of  issues  forming  basket  and  the 
number of stocks of a basket issue of shall be as follows: 

1. The number of basket forming issues shall be at least five (5) issues; and 

2. The requirement on the number of stocks of a basket shall be more than the quantity 
equivalent to the sum of the amounts obtained by multiplying the number of stocks by 
the price of each issue forming the basket is at least KRW 200 million. 

(5)  The  trading  unit  under  [§19-4(3)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  in  accordance  with  the 
trading unit under [§18(3)]. 

(6) In making a request for regular session basket trading under paragraph (1), if there are 
no trades executed in the regular session by the individual auction methods under [§18] and 
[§19]  of  the  Regulation  until  the  relevant  quotation  was  received,  the  quotation  shall  be 
made at the base price of the day. [July 11, 2019] 

(7) The provisions of [§22-2(2) through (4)] and [§24(3)] shall apply mutatis mutandis to 
regular session basket trade. 

[June 24, 2014] 

§23. Off-hours Closing Price Trade   

(1) When applying  [§20(1)] of the Regulation, in the case of the pre-hours session for an 
issue whose closing price of the previous day does not match the quotation price unit and 
an  issue  for  which  the  ex-dividend,  ex-right,  ex-distribution,  stock  split  or  reverse  stock 
split takes place on the day of quotation, the previous day’s closing price shall be deemed 
as the base price of the day. (Amended on July 7, 2006; February 3, 2009; April 20, 2012; 
February 27, 2025)   

(2)  The  trading  unit  under  [§20(2)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  in  accordance  with  the 

62 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
trading unit under [§18(1)]. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(3) The priority of quotations for off-hours closing price trade pursuant to [§20(2)] of the 
Regulation shall be in accordance with the time priority where a quotation received earlier 
has priority over a quotation received later. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

§24. Off-Hours Block Trade   

(1)  The  off-hours  block  trade  pursuant  to  [§21(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  applied  by 
notifying  the  negotiated  details,  such  as  the  name  of  issue,  quantity  and  price  agreed 
between the buying and selling parties, in accordance with any of each item of [§22-2(1)] 
during  the  quotation  receiving  hours  for  off-hours  sessions.  In  such  cases,  in  the  case  of 
receiving an entrustment of order from a listed company that intends to purchase or sell its 
treasury stocks by way of off-hours block trading after obtaining the approval of Financial 
Services Commission pursuant to [§10(4)2] of the Regulation, the member shall submit the 
material proving such fact before placing the quotation. (Amended on December 23, 2005; 
February 3, 2009; March 8, 2012; December 21, 2022) 

(2)  In  the  case  of  making  a  request  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1),  either  the  bid  or  the  offer 
shall be placed by a single member, and the amount obtained by multiplying the quotation 
quantity by the share price shall be at least KRW 50 million. In such cases, in the case of 
the transaction between the foreign investors pursuant to Article 6-7(1)6 of the Regulations 
on Financial  Investment Business, both the buying and selling parties shall be the foreign 
investors. (Amended on August 16, 2007; February 3, 2009; June 24, 2014) 

(3)  Notwithstanding  [§18(2)],  the  quotation  price  unit  for  off-hours  block  trade  shall  be 
KRW 1. (Amended on September 8, 2006; August 16, 2007; February 3, 2009; March 25, 
2013)   

(4) [Deleted on December 23, 2005]   

(5)  The  provisions  of  [§22-2(2)  through  (4)]  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis  to  off-hours 
block trade. (Amended on December 23, 2005; February 3, 2009) 

§24-2. Off-hours Auction-based Block Trade 

(1) The provisions of [§22-3(1)] shall apply to the calculation of trading volume weighted 
average price pursuant to the latter part of [§21-2(1)1] of the Regulation.   

(2)  “Price  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§21-2(1)2]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the base price.   

63 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(3) The provisions of [§22-2(3) through (5)] shall apply mutatis mutandis to the case of off-
hours auction-based block trade.   

[July 29, 2010] 

§25. [Deleted on Dec.23, 2005]   

§25-2. Off-hours Periodic Call Trades   

(1)  The  “cases  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§21-3(1)]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to any of the following subparagraphs: [February 27, 2025] 

1. Issues for which no trading was made during the regular market trading hours on the   
Day; and [February 27, 2025] 

2. Issues notified by the multilateral trading company as those to be traded on the day. In 
this  case,  KRX may exclude stocks if it is  unable to  receive notification  on or confirm 
the stocks subject to trading at the multilateral trading company due to system failure, etc. 
[February 27, 2025] 

(2) Quotations eligible to  participate in  the determination of price of issues traded in  off-
hours call auctions pursuant to [§21-3(2)] of the Regulation shall be those received by the 
time when the Exchange specifies randomly within thirty (30) seconds after the time when 
every ten (10)-minute {every thirty (30)-minute in the case of subparagraphs 2, 3 and 4 of 
[§23(1)]} has elapsed from the opening of quotation receiving hour for off-hours periodic 
call trade (referred to as the “unit trade execution time” hereinafter in this Article, and in 
the  case  of  being  applied  by  [§23-3(1)1],  it  shall  be  until  the  time  extended  for  two  (2) 
minutes  after  the  unit  execution  time),  and  those  received  earlier,  but  have  not  been 
executed,  if  there  are  any.  (Amended  on  February  3,  2009;  July  29,  2010;  October  17, 
2014; May 19, 2015; February 28, 2017) 

(3) [Deleted on May 19, 2015]   

(4) [Deleted on July 11, 2019] 

(5) The provisions of [§17(2)] of the Regulation shall apply mutatis mutandis to the priority 
of  quotations  for  off-hours  periodic  call  trade  pursuant  to  [§21-3(4)]  of  the  Regulation. 
(Amended on February 3, 2009; July 29, 2010) 

[May 16, 2005] 

64 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§25-3. Off-hours Basket Trade   

(1) The application for off-hours basket trade pursuant to [§21-4(1)] of the Regulation shall 
be made by notifying the details negotiated by the selling and buying parties, including the 
issue, quantity and price, to the member system and the KOSDAQ system via the electronic 
network for block trading, etc. during regular session and the member placing the quotation 
in accordance with the negotiated details. 

(2)  The  trading  unit  under  [§21-4(3)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  in  accordance  with  the 
trading unit under [§18(1)].   

(3)  The  provisions  of  [§22-2(2)  through  (4)],  [§22-4(2)  through  (4)]  and  [§24(3)]  of  the 
Regulation shall apply mutatis mutandis to off-hours basket trade. 

[June 24, 2014] 

§26. Exceptions to Application of Off-hours Sessions   

The Exchange may not execute the off-hours closing price trade, off-hours block trade, off-
hours  auction-based  block  trade  off-hours  periodic  call  trade  and  off-hours  basket  trade 
pursuant  to  [§20]  through  [§21-4]  of  the  Regulation  in  the  cases  falling  under  any  of  the 
following  subparagraphs.  Provided  that,  in  the  case  of  the  off-hours  auction-based  block 
trading  of  the  issues  designated  as  administrative  issues  and  the  issues  scheduled  to  be 
delisted, the provisions of subparagraphs 2(d) and 2(f) shall not apply thereto and the trades 
shall not be executed in accordance with [§22-3(5)] and [§24-2(3)]: (Amended on May 16, 
2005;  October  14,  2005;  February  3,  2009;  March  19,  2009;  March  30,  2009;  July  29, 
2010; December 30, 2010; June 24, 2014; April 12, 2023) 

1. Case where the trading hours of the regular session is changed pursuant to [§4(1)1];   

2. Pre-hours sessions when any of the following situations occurs:   

(a) The day when trading of the issue suspended from trading has been resumed;   

(b) The first trading day for the determination of the first price of issues falling under 
[§17(1)2] or issues using the first trading price as the base price;   

(c) [Deleted on March 19, 2009]   

(d) The first trading day of issues scheduled to be delisted; (Amended on September 
8, 2006; March 30, 2009)   

(e) The first trading  day of issue  for  which the  base price is  determined differently 

65 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
pursuant to [§17(5)]; and   

(f) The day of designation as administrative issue (the first trading day following the 
designation  if  it  is  not  a  trading  day)  in  accordance  with  the  Listing  Regulation. 
Provided that this provision shall not apply to the case where other reasons are added 
on while being designated as administrative issue.   

3.  In  addition,  the  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary  for  the  market 
management.   

§27. Methods of Determining First Price of Initially Listed Issues, etc.   

(1) “Issues stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§22] of the Regulation shall refer to the 
issues  using  the  first  trading  price  as  the  base  price:  (Amended  on  October  14,  2005; 
February  3,  2009;  December  30,  2010;  April  20,  2012;  March  25,  2013;  June  16,  2014;
