1. [Deleted on April 12, 2023]   

2. [Deleted on April 12, 2023]   

3. [Deleted on April 12, 2023]   

4. [Deleted on April 12, 2023]   

5. [Deleted on March 25, 2013] 

6. [Deleted on April 12, 2023]   

(2) Method  of determining the first price on the first trading day shall be the call auction 
noted in [§18] of the Regulation. (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 30, 2010) 

(3) The range of quotations participating in the determination of the first price on the first 
trading day pursuant  to  [§22] of the  Regulation  shall be the quotations received from  the 
beginning of quotation receiving hours for the regular session to the market opening time of 
the  regular  session  and/or  the  time  randomly  set  by  the  Exchange  within  30  seconds 
thereafter. [December 30, 2010] (Amended on December 21, 2022; April 12, 2023) 

(4)  The  quotations  noted  in  paragraph  (3)  shall  be  the  quotations  received  within  the 
following prices: (Amended on April 12, 2023)   

1. An issue using the first trading price as the base price (excluding an issue scheduled 
to be delisted); The lowest quotation price and the highest quotation price pursuant to 

66 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex 1]; and 

2. An initially listed issue noted in  [§17(1)2a]:  The highest price limit  and the lowest 
price limit pursuant to the price limit range noted in [§17-2(3)]. 

§28. Trade Execution Methods of Issues scheduled to be delisted, etc.   

(1)  “Methods  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  noted  in  provisions  other  than  each 
subparagraph of [§23(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to the trade execution by way of call 
auction  pursuant  to  [§18]  of  the  Regulation.  In  such  cases,  [§18(3)  through  (7)]  of  the 
Regulation shall apply mutatis mutandis to the issues designated as temporary overheated 
issue and call auction issues with abnormally soaring price, and [§18(4) through (6)] of the 
Regulation shall apply mutatis mutandis to the issues scheduled to be delisted. (Amended 
on  March  30,  2009;  October  26,  2012;  October  17,  2014;  May  19,  2015;  February  28, 
2017; February 27, 2025) 

(2) The range of quotations to be included in determining the price mentioned in paragraph 
(1)  shall  be  the  quotations  received  by  the  time  the  Exchange  specifies  randomly  within 
thirty (30) seconds after any of the following points of time and the unexecuted quotations 
that were received earlier, if there are any. (Amended on March 19, 2009; March 30, 2009; 
October 26, 2012; October 17, 2014; May 19, 2015; February 28, 2017)   

1.  Where  the  price  is  determined  according  to  [§18(1)1]  of  the  Regulation,  from  the 
opening  of  quotation  receiving  hour  for  the  regular  session  to  the  time  of  the  market 
opening;   

2. In the case of determining the price at each time when 30-minute has passed from the 
market  opening,  from  the  time  of  market  opening  to  every  time  when  30-minute  has 
passed  (refereeing  to  “the  unit  trade  execution  time”;  the  same  hereinafter  in  this 
Article)  since  the  market  opening.  Provided  that,  in  the  case  of  determining  the  price 
noted in [§18(1)3] of the Regulation, it shall be each time when 30-minute has passed 
after the time of trade resumption, but if the trade resumption time is during the ten (10) 
minutes immediately before the market closing time, such trade resumption time shall 
not  be  included.  In  such  cases,  when  determining  the  price  noted  in  [§18(1)4]  of  the 
Regulation,  if  the  period  from  the  trade  resumption  time  to  the  nearest  unit  trade 
execution  time  is  less  than  ten  (10)  minutes,  it  shall  be  until  the  next  unit  trade 
execution time; and   

3.  In  the  case  of  determining  price  according  [§18(1)2]  of  the  Regulation,  from  the 
latest  unit  trade  execution  time  among  the  unit  trade  execution  times  pursuant  to 
subparagraph 2 to the market closing time.   

(3) Notwithstanding paragraphs (1) and (2), the provisions of [§19-2], [§19-4], [§20], [§21], 

67 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[§21-3] and [§21-4] of the Regulation shall apply to the trading in the regular session other 
than the call auction. Provided that, [§21(2)], [§21-3(3)] and [§21-4(2)] of the Regulation 
shall  not  apply  to  the  issues  scheduled  to  be  delisted.  (Amended  on  May  16  2005; 
December 23, 2005; February 3, 2009; March 30, 2009; July 29, 2010; June 24, 2014; May 
19, 2015)   

(4)  Notwithstanding  the  latter  part  of  paragraph  (1)  (limited  to  the  temporary  overheated 
issues and the call auction issues with abnormally soaring price) in applying [§18(7)] of the 
Regulation mutatis mutandis, in cases where the trading was suspended or halted during the 
quotation receiving hours of a trading day pursuant to each subparagraph of paragraph (2), 
and  the  trading  has  not  been  resumed  in  the  day,  the  quotations  that  are  restricted  to 
participate in the determination of special quotation price shall be those received during the 
day. (Amended on  March 30, 2009; October 26, 2012;  October 17, 2014;  May 19, 2015; 
February 28, 2017) 

(5)  The  periods  for  changing  the  trade  execution  methods  of  the  call  auction  issues  with 
abnormally  soaring  prices  shall  be  as  follows.  Provided  that,  in  cases  where  it  is  deemed 
necessary  for  the  market  management,  the  Exchange  may  determine  such  periods 
differently: [February 28, 2017] 

1.  In  the  case  of  falling  under  [§7-2(1)1]  of  the  Enforcement  Rules  of  the  Market 
Oversight Regulation: Three (3) trading days from the day following the date of request; 
and 

2.  In  the  case  of  falling  under  [§7-2(1)2]  of  the  Enforcement  Rules  of  the  Market 
Oversight Regulation: From the day following the date of designation as investment risk 
issue pursuant to [§3-4] of the Enforcement Rules of the Market Oversight Regulation to 
the previous day of the date of release therefrom. 

(6)  In cases  where  it is  deemed necessary  for the investor protection and market  stability 
due to sudden changes in the market situation, etc., the following additional measures may 
be  taken  pursuant  to  the  proviso  to  the  part  other  than  subparagraphs  of  [§23(1)]  of  the 
Regulation: [February 28, 2017] (Amended on November 26, 2020) 

1. Change of the price change limits pursuant to [§14(2)] of the Regulation; 

2. Change of the rates under paragraphs (1) and (2) of [§28-5]; and 

3. Other measures that are deemed necessary for the market management. 

(7)  When  making  changes  in  the  trade  execution  methods  pursuant  to  paragraph  (5)  or 
taking  the  additional  measures  pursuant  to  paragraph  (6),  the  Exchange  shall  officially 
announce such fact immediately and notify it to the members. In such cases, the provision 

68 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
of [§8-5(8)] shall apply mutatis mutandis to the notification methods. [February 28, 2017] 
(Amended on November 26, 2020; February 27, 2025) 

§28-2. Designation of Temporary Overheated Issues 

(1) “Criteria specified in the Enforcement Rules” in each subparagraph of [§23-2(1)] of the 
Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  case  where  an  issue  falls  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs  (limited  to  the  case  where  the  closing  price  on  the  day  of  making  the 
decision on whether or not falling under the criteria is higher than the closing prices of the 
immediately preceding trading day and the trading day immediately preceding the date of 
prior  notification  of  designation  for  the  issues  stipulated  in  subparagraphs  1  through  5) 
within ten (10) trading  days after issuing  the prior notification on the possibility of being 
designated as a temporary overheated issue pursuant to [§28-3(1)]. Provided that, in cases 
where an issue noted in subparagraph 2 was forewarned on the designation as a temporary 
overheated issue pursuant to [§28-3(1)1], the provisions of subparagraph 2 shall apply even 
in the case when six (6) months elapse since the trade resumption before the end of ten (10) 
trading days after the prior notification of designation. (Amended on April 26, 2013; March 
23, 2016; May 4, 2016; May 30, 2018; September 10, 2019; September 21, 2020) 

1. For an issue, which is managed as an administrative issue or investment precaution 
issue,  whose  the  number  of  circulating  common  stocks  (referring  to  the  number  of 
stocks  that  are  available  after  excluding  the  number  of  stocks  held  by  the  largest 
shareholder, etc. from the number of floating stocks; the same hereinafter) is less than 
5/100  of  the  total  number  of  common  stocks  of  the  relevant  listed  corporation  or 
300,000 shares (this provision shall not apply if  the listed corporation of the relevant 
issue  proves  that  it  does  not  fall  under  the  criteria  specified  in  this  Subparagraph  for 
such  reasons  as  the  supplementary  listing  resulting  from  a  capital  increase  with 
consideration,  release  from  the  mandatory  holding  under  [§2(15)3&4]  of  the  Listing 
Regulation,  etc.),  the  case  of  meeting  any  of  subparagraphs  1  through  3  under  [§28-
3(3)]: 

(a) The number of circulating stocks as stated in the Summary Table of Shareholders 
of  KOSDAQ-listed  Corporations  as  of  the  end  of  the  latest  fiscal  year  under 
[§26(14)] of the Enforcement Rules of KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation; and 

(b) In the case of a listing change or supplementary listing pursuant to [§18] of the 
Listing Regulation due to capital reduction, reverse stock split or capital increase or 
decrease during the rehabilitation procedures, etc., the number of circulating stocks 
as stated in the Status of Circulating Stocks of KOSDAQ-listed Corporations under 
[§18(1)9] of the Enforcement Rules of KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation. 

2.  For  an  issue  of  common  stocks  whose  trading  was  resumed  in  the  latest  six  (6) 
months  after  having  been  suspended  for  thirty  (30)  trading  days  or  longer  for  such 

69 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
reasons  of  capital  reduction,  reverse  stock  split,  capital  increase/decrease  during  the 
rehabilitation  procedures,  etc.,  the  case  of  meeting  any  of  the  criteria  specified  in 
subparagraphs 1 through 3 of [§28-3(3)]; 

3. [Deleted on September 21, 2020]   

4. For an issue that was designated as an administrative issue due to the failure to meet 
the stock distribution requirements under subparagraph 13 or 15-2(b) of [§28(1)] of the 
Listing Regulation, the case of meeting any of the subparagraphs 1 through 3 of [§28-
3(3)]; and 

5.  For  an  issue  other  than  those  noted  in  subparagraphs  1  through  4  (excluding  the 
different  classes  of  stock  subject  to  call  auction  pursuant  to  [§28-8(1)]),  the  case  of 
meeting all of the requirements under subparagraphs 1 through 3 of [§28-3(3)]. 

6.  For  an  issue  of  different  classes  of  stock  which  does  not  fall  under  the  different 
classes of stock subject to call auction pursuant to [§28-8(1)], the case of meeting all 
the requirements under subparagraph 4 of [§28-3(3)]. 

(2) The Exchange may designate an issue falling under any of the subparagraphs of [§23-
2(1)]  of  the  Regulation  as  a  temporary  overheated  issue  on  the  following  trading  day. 
Provided  that  this  provision  shall  not  apply  to  any  of  the  following  cases:  (Amended  on 
January 7, 2026) 

1. Where an issue falling under paragraph (1)5 or paragraph (1)6 is ranked within the 
top 100 based on the value obtained by multiplying the closing price of the preceding 
trading  day  by  the  number  of  shares  listed  on  the  KOSPI  or  KOSDAQ  Markets;  or 
[January 7, 2026] 

2. Any other case where such designation is deemed manifestly inappropriate. [January 
7, 2026] 

[October 26, 2012] 

§28-3. Prior Notification of Designation as Temporary Overheated Issue 

(1) In cases where an issue falls under any of the following cases, the Exchange may issue a 
prior notification on the following trading day about the fact that the relevant issue may be 
designated as a temporary overheated issue: (Amended on April 26, 2013; March 23, 2016; 
May 4, 2016; May 30, 2018; September 21, 2020)           

1.  For  an  issue  noted  in  subparagraphs  1  through  4  of  [§28-2(1)],  the  case  where  the 
closing  price  of  the  day  when  any  of  the  criteria  specified  in  the  subparagraphs  1 

70 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
through 3 under paragraph (3) was met is higher than that of the immediately preceding 
trading day;   

2. For the issues other than those noted in subparagraph 5 in [§28-2(1)], the case where 
the  issue  once  again  falls  under  all  of  the  criteria  specified  in  the  subparagraphs  1 
through 3 under paragraph (3) (limited to the case where the closing price of the day of 
making  the  decision  on  whether  or  not  the  criteria  are  met  is  higher  than  the  closing 
prices  of  the  immediately  preceding  trading  day  and  the  base  day)  within  ten  (10) 
trading  days  from  the  trading  day  (referred  to  as  the  “base  day”  in  this  Article) 
following the day when all of the criteria specified in subparagraphs 1 through 3 under 
paragraph  (3)  are  met  and  the  closing  price  of  such  day  is  higher  than  that  of  the 
immediately preceding trading day; and 

3. For the issue pursuant to [§28-2(1)6], the case where the issue once again falls under 
the  criteria  specified  in  subparagraph  4  of  paragraph  (3)  within  ten  (10)  trading  days 
from  the  trading  day  after  the  day  when  the  criteria  specified  in  subparagraph  4  of 
paragraph (3) are met. 

(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), in cases where an issue falls under any of the following 
subparagraphs, the Exchange may not issue the prior notification for the relevant issue on 
the  fact  about  possible  designation  as  a  temporary  overheated  issue:  (Amended  on 
December 10, 2015) 

1. [Deleted on December 10, 2015] 

2.  In  addition,  in  cases  where  it  is  clearly  inappropriate  for  an  issue  to  issue  a  prior 
notification about the possible designation as a temporary overheated issue. 

(3) The Exchange shall calculate the criteria noted in each of the following subparagraphs 
for each issue (limited to the stocks and  DRs of foreign  stocks) on  a daily  basis.  In such 
cases,  the  numbers  shall  be  rounded  off  at  the  fourth  decimal  places.  (Amended  on 
September 21, 2020)     

1. Rate of price increase 

The closing price of the day shall be at least 130/100 of the average of closing prices of 
most recent forty (40) trading days. 

2. Turnover ratio 

The average of daily turnover ratios (to be calculated using the following formula) of 
most recent two (2) trading days (based on the trading day of the issue), including the 
relevant  day,  shall  be  at  least  600/100  of  the  average  daily  turnover  ratios  of  most 
recent forty (40) trading days:     

71 

 
 
 
 
 
 
   
 
 
 
 
Daily turnover ratio = {Total trading value of trades executed using individual auction 
method during the trading hours of regular session of the day / (Closing price of the day 
x Total number of listed stocks)} 

3. Price volatility 

Average of daily price volatilities (to be calculated using the formula noted below) of 
most recent two (2) trading days (to be based on the trading day of issue), including the 
relevant day, shall be at least 150/100 of the average of daily price volatilities of most 
recent forty (40) trading days.   

Daily price volatility = {Highest price (referring to the price established by individual 
auction in the trading hours of regular session of the day) – Lowest price} / {(Highest 
price + Lowest price) / 2} 

4. Disparate ratio 

The disparate ratio (calculated by the below formula) between the price of the different 
classes of stock and the price of the relevant common stocks based on the closing price 
of the day shall exceed 50/100. 

Disparate ratio = (Price of different classes of stock – Price of relevant common stocks) 
/ Price of relevant common stocks 

(4) Notwithstanding paragraph (3), the parameters noted in each subparagraph of paragraph 
(3) shall not be calculated for the issue  falling under any of the following subparagraphs: 
(Amended on April 26, 2013; March 23, 2016; May 4, 2016; February 28, 2017; January 2, 
2018; May 30, 2018; September 21, 2020) 

1. Temporary overheated issues; 

2. Issues scheduled to be delisted; 

3. Issues suspended from trading;   

4.  Issues  for  which  the  number  of  days  with  trades  executed  by  individual  auction 
during the trading hours (including trading hours corresponding to the regular market of 
the Exchange among the trading hours of the multilateral trading company) of regular 
sessions in the latest forty (40) days is twenty (20) [three (3) days for the issues noted in 
subparagraphs 1 through 4 of [§28-2(1)] or less; and (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

5.  Investment  alert  issues  or  investment  risk  issues  (including  issues  scheduled  to  be 
designated  as  investment  alert  issues  or  investment  risk  issues  on  the  next  day). 

72 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Provided  that,  the  issues  under  subparagraphs  1  through  4  of  [§28-2(1)]  shall  be 
excluded. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(5)  In  the  case  of  an  issue  that  has  been  released  from  the  designation  as  temporary 
overheated  issue  pursuant  to  [§28-4],  the  base  day  (including  the  day  on  which  an  issue 
under  subparagraph  3  of  paragraph  (1)  meets  the  requirement  under  subparagraph  4  of 
paragraph (3) for the first time) may be re-established after the release date. (Amended on 
September 21, 2020) 

(6) Each of “average of closing prices” noted in paragraph (3)1, “average of daily turnover 
ratios” noted in paragraph (3)2 and “average of daily price volatilities” noted in paragraph 
(3)3 shall be calculated on the basis of trading day of the relevant issue.   

(7) The “total value of the trades executed by continuous auction during the trading hours 
of regular  session of the day”  noted in the calculation  formula of  paragraph (3)2 shall be 
calculated by including the trading value of the multilateral trading company (limited to the 
trading value during the trading hours corresponding to the regular market of the Exchange; 
the same hereinafter in this paragraph), however, in the case where the Exchange is unable 
to receive information on trading value of the multilateral trading company, due to system 
failure, etc., it may be calculated excluding such information. [February 27, 2025] 

[October 26, 2012] 

§28-4. Release from Designation as Temporary Overheated Issue, etc. 

(1) The Exchange shall release the issue designated as temporary overheated issue on the 
trading  day  following  the  day  when  the  period  specified  in  each  of  the  following 
subparagraphs expires: (Amended on April 26, 2013; December 10, 2015; March 23, 2016; 
May 4, 2016; May 30, 2018; September 21, 2020) 

1. For the issues falling under subparagraphs 1 through 4 of [§28-2(1)], ten (10) trading 
days.  Provided  that,  in  cases  where  it  is  confirmed  that  the  issue  does  not  fall  under 
subparagraph 1 or 4 of [§28-2(1)], the issue shall be released from such designation on 
the day following the date of confirmation; and 

2. For the cases noted in subparagraphs 5 and 6 of [§28-2(1)], three (3) trading days. 

(2)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1),  in  the  case  of  falling  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs, such designation shall be released on the day specified in the corresponding 
subparagraph: (Amended on April 26, 2013; December 10, 2015; March 23, 2016; May 4, 
2016; May 30, 2018; September 21, 2020)   

1.  Cases  falling  under  subparagraphs  1  through  5  of  [§28-2(1)]:  In  cases  where  the 

73 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
       
 
 
closing  price  of  the  day  when  the  period  specified  in  each  subparagraph  under 
paragraph  (1)  expires  is  higher  than  120/100  of  that  of  the  trading  day  immediately 
preceding  the  designation  date,  the  issue  concerned  shall  be  released  from  the 
designation  on  the  trading  day  after  the  day  when  the  period  specified  in  each 
subparagraph  under  paragraph  (1)  expires.  In  such  cases,  if  a  temporary  overheated 
issue corresponds to any issue noted in subparagraphs 1 through 4 of [§28-2(1)] on the 
day  when  the  period  stipulated  in  subparagraph  2  of  paragraph  (1)  ends,  the  period 
specified in subparagraph 1 of paragraph (1) shall apply; 

2.  Cases falling under subparagraph 6 of [§28-2(1)]: In cases where the disparate ratio 
calculated  based  on  the  closing  price  on  the  day  when  the  period  specified  in 
subparagraph 2 of paragraph (1) ends meets the requirement specified in subparagraph 
4  of  [§28-3(3)],  the  concerned  issue  shall  be  released  from  the  trading  day  after  that 
until  the  designation  on  the  trading  day  after  the  day  when  the  period  specified  in 
subparagraph  2  under  paragraph  (1)  expires.    In  such  cases,  if  the  disparate  ratio 
calculated based on the closing price on the day when the extension period ends meets 
the requirement  specified  in  subparagraph 4 of [§28-3(3)] once  again,  the designation 
shall  be  re-extended  for  the  period  specified  in  subparagraph  2  of  paragraph  (1),  and 
this shall apply repeatedly until the disparate ratio calculated based on the closing price 
on  the  day  when  the  re-extension  period  ends  does  not  satisfy  the  requirement  in 
subparagraph 4 of [§28-3(3)]; and 

3.  Cases satisfying the requirements specified in subparagraphs 5 and 6 of [§28-2(1)] 
at the same time: The later of the days specified in subparagraphs 1 and 2. 

(3) In cases where ex-dividends, ex-rights, stock split or reverse stock split, etc. have taken 
place,  the  “closing  price”  noted  in  [§28-2(1)],  [§28-3(1)  &  (3)]  and  [§28-3(2)]  shall  be 
determined by taking into account such facts.   

[October 26, 2012] 

(4) Regarding the matters concerning the temporary overheated issues stated in [§28-2] and 
[§28-3]  and  paragraph  (1)  and  (2)  of  this  article,  the  Exchange  shall  officially  announce 
such fact and notify the members of the issues immediately. In such cases, the provision of 
[§8-5(8)]  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis  to  the  notification  methods.  [November  26,  2020] 
(Amended on February 27, 2025) 

§28-5. Change of Trade Execution Method by Issue 

(1)  “Rates  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§23-3(1)1]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be 
6%. Provided that, in the case of falling under any of the following subparagraphs, it shall 
be as stipulated in the relevant subparagraph: (Amended on May 19, 2015; March 21, 2018; 
July 11, 2019) 

74 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1.  In  the  case  of  quotation  receiving  hours  for  determination  of  the  market  closing 
prices under [§18(1)2] of the Regulation, 4%; and 

2.  In  the  case  of  quotation  receiving  hours  for  determination  of  prices  at  the  market 
closing  of  the  underlying  stocks  (in  the  case  of  stock  indices,  it  refers  to  the 
constituents  of  the  relevant  index;  the  same  hereinafter  in  this  Article)  on  the  last 
trading  day of single stock futures of the equity derivatives market  under [§3(2)1] of 
the Derivatives Market Business Regulation, 1%. 

(2)  “Rates  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§23-3(1)2]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be 
10%. [May 19, 2015] 

(3)  The  change  of  trade  execution  method,  etc.  under  [§23-3(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall 
refer to an action falling under any of the followings during the time specified in [§20(1)4] 
of the Regulation;   

1. In the case of continuous call auction; Change into call auction; and 

2. In the case of call auction; Expansion of the range of participating quotations. 

(4)  Notwithstanding  the  provisions  of  [§23-3(1)]  of  the  Regulation,  when  an  issue  falls 
under any of following subparagraphs, any change to the trade execution method, etc. shall 
not be made: (Amended on October 17, 2014; May 19, 2015; March 25, 2016; February 28, 
2017; September 12, 2018; July 11, 2019; September 21, 2020; November 26, 2020) 

1. Issues scheduled to be delisted; 

2. Temporary overheated issues; (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

2-2. Call auction issues with abnormally soaring price; 

2-3.  Low  liquidity  issues  subject  to  call  auction  pursuant  to  [§28-7(1)]  and  different 
classes of stock subject to the call auction stated in [§28-8(1)]; 

2-4.  Newly  listed  issues  (limited  to  the  day  of  listing  on  stocks  or  DRs,  excluding 
issues transferred from the KOSPI market) 

3. Where the call auction is conducted to determine the prices noted in subparagraphs 3 
and  4  of  [§18(1)]  of  the  Regulation  when  resuming  the  halted  or  suspended  trading 
before the day’s market closing time. Provided that this provision shall not apply to the 
case  where  the  execution  method  was  changed  to  the  call  auction  under  [§18]  of  the 
Regulation pursuant to [§28-7(2)]; 

75 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
4.  Where  the  trade  execution  method,  etc.  is  changed  as  it  falls  under  any  of  the 
subparagraphs  of  paragraph  (1)  or  paragraph  (2),  and  the  first  price  determined 
pursuant to [§18(1)5] of the Regulation falls again under any of the subparagraphs of 
paragraph (1) or paragraph (2);   

5. [Deleted on May 19, 2015] 

6. Where a provisional matching price based on the quotation is determined within the 
five (5) quotation units on the basis of the most recent price (restricted to a case where 
the  price  is  less  than  KRW  1,000)  as  at  the  time  when  the  relevant  quotation  is 
received; or 

7. Other cases that the Exchange deems necessary considering market situation etc.   

(5)  Pursuant  to  [§23-3(3)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  Exchange  may  determine  the  ratio 
standard  referred  to  in  paragraphs  (1)  and  (2)  differently  when  it  seems  difficult 
significantly  to  apply  the  ratio  standard  referred  to  in  paragraphs  (1)  and  (2)  considering 
quotations and market circumstances, etc. (Amended on May 19, 2015) 

(6) Pursuant to [§23-3(1)] of the Regulation, the change of trade execution method by issue 
shall apply after applying the self-match prevention condition noted in [§18-3]. [December 
22, 2022] 

[June 24, 2014]   

§28-6. Publication of Changes of the Methods of Executing Trade by Issue, etc. 

(1) The Exchange shall make public the fact immediately if any changes to the methods, etc. 
of executing trade are made pursuant to [§23-3(1) & (3)] of the Regulation. (Amended on 
May 19, 2015) 

(2) The Exchange  shall include changed details  such as  name of issue, changed/  released 
time and the methods of executing trade of issue when making public pursuant to paragraph 
(1). 

[June 24, 2014]   

§28-7. Methods of Trade Execution of Low Liquidity Issues 

(1) “Issue of which trading is deemed significantly inactive in terms of trade frequency in 
the light of the criteria stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§23-4(1)] of the Regulation 
shall  refer  to  an  issue  with  low  liquidity  subject  to  period  call  auction  that  is  selected 

76 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
according to the criteria specified in [Annex 5] (hereinafter referred to as the “low liquidity 
issue subject to call auction”). (Amended on December 27, 2018; September 21, 2020) 

(2) The trade execution of a low liquidity issue subject to call auction shall be conducted by 
the way of call auction under [§18] of the Regulation. Provided that this provision shall not 
apply to an issue that falls under the criteria for exclusion under [Annex 5] or is released 
from  the  list  of  low  liquidity  issues  subject  to  call  auction  during  the  effective  period. 
(Amended on December 27, 2018) 

(3) [Deleted on December 27, 2018] 

(4)  The  provisions  of  [§18(3)  through  (7)]  of  the  Regulation  and  [§28(2)]  (the  provisos 
other  than  the  main  body  shall  be  excluded)  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis  to  the  low 
liquidity issues subject to call auction. (Amended on November 26, 2020) 

(5) Notwithstanding paragraphs (2) and (4), the provisions from [§19-2] to [§21-4] of the 
Regulation  shall  apply  to  the  trades  that  are  executed  by  the  methods  other  than  the 
continuous  auction  during  the  trading  hours  of  a  regular  session.  In  such  cases,  “ten  (10) 
minutes” in [§25-2(2)] shall be construed as “thirty (30) minutes”. (Amended on September 
21, 2020; November 26, 2020; February 27, 2025) 

(6)  The  matters  necessary  for  the  application  of  the  selection,  additional  selection, 
applicable  period,  etc.  of  the  low  liquidity  issues  subject  to  call  auction  other  than  those 
stipulated in paragraphs (1) and (2) shall be set forth in [Annex 5]. (Amended on December 
27, 2018) 

(7) The Exchange shall officially announce the low liquidity issues subject to call auction 
pursuant  to  the  provisions  of  paragraphs  (1)  through  (6)  immediately  and  notify  the 
members  of  the  issues.  In  such  cases,  the  provision  of  [§8-5(8)]  shall  apply  mutatis 
mutandis  to  the  notification  methods.  [November  26,  2020]  (Amended  on  February  27, 
2025) 

[March 25, 2016] 

§28-8.  Trade  Execution  Methods  of  Different  Classes  of  Stock  with  Insufficient 
Number of Listed Stocks 

(1)  “The  issue  whose  number  of  listed  stocks  does  not  meet  the  criteria  stipulated  in  the 
Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§23-4(2)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  different  classes  of 
stock with less than five hundred thousand (500,000) listed stocks (hereinafter referred to as 
the “different classes of stock subject to call auction”). 

(2) The number of listed stocks in paragraph (1) shall be assessed on the last trading day of 

77 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
each  quarter,  and  in  cases  where  it  falls  under  the  requirement  in  paragraph  (1),  the 
concerned  issue  shall  be  selected  as  the  different  classes  of  stock  subject  to  call  auction 
during the following quarter of the quarter in which the assessment date belongs. 

(3) The trade execution method of the different classes of stock subject to call auction shall 
be the call auction by single price pursuant to [§18] of the Regulation. 

(4)  The  provisions  of  [§18(3)  through  (7)]  of  the  Regulation  and  [§28(2)]  of  the 
Enforcement Rules (excluding the provisos other than the main clause) shall apply mutatis 
mutandis to the different classes of stock subject to call auction. 

(5)  Notwithstanding  paragraphs  (3)  and  (4),  the  provisions  of  [§19-2]  through  [§21-4]  of 
the Regulation shall apply to the trades other than those executed by the continuous auction 
during the trading hours of a regular session. In such cases, “ten (10) minutes” in [§25-2(2)] 
shall be construed as “thirty (30) minutes”. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(6)  In  cases  where  a  low  liquidity  issue  subject  to  call  auction  pursuant  to  [§28-7(1)]  is 
selected  as  different  classes  of  stock  subject  to  call  auction  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1), 
paragraphs (1) through (5) shall take priority over [§28-7] during the selected period. 

(7)  The  Exchange  shall  officially  announce  the  different  classes  of  stock  subject  to  call 
auction pursuant to the provisions of paragraphs (1) through (6) immediately and notify the 
members  of  the  stocks.  In  such  cases,  the  provision  of  [§8-5(8)]  shall  apply  mutatis 
mutandis  to  the  notification  methods.  [September  21,  2020]  [November  26,  2020] 
(Amended on February 27, 2025) 

§29. Details of Trade Execution   

(1)  In  the  trade  details  referred  to  in  [§24(1)]  of  the  Regulation,  each  of  the  following 
subparagraphs shall be recorded: (Amended on September 27, 2005; February 3, 2009; July 
29, 2010)   

1. Classification of sale or purchase;   

2. Name of issue;   

3.  Price  (excluding  the  price  established  as  a  result  of  auction-based  block  trade)  and 
quantity;   

4. Classification of brokering or dealing; and   

5. Name or ID number of the member.   

(2)  Pursuant  to  [§24(2)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  Exchange  shall  notify  the  designated 

78 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
clearing members each of the following details of the trades executed under the names of 
non-clearing members after the market closing. Provided that the details noted in paragraph 
(2)4  shall  be  notified  to  the  designated  clearing  member  only  when  the  prior  consent  of 
non-clearing member has been obtained. [September 27, 2005] (Amended on September 27, 
2005; July 7, 2006; February 3, 2009) 

1. ID number of non-clearing member;   

1-2. Issue name; 

2. Quantities sold and quantities purchased;   

3. Sale amount and purchase amount; and   

4. In addition, any other details that are deemed necessary by the Exchange.   

(3) The Exchange shall notify the price established as a result of auction-based block trade 
to the members via the computer system immediately after the market closing and it shall 
be  deemed  that  the  member  has  confirmed  the  relevant  details  upon  receiving  the 
notification. [July 29, 2010] 

§30. Suspension of Trade and Resumption of Trade Thereafter   

(1)  The  period  of  trade  suspension  of  the  issue  of  which  the  trading  has  been  suspended 
pursuant  to  [§25(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  any  one  of  the  followings:  (Amended  on 
June  28,  2005;  October  14,  2005;  July  7,  2006;  August  16,  2007;  December  27,  2007; 
February  3,  2009;  October  26,  2012;  February  28,  2014;  December  10,  2015;  May  10, 
2016; February 28, 2017) 

1. For one (1) day, in  the case of  falling  under [§25(1)1] of the Regulation. Provided 
that  it  shall  be  the  period  not  longer  than  five  (5)  days  in  cases  when  the  Exchange 
deems it necessary; 

2. Until the time when the relevant cause of trade suspension is deemed to have been 
resolved in the cases falling under any of subparagraphs 2 through 6 of [§25(1)]; and 

3. In the case of falling under [§25(1)5-2] of the Regulation, for the period requested. 
Provided that, in cases where the Exchange deems it necessary for market management, 
the period specified separately. 

4. [Deleted on December 10, 2015] 

(2)  Period  of  trade  suspension  of  subscription  warrants  and  subscription  right  certificates 
pursuant  to  [§25(2)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  the  period  of  trade  suspension  of  the 
relevant issue. [December 29, 2009] (Amended on March 16, 2026) 

79 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(3) The calculation of period noted in paragraphs (1) and (2) shall be based on the trading 
day  (including  the  day  when  trading  is  suspended)  pursuant  to  [§4(3)]  of  the  Regulation. 
(Amended on December 29, 2009; December 21, 2022) 

(4)  In cases  where it is  deemed necessary  for the investor protection  and market  stability 
due to sudden changes in the market situation, etc., pursuant to the proviso to the part other 
than the subparagraphs of [§25(1)] of the Regulation, the Exchange may take the following 
additional measures from the date of release from the trade suspension: [February 28, 2017] 

1.  Change  of  the  trade  execution  methods  of  the  call  auction  issues  with  abnormally 
soaring price noted in paragraphs (1) through (4) of [§28]; 

2. Change of the price change limits specified in [§14(2)] of the Regulation; 

3. Change of the rates specified in paragraphs (1) and (2) of [§28-5]; and 

4. Other measures that are deemed necessary for market management. 

(5) When taking the measure of trade suspension noted in paragraph (1) or the additional 
measures  noted  in  paragraph  (4),  the  Exchange  shall  officially  announce  such  fact 
immediately  and  notify  it  to  the  members.  In  such  cases,  the  provision  of  [§8-5(8)]  shall 
apply  mutatis  mutandis  to  the  notification  methods.  [February  28,  2017]  (Amended  on 
November 26, 2020; February 27, 2025) 

§30-2.  Measures  in  Case  of  Computer  System  Failures  or  Excessive  Influx  of 
Quotations 

(1)  Pursuant  to  [§25-2]  of  the  Regulation,  in  cases  where  a  computer  system  failure  has 
been  confirmed,  the  Exchange  may  take  any  of  the  following  measures:  (Amended  on 
February 3, 2009; February 28, 2014; January 15, 2026) 

    1. Cancellation of quotations that caused computer system failure; or [January 15, 2026] 

    2.  Suspension  of  receiving  quotations  (referring  to  the  suspension  of  receiving  new 
quotations,  correction  quotations,  and  cancellation  quotations;  the  same  hereinafter)  or 
halt of trading. In this case, if the restoration of details of quotations is impossible or it is 
necessary to promptly recover from a computer system failure, quotations that have not 
been concluded by the time of suspension of receiving quotations or halt of trading may 
be cancelled. [January 15, 2026] 

(2) Pursuant to [§25-2] of the Regulation, in cases where there is a possibility of a computer 
system  failure  due  to  excessive  influx  of  quotations,  the  Exchange  may  take  any  of  the 

80 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
following measures: [January 15, 2026] 

    1. Suspension of receiving quotations or halt of trading. In this case, if the restoration of 
details  of  quotations  is  impossible  or  there  is  a  risk  of  computer  system  failure  during 
restoration,  quotations  that  have  not  been  concluded  by  the  time  of  suspension  of 
receiving quotations or halt of trading may be cancelled; or [January 15, 2026] 

    2. Closing of trading of the day. [January 15, 2026]   

(3) When the Exchange determines  that the computer system  is  back  to normal  operation 
and  the  risk  of  computer  system  failure  due  to  excessive  influx  of  quotations  has  been 
eliminated  following  the  suspension  of  receiving  quotations  or  the  halt  of  trading  under 
paragraph (1)2 or paragraph (2)1, the receiving of  quotations or trading  shall resume at  a 
time determined by the Exchange. In such cases, when the recovery of quotations and trade 
details, etc. is not possible due to inevitable causes such as natural disaster and other similar 
reason, the recovery may proceed except for such areas. [February 28, 2014] (Amended on 
January 15, 2026) 

(4)  In  cases  where  trading  is  resumed  pursuant  to  paragraph  (3),  the  first  price  shall  be 
determined  by  way  of  the  call  auction  under  [§18]  of  the  Regulation.  In  such  cases,  the 
range of quotations participating in the determination of such price shall be decided by the 
Exchange  at  each  case.  (Amended  on  February  3,  2009;  February  28,  2014;  January  15, 
2026) 

(5)  When  determining  the  range  of  quotations  participating  in  the  determination  of  the 
relevant price pursuant to the latter part of paragraph (4), the Exchange shall make public 
such  fact  without  delay.  (Amended  on  February  3,  2009;  February  28,  2014;  January  15, 
2026) 

(6) In addition  to  paragraphs (1) through (5), method  of trade execution  in  the event  of a 
computer system  failure or excessive influx  of  quotations shall be in accordance with  the 
decision made by the Exchange for each case. (Amended on February 3, 2009; February 28, 
2014; January 15, 2026) 

[June 28, 2005]   

§31. Temporary Suspension of Market, etc.   

(1)  “Cases  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  other  than  each  of  the 
subparagraphs of [§26(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to the case falling under any of the 
following  subparagraphs,  and,  in  each  case,  the  trading  of  stock  market  shall  not  be 
suspended. [May 19, 2015] 

81 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. Where it does not decline by 1% or more than the KOSDAQ index at the time of the 
suspension of trading pursuant to [§26(1)1] of the Regulation, or where it does not last 
for  one  (1)  minute  after  declining  by  1%  or  more,  when  applying  [§26(1)2]  of  the 
Regulation. 

2. Where it does not decline by 1% or more than the KOSDAQ index at the time of the 
suspension of trading pursuant to [§26(1)2] of the Regulation, or where it does not last 
for  one  (1)  minute  after  declining  by  1%  or  more,  when  applying  [§26(1)3]  of  the 
Regulation. 

(2) The suspension of trading pursuant to [§26(1)1&2] of the Regulation shall apply only 
when the market falls under such condition for the first time in the day, and the market shall 
not  be  suspended  during  the  last  forty  (40)  minutes  before  the  market  closing  time. 
Provided  that  the  suspension  and  conclusion  of  trading  pursuant  to  [§26(1)3]  shall  apply 
even  during  the  last  forty  (40)  minutes  before  the  market  closing.  .  [Proviso  on  May  19, 
2015] (Amended on February 3, 2009; May 19, 2015) 

(3) In cases where the trading cannot be resumed due to the computer system failure that 
has occurred before the market resumption, the trading shall be resumed at the time when 
the computer system is recovered. Provided that this provision shall not apply to the case 
specified in the proviso to [§4(2)]. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(4) The trading suspension for one (1) minute under [§26(1)1] of the Regulation shall start 
and calculate from one (1) minute after the market opening. [November 26, 2020] 

§31-2. Publication of Suspension of Trading and Resumption Thereafter, etc.   

(1)  In  the  case  of  halting  or  resuming  a  trade  pursuant  to  [§25]  of  the  Regulation  or 
suspending or resuming the market pursuant to [§26] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall 
make such fact public without delay. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(2) [Deleted on February 28, 2014] 

[December 27, 2007] 

§32. Extent of Correction of Transaction Errors   

Transaction errors noted in [§27] of the Regulation shall be classified  into the transaction 
errors made by the Exchange and the transaction errors made by the member, and the extent 
of  correction  thereof  shall  be  each  of  the  followings:  (Amended  on  February  3,  2009; 
December 21, 2022) 

82 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. Errors made by the Exchange: Transaction where the details are not consistent with 
the quotation details, which has occurred due to the KOSDAQ system failure, a failure 
in program operation, or error made in the course of inputting the trade details; and   

2. Errors made by the members: Transaction where the details are not consistent with 
the  details  of  orders,  which  has  occurred  because  the  details  of  quotation  received  by 
KOSDAQ computer system were different from the order details due to the error made 
in  the  courses  of  processing  the  orders  received  from  customers,  inputting  such  order 
details into the member system or transmitting the quotation details into the KOSDAQ 
computer  system.  In  such  case,  if  there  is  an  error  of  an  overseas  affiliate,  etc.  of  a 
member in the course of the member’s receiving of customers’ orders of the overseas 
affiliates, etc., this error is considered as an error of the member. 

§33. Methods of Correcting Transaction Errors   

(1)  The  Exchange  shall  correct  the  transaction  errors  according  to  each  of  the  following 
methods: (Amended on February 3, 2009; June 21, 2016) 

1. For the transaction errors made by the Exchange:   

In cases where it is possible to correct the error, the Exchange shall make the correction 
according to the original quotation details, and in other cases, the error shall be corrected 
after having the member to take over the relevant issue as an own account transaction.   

2. For the transaction errors made by members: 

In the case of errors relating to the issue, quantity, price or sell/buy classification, such 
errors  are  corrected  after  the  relevant  member  took  over  the  relevant  issue  as  an  own 
account transaction, and in cases of the errors relating to classification of brokering and 
dealing  resulted  from  the  failure  in  program  operation  of  the  member  system,  the 
correction shall be made as required. Provided that this provision shall not apply to the 
large-scale transaction errors stipulated in [§35-2].   

(2) When taking over the issue pursuant to paragraph (1), in the case of a member who have 
not obtained the permit for investment dealing business in Article 6(1)1 of the Act, it shall 
be accomplished by way of such member entrusting the trade to another member as an own 
account transaction. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(3) In the case of transaction errors made by a member, the correction shall be made only in 
cases  where  the  relevant  member  has  submitted  a  request  for  correction  of  transaction 
errors according to [Annex: Form No. 8] by the time of market closing on the day after the 
transaction error has occurred. (Amended on July 7, 2006; February 3, 2009; July 31, 2009; 
June 21, 2016; November 28, 2019)   

83 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(4)  The  provisions  of  [§10(4)]  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis  to  the  case  of  correcting  the 
transaction error made by a member. [July 7, 2006] (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

§34. Agreement for Correction of Transaction Errors   

When correcting a transaction error made by the Exchange, in order to handle the issue to 
which a transaction error has occurred as the issue that the member traded through its own 
account, the Exchange shall enter into an agreement for correction of transaction error with 
the relevant member in accordance with  [Annex: Form No. 9]. (Amended on February 3, 
2009) 

§35. Settlement of Profits and Losses   

(1)  In  cases  where  transaction  error  is  corrected  by  letting  the  relevant  members  to  take 
over the relevant issue as its own account transaction, the Exchange shall settle any profit 
or loss sustained in the course of error correction.   

(2) The securities transaction tax, all commissions, and amount equivalent to member fees 
relating  to  the  correction  of  transaction  errors  shall  be  reckoned  as  a  loss  when  settling 
profits and losses pursuant to paragraph (1). (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(3) The Exchange shall settle all profits and losses without delay, upon receiving the bills 
for  settlement  of  transaction  errors  in  accordance  with  the  agreement  for  correction  of 
transaction errors. Provided that, from among the transaction errors made by the Exchange, 
those due to the negligence of the company operating the KOSDAQ computer system shall 
be settled separately. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

§35-2. Requirements for Relief of Large-scale Transaction Errors 

“Transactions that meet the requirements stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the main 
sentence of [§27-2(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to the transactions that satisfy all of the 
requirements  under  each  of  the  following  subparagraphs  for  each  account  (hereinafter 
referred to as “large-scale transaction errors”). (Amended on February 28, 2017) 

1.  It  shall  not  be  a  trade  that  was  executed  by  the  method  of  call  auction  stipulated  in 
[§18] of the Regulation; 

2. It shall not be a trade that was executed by the market making quotations; 

84 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
3. The time period between the first occurrence and the conclusion of the trade shall be 
within thirty (30) minutes; 

4. Out of the issues with transaction errors of an account, there shall be one (1) or more 
of  issues  of  which  execution  price  falls  under  each  of  the  following  items  (hereinafter 
referred to as the “issues subject to relief”):   

(a)  In  the  case  of  having  purchased  by  error:  The  price  that  went  up  by  over  10%, 
compared to the latest price immediately before the execution of the relevant trade (in 
cases  where  there  is  no  latest  price,  it  shall  be  the  first  execution  price  and  shall 
hereinafter be referred to as the “base price for the relief of transaction errors”); and 

(b)  In  the  case  of  having  sold  by  error:  The  price  that  went  down  by  over  10%, 
compared to the base price for the relief of transaction errors. 

5. The sum of the amounts obtained by multiplying the difference between the execution 
price of the issue with transaction errors of the relevant account and the base price for the 
relief  of  transaction  errors  (referring  to  the  amount  obtained  by  subtracting  the  selling 
execution  price  from  the  base  price  for  the  relief  of  transaction  errors  or  the  amount 
obtained by subtracting the base price for the relief of transaction errors from the buying 
execution price) by the execution quantity of the relevant trade shall be KRW 10 billion 
or  more.  In  this  case,  the  sum  of  the  relevant  amounts  is  calculated  separately  for  the 
stock  market  and  the  collective  investment  securities  market  of  business  development 
collective investment vehicle; (Amended on March 16, 2026) 

6. The trades shall continuously be executed by same kind of errors; and 

7. Additionally, there shall be a need for relief of the trades for the reliable and efficient 
settlement. 

[June 21, 2016] 

§35-3. Requesting for Relief of Large-scale Transaction Errors 

(1) Any member intending to request for relief of large-scale transaction errors pursuant to 
[§27-2(2)] of the Regulation (hereinafter referred to as the “request for relief”) (including a 
case  where  the  request  for  relief  is  made  by  the  customer  who  caused  the  large-scale 
transaction  errors)  shall  make  the  request  for  relief  by  way  of  inputting  the  details  of  the 
relevant large-scale transaction errors into the Exchange computer system via the member 
computer  system  or  the  member  securities  terminals.  Provided  that,  in  the  case  of  an 
emergency  including  system  failures,  etc.,  the  request  for  relief  may  be  made  by  way  of 
submitting a request prepared in accordance with [Annex: Form No. 10-2] to the Exchange. 

85 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) The request for relief shall be made within thirty (30) minutes from the time when the 
large-scale transaction errors occurred. Provided that the Exchange may extend the deadline 
for the request in cases that are deemed unavoidable, including member computer system 
failures, etc. 

(3) Any member who has made the request for relief shall submit the explanatory materials 
concerning the large-scale transaction errors to the Exchange without delay. 

(4) In cases where some of the details of the request for relief are omitted or the details of 
the  relevant  explanatory  materials  are  deemed  insufficient,  the  Exchange  may  require 
resubmission. 

(5) When receiving the request for relief from a member, the Exchange shall make public 
the fact of receiving the relevant request for relief, etc. without delay and shall notify such 
fact to the counter party member. 

[June 21, 2016] 

§35-4. Methods of relieving Large-scale Transaction Errors 

(1) Pursuant to [§27-2(2)] of the Regulation, after reviewing the details of the request for 
relief  and the explanatory  materials, the Exchange  may relieve the large-scale transaction 
errors, in cases of satisfying all of the requirements noted in each of the subparagraphs of 
[§35-2]. 

(2)  The  Exchange  shall  make  the  decision  on  whether  or  not  to  relieve  the  large-scale 
transaction errors by 17:00 hours on the next trading day of the day  when the request for 
relief was received (hereinafter referred to as the “date of the request for relief”) and make 
it public without delay and shall notify it to the member who requested for the relief and the 
counter  party  member.  The  concerned  member  shall  notify  it  to  the  relevant  customer 
without delay. 

(3)  When  it  was  decided  to  relieve  the  large-scale  transaction  errors,  the  Exchange  may 
change the settlement  prices of the issues subject  to  relief between the Exchange and the 
clearing member to the prices noted in each of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  In  the  case  of  having  bought  by  error:  The  price  (if  the  price  does  not  match  the 
quotation price unit, it shall be the price closest to that price, among the prices that are 
higher than that price and that match the quotation price unit) that is higher than the base 
price for the relief of transaction errors by 10% (the price lower than the quotation price 
unit shall be rounded off; the same hereinafter); and (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

86 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2. In the case of having sold by error: The price (if the price does not match the quotation 
price unit, it shall be the price closest to that price, among the prices that are lower than 
that price and that match the quotation price unit) that is than the base price for the relief 
of transaction errors by 10% lower. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(4) Notwithstanding paragraph (3), in cases where the counter party member has traded the 
issues subject to relief before the fact of receiving the member’s request for relief was made 
public  pursuant  to  [§35-3(5)]  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “sequential  transaction”)  and 
the  relevant  trade  satisfies  all  the  requirements  noted  in  each  of  the  following 
subparagraphs, the Exchange may determine the settlement prices differently. 

1. The counter  party member shall  make the request  for change of settlement prices to 
the Exchange in accordance with [Annex: Form No. 10-3]. In such cases, provisions of 
[§35-3(1), (3) & (4)] shall apply mutatis mutandis, but the deadline for the request shall 
be from 08:00 hours to 10:00 hours on the next trading day of the date of the request for 
relief stipulated in [§35-3] (the deadline for the customer’s request to the member shall 
be by the date of the request for relief); 

2. It shall be the cases of trading the issue purchased or sold as a result of the large-scale 
transaction  errors  within  the  executed  quantity  of  the  relevant  transaction  through  the 
same account, and of falling under each of the following items:   

(a) Case of having sold the issues purchased; or 

(b) Case of having purchased the issues sold. 

3. It shall be a trade executed by way of a continuous call auction stipulated in [§19] of 
the Regulation during the trading hours of the regular session. 

(5) When determining the settlement prices pursuant to paragraph (4), the Exchange shall 
consider the calculation of trading volume weighted average based on the sequence of trade 
executions and the prices specified in each of the following subparagraphs, etc.: 

1. For the case of paragraph (4)2(a), the price specified in each of the following items: 

(a) Where the execution price is lower than the price specified in paragraph (3)2, but 
higher than the execution price of large-scale transaction errors: the execution price 
(if  the  prices  does  not  match  up  with  the  quotation  price  unit,  it  shall  be  the  price 
closest to that price, among the prices that are higher than that price and that match 
up with the quotation price unit); and (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(b) Where the execution price is equal to or lower than the execution price of large-
scale  transaction  errors:  the  execution  price  of  large-scale  transaction  errors  (if  the 

87 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
prices does not match up with the quotation price unit, it shall be the price closest to 
that price, among the prices that are lower than that price and that match up with the 
quotation price unit). (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

2. For the case of paragraph (4)2(b), the price specified in each of the following items: 

(a) Where the execution price is higher than the price specified in paragraph (3)1, but 
lower than the execution price of large-scale transaction errors: the execution price (if 
the prices does not match up with the quotation price unit, it shall be the price closest 
to that price, among the prices that are higher than that price and that match up with 
the quotation price unit); and (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(b) Where the execution price is equal to or higher than the execution price of large-
scale  transaction  errors:  the  execution  price  of  large-scale  transaction  errors  (if  the 
prices does not match up with the quotation price unit, it shall be the price closest to 
that price, among the prices that are lower than that price and that match up with the 
quotation price unit). (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(6) The counter party member who was notified of the receipt of the request for relief from 
the  Exchange  pursuant  to  [§35-3(5)]  shall,  if  there  are  customers  who  fall  under 
subparagraphs 2 and 3 or paragraph (4), notify them of the details of paragraph (4)1 on the 
date of request for relief. 

(7) In cases where the Exchange determines to relieve large-scale transaction errors resulted 
from customer account transactions, the member shall calculate the settlement prices for the 
customers by applying the settlement prices that were changed pursuant to paragraph (3) or 
(5). 

(8) Notwithstanding paragraphs (3) and (5), in the event that it is deemed necessary for the 
market  management  considering  the  trading  and  market  conditions  comprehensively,  the 
Exchange may change the prices specified in paragraphs (3) and (5). 

(9) The Exchange shall keep the records and documents related to the relief of large-scale 
transaction errors for ten (10) years. 

[June 21, 2016]
