CHAPTER V. RECEIVING OF TRADING ENTRUSTMENT   

§37-2. Order Types   

The  orders  under  [§33]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  classified  into  each  of  the  following 

93 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
types:  (Amended  on  June  28,  2005;  December  23,  2005;  February  3,  2009;  March  19, 
2009; July 29, 2010; July 11, 2019) 

1. Limit order: An order specifying the issue, quantity, and price;   

2. Market order: An order specifying the issue and quantity, but not the price;   

2-2.  Limit-to-market-on-close  order:  A  limit  order  with  the  condition  that  it  would 
convert into a market order at the time when the price at market closing is determined 
by call auction in accordance with [§18(1)2] of the Regulation;   

3. Immediately executable limit order: An order specifying the issue and quantity, but 
intending to trade by deeming that the price is specified at the prices under [§2(2)];   

4. Best limit order: An order specifying the issue and quantity, but intending to trade by 
deeming that the price is specified at the prices under [§2(3)]; and   

5. Target order: The order specifying the issue and quantity but putting a condition to 
execute  the  order  at  specific  price  level  such  as  the  trading  volume  weighted  average 
price noted in [§19-3(1)] or [§21-2(1)] of the Regulation as the target.   

6.  Auction-based  block  trade  order:  The  order  specifying  the  issue  and  quantity  but 
intending to trade at the price noted in [§19-3] or [§21-2] of the Regulation.   

7. Mid-price order: An order specifying the issue and quantity, but intending to trade by 
deeming that the price is specified at a mid-price; and [February 27, 2025] 

8. Stop-limit order:  An  order specifying the issue and quantity,  but  intending to  trade 
when the stop price satisfies the conditions stipulated in paragraph (2)5. [February 27, 
2025] 

[May 16, 2005] 

§38. Opening of Accounts, etc.   

(1) “Facts stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§33(2)] of the Regulation shall mean the 
matters in each of the followings: (Amended on May 16, 2005; February 3, 2009; March 19, 
2009; November 23, 2023) 

1. Name or designation, the resident registration number and the identification number, 
taxpayer number, in the case of foreigners, the number identifying the real name such as 
the  number  of  foreigner  identification  means  (in  the  case  of  foreigners  treated  as 
citizens,  it  refers  to  the  passport  number,  business  registration  number,  or  taxpayer 

94 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
number); 

2. Address and telephone number;   

3. Password;   

4. In the case of non-member securities companies, type of account (customer account 
or own account);   

5. In the case of foreigners,   

(a) Nationality or permanent residency 

(b) Residence status in Korea 

(c) [Deleted on November 23, 2023]   

6. Investor classification code. Provided that, in the case of trading linked to the CFD, it 
is based on the investor who concluded the CFD; and   

7. In cases where a proxy has been designated, the name or title, the number such as the 
resident  registration  number  or  business  registration  number,  which  confirms  the  real 
name, the relationship with the customer, address, and the power of such proxy.   

(2) Investor classification code pursuant to paragraph (1)6 shall be each of the followings: 
(Amended on May 14, 2008; February 3, 2009; March 19, 2009; June 22, 2012) 

1. Financial investment companies: 1000   

2. Insurance companies: 2000   

3. Collective investment vehicle, etc.   

(a) Collective investment vehicle other than those noted in paragraph (2)3(b): 3000       

(b) Privately placed funds: 3100 

4. Banks (the collective investment assets of the collective investment schemes shall be 
classified under paragraph (3)): 4000   

5. Other financial institutions: 5000       

6. Pensions, funds, and cooperatives: 6000   

95 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
7.  The  Government,  local  governments,  international  organizations  and  public  service 
institutions: 7000   

7-2. Companies other than those noted in subparagraphs 1 through 7: 7100   

8. Individuals: 8000   

9. [Deleted on March 19, 2009] 

(3)  In cases  where  a  customer falls under  an investor classification code  other than those 
mentioned in paragraph (2) at the time of opening of a trading account, the member shall 
verify  such  fact  immediately,  and  maintain  a  written  record  of  such  fact.  (Amended  on 
February 3, 2009) 

§38-2. Terms and Conditions for High-speed Algorithmic Trades 

Pursuant  to  [§34(1)8(b)]  of  the  Regulation,  in  case  where  a  customer  of  a  member  is  a 
person who is required to registered as a high-speed algorithmic trader, the member shall 
include each of the following matters in the terms and conditions: 

    1.  The  customer  shall  identify  and  systemically  manage  risks  that  may  arise  from  the 

high-speed algorithmic trading;   

2. The customer shall prepare the procedures for developing and changing the electronic 
systems  including  an  ordering  system,  etc.  and  the  program  related  to  the  high-speed 
algorithmic trading, and shall comply with them when operating; 

    3.  The  customer  shall  cooperate  in  fulfilling  the  member’s  obligation  to  manage  high-
speed algorithmic traders, including checking the electronic system such as the ordering 
system, etc.; 

    4. The customer shall prepare an appropriate control and response system to effectively 
cope with accidents or system failures related to the high-speed algorithmic trading and 
to minimize damage therefrom; 

    5.  The  customer  shall  maintain  a  mutual  contact  system  with  members  to  respond 
promptly in  the event  of an emergency, such as  errors in  the electronic system  such as 
the ordering system, etc.; and 

    6. In the case where the customer who has conducted the high-speed algorithmic trading 
through  multiple  members  pursuant  to  [§52-6]  is  suspended  to  submit  the  orders  for 
high-speed  algorithmic  trading  pursuant  to  [§50-3(5)],  he/she  shall  notify  all  other 
members of the relevant fact and reason. 

96 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[December 21, 2022] 

§39. Notification Deadline of Agreement for Receiving of Trading Entrustment   

“Duration  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  mentioned  in  [§34(3)]  of  the  Regulation 
shall be five (5) trading days from the effective day of the relevant agreement. (Amended 
on May 16, 2005; February 3, 2009) 

§40. Matters to be recorded When Receiving Entrustment of Orders   

“Information  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§38]  of  the  Regulation  shall  mean 
the matters in each of the followings: (Amended on July 29, 2010; January 26, 2011; March 
25, 2013; June 12, 2013; September 13, 2013; June 24, 2014; December 1, 2014; July 11, 
2019; December 21, 2022; August 8, 2023) 

1. Issue name;   

2. In the case of handling an order, each of following classifications:   

(a) New order; 

(b) Correction of order already submitted; and 

(c) Cancellation of order already submitted. 

3. Classification of buy and sell;   

4. In the case of offer order, each of the following classifications;   

(a)  Order  to  carry  out  a  sale  falling  under  any  subparagraph  of  [§9-2(1)]  of  the 
Regulation;   

(b) Order to  carry out  a  covered short sale pursuant  to  [§9-2(2)]  of the Regulation; 
and   

(c) Any other offer orders.   

5. Quantity; 

6.  Price.  Provided  that  this  provision  shall  not  apply  to  the  market  order,  limit-to-
market-on-close order, target order, best limit order, target price order, mid-price order, 

97 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
order for auction-based block trade, order participating in off-hours closing price trade, 
and case of canceling the order already submitted. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

6-2. Stop price in the case of stop-limit order; [February 27, 2025] 

7. Time of order receipt; 

8. In the case of order types noted in [§37-2(1) through (8)], each of such classification; 
(Amended on February 27, 2025) 

9. In the case of market session, each of following classifications;   

(a) In the case of order submitted for trade other than those noted in subparagraphs 
9(b) through 9(d), following classifications: 

(i) Pre-hours session; 

(ii) Regular session; 

(iii) After-hours session (for the off-hours closing price trade); and   

(iv) After-hours session (for the off-hours periodic call trade) 

(b) In the case of order for block trading, the following classifications: 

(i) Pre-hours session; 

(ii) Regular session; and 

(iii) After-hours session. 

(c)  In  the  case  of  order  submitted  for  auction-based  block  trade,  the  following 
classifications:   

(i) Pre-hours session; and 

(ii) Regular session. 

(d) In the case of order submitted for basket trade, the following classifications:   

(i) Pre-hours session; 

(ii) Regular session; and 

98 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(iii) After-hours session. 

9-2. [Deleted on September 13, 2013] 

10.  In  the  case  of  order  for  trading  the  treasury  stocks,  each  of  the  following 
classifications: 

(a)  Trade  conducted  for  the  purpose  of  purchasing  the  stocks  to  be  distributed 
subsequent to the exercise of stock option; 

(b)  Trade  subsequent  to  entering  into  the  money  trust  contract  for  treasury  stocks; 
and 

(c) Trade carried out  for the purpose  other than those noted in  subparagraphs 10(a) 
and 10(b). 

11.  In  the  case  of  trading  method  of  treasury  stocks,  each  of  the  following 
classifications: 

(a) The methods subject to [§21(3)] of the Regulation; 

(b) The methods subject to both [§10(4)] and [§21(2)] of the Regulation; and 

(c) The methods other than subparagraphs 11(a) and 11(b). 

12.  In  the  case  of  an  order  related  to  arbitrage  trading,  each  of  the  following 
classifications:   

(a) Index arbitrage trading;   

(b) Sector index arbitrage trading; [January 15, 2026] 

(c) Stock arbitrage trading; 

(d) Non-arbitrage trading, while it is arbitrage trading collective investment securities 
of ETF collective investment vehicle;         

(e)  Trade  that  is  not  non-arbitrage  trading  while  it  is  arbitrage  trading  collective 
investment securities of ETF collective investment vehicle; 

(f) Non-arbitrage trading while it is arbitraging trading of ETNs; 

(g) Trade that is not non-arbitrage trading while it is arbitrage trading of ETNs;   

99 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(h) DR arbitrage trading; and 

(i) DRs of foreign stock arbitrage trading   

13.  In  the  case  of  an  order  for  trading  a  basket  of  stocks,  each  of  the  following 
classifications:   

(a) Non-arbitrage trading;   

(b)  Trading  a  basket  of  stocks  for  the  purpose  of  creating  collective  investment 
securities of ETF collective investment vehicles, which is non-arbitrage trading; and         

(c)  Trading  a  basket  of  stocks  for  the  purpose  of  creating  collective  investment 
securities of ETF collective investment vehicles, which is not non-arbitrage trading.   

13-2. [Deleted on July 11, 2019] 

14. Classification for cash transaction or margin transaction;   

14-2. In the case of trading linked to the CFD, such classification; 

15. In cases where the conditions such as the time of quotation are affixed on the order, 
such conditions;   

16. In cases where the validity of order is specified, such validity period; 

17. In cases of limit order, market order, immediately executable limit order, order for 
auction-based block trade and mid-price order, to which any of the following conditions 
is affixed, such conditions: (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(a) The condition specifying to execute the amount of quotation quantity that can be 
executed as soon as the quotation is placed, and to cancel any unexecuted quantity of 
the order; and   

(b)  The  condition  specifying  to  execute  the  order  if  its  entirety  can  be  executed  as 
soon as the quotation is placed, and to cancel the order if it cannot be executed in its 
entire quantity.   

    18.  Following  condition  in  the  case  of  limit  order,  best  limit  order,  and  immediately 

executable limit order: Self-match prevention condition pursuant to [§18-3]. 

    19. Specification of designated trading markets; and [February 27, 2025] 

    20.  In  cases  where  a  customer  receives  the  short  selling  registration  number,  the  short 

100 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
selling  registration  number  (limited  to  the  case  of  stocks  and  stocks  of  investment 
company for business development collective investment). [March 26, 2025] (Amended 
on March 16, 2026) 

(Wholly amended on May 19, 2009) 

§41. Methods of Receiving Order Entrustment   

(1) [Deleted on December 28, 2011] 

(2)  When  a  member  receives  an  order  through  the  methods  pursuant  to  [§39(1)1]  of  the 
Regulation,  it  shall  be  in  accordance  with  the  order  slip  that  the  customer  filled  out  the 
entrustment  details  pursuant  to  [§40]  and  signed  or  imprinted  his/her  seal  thereon. 
(Amended on February 3, 2009; December 28, 2011) 

(3)  When  a  member  receives  an  order  through  the  methods  pursuant  to  [§39(1)2]  of  the 
Regulation,  the  employee  of  the  member  company  who  receives  the  order  shall  confirm 
that the customer is the said person and prepare the order sip in accordance with any of the 
following methods. In such cases, the member may use such method as the tape-recording 
to prove the details of order. (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 28, 2011) 

1. The employee receiving the order shall write down the details of order specified in 
[§40] by hand on the order slip and sign or imprint his/her seal thereon; and (Amended 
on February 3, 2009) 

2. The employee receiving the order shall input the details of order specified in [§40] 
into the member computer system and sign or affix his/her personal seal on the printed 
copy of the order slip. In such cases, this provision shall not apply to the case where the 
details  of  orders,  etc.  are  electronically  kept  after  putting  signature  using  electronic 
device  (including  the  electronic  signature  and  any  other  means  equivalent  to  the 
electronic signature). (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 28, 2011) 

(4)  When  a  member  receives  an  order  through  the  method  noted  in  [§39(1)3]  of  the 
Regulation, such order shall be submitted using a system  satisfying each of the following 
requirements,  and such  member shall  enter into  a prior  agreement with  customers for the 
entrustment through the electronic communication means: (Amended on February 3, 2009; 
December 28, 2011; December 18, 2013; June 21, 2016) 

1. The member shall be able to confirm the system user;   

2. The member shall be able to confirm any of the following information that identifies 
the order input device of customer: 

101 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(a) IP & MAC address, in the case of using home trading system and internet;   

(b) Mobile phone number and the unique ID number of device, in the case of using 
personal mobile phone or wireless internet phone; 

(c) Unique ID number of unit, in the case of using exclusive stock order input device; 
and   

(d)  Other  information  through  which  the  customer’s  order  input  device  can  be 
identified.   

3.  The  customer  shall  be  able  to  verify  the  details  of  order  at  the  time  of  placing  the 
orders;   

4. In cases where a member refuses to accept an entrustment of customer, the record of 
refusal shall be kept;   

4-2.  When  a  customer  request  for,  the  member  shall  be  able  to  submit  cancellation 
quotations at once without delay as requested; 

5. The customer shall be able to inquire about the details of order and trade execution;   

6. The system shall be able to prevent the use by other than the authorized users; and   

7.  The  member  shall  be  able  to  record  and  maintain  the  records  of  data  processing, 
including the details of the orders and execution thereafter.   

§41-2. Publication of Order Placing Methods, etc. 

(1)  In  cases  where  a  member  establishes  the  details  about  order  placing  method,  etc. 
pursuant to [§39-2(4)] of the Regulation, the matters in the following subparagraphs shall 
be  included:  (Amended  on  June  12,  2013;  September  13,  2013;  February  28,  2014; 
December 21, 2022) 

1. With regard to method of accepting the order entrustment, the matters noted in each 
of the following items: 

(a) Originator of order;   

(b) Location where the order originated; 

(c) Order input device; 

102 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(d) Order transmitting device; and 

(e) Order receiving device. 

2. With regard to order processing method, the matters noted in each of the following 
items:   

(a)  Verification  method  of  order  suitability,  etc.  according  to  [§9(7)]  of  the 
Regulation and physical location of system used for verification; and         

(b) Session type specified in the Guideline on Connection, etc. to Member System.   

3. Conditions of use and user fees per method according to subparagraphs 1 and 2.   

4. In addition, the matters that the member deems necessary to explain the differences 
between the ordering methods.   

(2) When intending to introduce or change the order placing method, etc. pursuant to [§39-
2(4)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  member  shall  make  public  such  details  through  the  medium 
such  as  the  member’s  internet  homepage  and  notify  the  details  to  the  Exchange  without 
delay.   

[December 28, 2011] 

§42. Processing of Entrusted Order   

(1) “Manners stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§41(1)] of the Regulation shall refer 
to the receipt of orders in a sequential order while recording the exact time of receipt on the 
order slip or in the system in the case of receiving orders from a customer (including the 
correction  orders  and  cancellation  orders:  the  same  hereinafter)  according  to  the  methods 
noted in each subparagraph of [§39(1)] of the Regulation and the input of order details in a 
sequence  of  receipt  into  the  order  input  device  of  the  member  (hereinafter  referred  to  as 
“the  order  input  device”)  in  the  case  of  order  received  through  the  method  noted  in 
[§39(1)1  &  2]  of  the  Regulation.  (Amended  on  February  3,  2009;  October  19,  2010; 
December 28, 2011) 

(2) [Deleted on December 28, 2011] 

(3) When the order input device malfunctions, a member shall be able to process the orders 
using the emergency terminals. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(4) Pursuant to [§41(4)] of the Regulation, the members shall, in any of the following cases, 
post a notice about investment  risks using the electronic communication  means to inform 

103 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
the customers of such facts or urge the customer to take caution: (Amended on February 3, 
2009; April 20, 2012; September 21, 2020) 

1.  Where  posting  of  notice  is  deemed  necessary  for  the  protection  of  investors  or 
maintenance of orderliness in the market because there is a sign of abnormal trading or 
abnormality in trading (referred to as "the signs of abnormal trading, etc." hereinafter in 
this Article) of specific issues;   

2. Where the Exchange requests the members to send a notice of investment risk to the 
customers or urge the customer to take caution, because the signs of abnormal trading, 
etc. mentioned in paragraph (1) have been observed;   

3. Temporary overheated issue; and (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

4. Where a specific issue is designated as an issue scheduled to be delisted. 

§42-2. Handling of Trading Errors 

In cases where an error has occurred in the course of processing the order entrusted by the 
customer or inputting such order or quotation into the member system or KOSDAQ system, 
the member shall immediately take an action that is appropriate for the order entrusted. In 
such cases, the member may sell or purchase the relevant order.   

[December 29, 2009] 

§42-3. Recording and Retaining Details of Error Corrections 

In cases where the details of order and trade have to be corrected, the member shall record 
the correction details and reasons in the correction book and retain it.   

[December 29, 2009] 

§43. Reporting of Good Faith Deposit   

“In accordance with the stipulation in the Enforcement Rules” in [§42(3)] of the Regulation 
shall be the reporting within five (5) trading days from the day when the relevant guidelines 
for  collection  of  the  good  faith  deposit  became  effective.  (Amended  on  May  16,  2005; 
February 3, 2009)         

§43-2. Special Case for Collection of Good Faith Deposit   

104 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
“Case stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§42(6)2] of the Regulation shall mean the 
case where the number of delivery failure of sold securities is five (5) times or more by the 
settlement day for recent six (6) months and the case where the total shortage of settlement 
amount excesses KRW one (1) billion.   

[December 18, 2013] 

§43-3.  Separate  Management  of  Good  Faith  Deposits  and  Restrictions  on  Use  as 
Member Margins 

(1)  With  regard  to  “shall  manage  the  good  deposits  separately  from  their  own  assets”  in 
[§42(10)]  of  the  Regulation,  members  shall  state  the  cash  good  faith  deposits  separately 
from the customer deposits in accounting.   

(2) With regard to “shall not use the good faith deposits as member margins” in [§42(10)] 
of  the  Regulation,  members  shall  maintain  liquid  assets  over  the  liquid  liabilities  under 
[Annex 10] and [Attachment 1] of the Detailed Regulations of the Regulations on Financial 
Investment Business. 

(3) [Deleted on January 15, 2026] 

[September 19, 2017]

CHAPTER VI. MARKET MANAGEMENT 

§52. Publication of Expected Matching Prices, etc. during Call Auctions 

(1)  Pursuant  to  [§50(1)5]  of  the  Regulation,  the  Exchange  shall  publish  the  details  of 
quotation  information  specified  in  each  of  the  following  subparagraphs:  (Amended  on 
February 3, 2009; July 29, 2010) 

1.  During  the  quotation  receiving  hours  for  call  auction,  the  three  (3)  successive 
expected best quotation prices and quantities per bid and offer, respectively, including 
the  expected  matching  price,  expected  matching  quantity  and  expected  best  bid  and 
offer quotations and the quotation quantities at such prices;   

2. During the quotation receiving hours for continuous call auction, ten (10) successive 
best quotation prices per bid and offer, respectively, including the best expected bid and 
offer quotations, the quotation quantities at such prices and the aggregated quantity of 
such quotations; and   

      2-2.  During  the  quotation  receiving  hours  for  continuous  auction,  mid-price  and  the 
quantity of mid-price quotation. In this case, such price and quantity shall be announced 
separately  from  the price and quantity announced in  accordance with  subparagraph 2, 
but if the input of mid-price quotation is restricted, it shall not be announced. [February 
27, 2025] 

3. In cases where there is a quotation with unexecuted quantity on either bid or ask side 
during the quotation receiving hours for regular session auction-based block trade, the 

107 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
side where there is the quotation with unexecuted quantity.   

(2) The expected matching prices, etc. that are made public pursuant to paragraph (1) shall 
be calculated according to each of the following methods: (Amended on February 3, 2009; 
June 12, 2013; September 13, 2013; July 13, 2022) 

1. Expected matching price and expected matching quantity: Of the quotations received 
by the relevant time, the price and quantity of quotations that are expected to match in 
accordance with [§18(3) through (6)] of the Regulation; and   

2. Prices and quantities of three (3) successive expected best quotations, including the 
price  of  expected  best  quotation:  The  prices  of  three  (3)  successive  expected  best 
quotations,  including  the  price  of  expected  best  quotation  per  bid  and  offer,  and  the 
quantities  at  such  prices.  In  such  cases,  when  it  is  possible  to  establish  the  expected 
matching  price  pursuant  paragraph  (1),  it  shall  be  based  on  the  best  quotation  for  the 
case where such trade has been executed.   

3.Notwithstanding  subparagraphs  1  and  2,  the  Exchange  may  determine  the  calculation 
method  and  cycle  of  the  expected  execution  price,  etc.  differently  in  case  of  excessive 
quotations, system failure, and other cases that it deems necessary for market management. 
(3) The expected matching prices, etc. that are made public pursuant to paragraphs (1) and 
(2) shall be published during the quotation receiving hours for call auction. Provided that, 
during  the  quotation  receiving  hours  for  the  determination  of  opening  price,  it  shall  be 
made  public  after  twenty  (20)  minutes  has  elapsed  from  the  beginning  of  the  quotation 
receiving hours. (Amended on February 3, 2009; February 27, 2025) 

(4) [Deleted on February 28, 2014] 

(5) Pursuant  to  [§50(4)]  of the Regulation, the publication  of market  prices  related to  the 
trading  of  listed  issues  shall  be  disclosed  through  the  disclosure  medium.  (Amended  on 
February 3, 2009) 

(6)  Pursuant  to  [§50(4)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  Exchange  may  make  public  any  of  the 
following  subparagraphs  for  investors’  reference:  (Amended  on  December  23,  2005; 
August  16,  2007;  February  3,  2009;  July  29,  2010;  June  12,  2013;  September  13,  2013; 
June 24, 2014; June 21, 2016) 

1. [Deleted on August 16, 2007] 

2. The top twenty (20) issues in terms of daily turnover ratio;   

3. The issues traded by way of the regular session block trade or off-hours block trade;   

3-2. The issues traded by way of regular session auction-based block trade or off-hours 

108 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
auction-based block trade;   

3-3. The issues traded by way of regular session basket trade or off-hours basket trade;   

3-4. [Deleted on September 13, 2013] 

4.  The  treasury  stocks  traded  by  the  listed  companies  (including  trading  of  treasury 
stocks under trust contract);   

5. The matters to be disclosed with respect to net holding balance prescribed in Article 
180-3 of the Act; 

6.  Details  of  the  net  holding  balance  aggregated  by  issue,  which  was  reported  to  the 
Exchange pursuant to Article 180-2 of the Act; and 

7.  Additionally,  the  issues  that  the  Exchange  deems  them  useful  for  making  the 
investment decision.   

(7)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1),  when  it  is  deemed  necessary  for  the  market 
management,  the  Exchange  may  differently  determine  the  details  of  market  prices 
published. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

§52-2. Methods of Reporting of Accounts for Algorithmic Trades 

The  reporting  of  algorithmic  trading  accounts  by  members  pursuant  to  [§50-2(2)]  of  the 
Regulation shall be carried out by inputting a report prepared in accordance with [Annex: 
Form No. 19] into the KOSDAQ system via the member computer systems by 18:00 hours. 

[June 21, 2016] 

§52-3. Methods of requesting for Quotation Handling by Account, etc. 

(1) The request for quotation handling by account by members pursuant to [§50-2(3)] of the 
Regulation  shall  be  carried  out  by  the  way  of  entering  the  matters  noted  in  each  of  the 
following  subparagraphs  into  the  KOSDAQ  system  via  the  member  computer  systems  or 
the member securities terminals. 

1.  Algorithmic  trading  account  number  (limited  to  the  account  that  was  reported  as  an 
algorithmic trading account no later than the day before the date of request); 

2. Types and details of the quotation handling by account. In such cases, the details shall 
be classified as follows: 

109 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(a)  In  the  case  of  [§50-2(3)1]  of  the  Regulation:  Cancellation  of  all  quotations 
received in the regular session; and 

(b)  In  the  case  of  [§50-2(3)2]  of  the  Regulation:  Blocking  the  receipt  of  additional 
new  quotations,  correction  quotations  and  cancellation  quotations  (excluding 
cancellation quotations in the case of the off-hours session). 

3. Other matters that the Exchange deems necessary. 

(2)  The  Exchange  shall  perform  the  quotation  handling  by  account  after  verifying  the 
matters noted in each of the subparagraphs at the request of members pursuant to paragraph 
(1). 

(3) Any member who has requested for the quotation handling by account may request for 
the release from such handling from the time when ten (10) minutes have elapsed since the 
request  for  the  quotation  handling  by  account  by  the  methods  specified  in  paragraph  (1), 
and, in cases where the member does not request for the release, the Exchange may release 
the quotation handling by account at the closing time of off-hours sessions after the market 
close of the day. (Amended on February 28, 2017) 

(4)  Notwithstanding  paragraphs  (1)  and  (3),  the  Exchange  may,  in  the  case  of  system 
failures  and  other  cases  that  are  deemed  necessary  for  the  market  management,  refuse  a 
member’s  request  for  the  quotation  handling  by  account  or  request  for  release  from  such 
handling. 

(5) When a member has requested for the quotation handling by account, the member shall 
keep the records and materials related thereto, including the details of system failures, etc., 
for ten (10) years. 

[June 21, 2016] 

§52-4. Registration of High-speed Algorithmic Trader, etc. 

(1) Registration or reporting pursuant to [§50-3(1) and (2)] of the Regulation shall be made 
by  a  member’s  inputting  all  matters  in  each  of  the  following  subparagraphs  through 
member system. Provided that, in the case where  a member reports itself as  a high-speed 
algorithmic trader, matters in subparagraphs 1 and 4 shall be excluded: 

    1.  Matters  concerning  the  fulfilment  of  the  requirement  in  each  subparagraph  of  [§50-

3(1)] of the Regulation; 

110 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
    2. Information about a customer or member as information that can identify the subject 

of registration, such as mane or trade name; 

    3. Application for registration in accordance with [Annex Form 24]; 

    4. Confirmation on inspection of registration information, etc. in accordance with [Annex 

Form 25]; and 

    5. Other matters that the Exchange deems necessary. 

(2)  In  case  where  there  is  a  change  in  the  matters  registered  or  reported  pursuant  to 
paragraph  (1),  the  member  shall  input  the  changed  matter  through  the  member  securities 
terminal without delay.   

(3) The “requirements specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§50-3(1)3] of the Regulation 
shall refer to all of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  The customer shall have a management system such as an internal control 
organization and two (2) or more of professional personnel in order to efficiently manage 
risks  that  may  arise  from  high-speed  algorithmic  trading.  Provided  that,  with  regard  to 
the  risks  that  occurs  from  high-speed  algorithmic  trading,  any  of  the  following  items 
shall be deemed to meet the relevant requirement: 

        (a) When a member directly conducts risk management, and   

        (b)  Where  a  member  judges  that  the  customer  can  recognize,  evaluate,  monitor,  and 

control risks in a timely manner.   

2. Other matters that the Exchange deems necessary for market management, etc. 

(4) When a member registers or reports itself as a high-speed algorithmic trader pursuant to 
paragraph (1), the Exchange shall process it without delay. In such case, the Exchange may 
ask the member to supplement if there is a defect in the registration or report. 

(5) The Exchange shall issue a trader registration number that can be commonly used in the 
KOSPI market, KOSDAQ market, KONEX market, and derivatives market for each high-
speed  algorithmic  trader  who  has  completed  registration  and  reporting.  In  such  case,  the 
high-speed algorithmic trader can set the risk management number (referring to the two (2) 
digit number set by the high-speed algorithmic trader to distinguish the range for applying 
the  self-match  prevention  condition  pursuant  to  [§18-3]  and  the  mass  order  cancellation 
pursuant to [§18-4]; the same hereinafter) to the relevant registration number.   

(6) In the case of reporting a high-speed algorithmic trade account pursuant to [§50-3(3)] of 

111 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
the  Regulation,  a  member  shall  report  the  relevant  account  to  the  high-speed  algorithmic 
trade number through the member system. 

(7)  The  “case  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§50-3(5)3]  of  the  Regulation  shall 
refer to each of the following subparagraphs: 

    1.  Where  a  customer  takes  out  the  ordering  system  from  the  member  computer  center, 

etc.; or 

    2.  Where  the  Exchange  recognizes  that  it  is  necessary  for  investor  protection  or  the 

stability of trading order in the market and notifies it to the member. 

(8)  In  case  where  all  members  that  have  received  orders  from  a  high-speed  algorithmic 
trader  cease  to  receive  the  orders  pursuant  to  [§50-3(3)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  Exchange 
may cancel the registration of the high-speed algorithmic trader of the relevant customer. 

[December 21, 2022] 

§52-5. Special Cases for Registration of High-speed Algorithmic Trader 

(1)  In  the  case  where  the  registration  or  reporting  of  a  high-speed  algorithmic  trader  is 
completed  in  accordance  with  any  of  the  regulations  of  the  KOSDAQ  market,  KONEX 
market, or derivatives market operated by the Exchange, the registration and reporting are 
also deemed to have been completed in the KOSDAQ market. 

(2)  In  the  case  where  multiple  customers  of  a  member  satisfy  all  of  the  following 
subparagraphs, the member can collectively register them as high-speed algorithmic traders. 
In such case, the Exchange may issue a single trader registration number that can be jointly 
used by the relevant customers to a specific customer: 

1.  The  customer  shall  be  an  affiliated  corporation  (including  a  foreign  corporation 

incorporated under foreign laws and regulations) of a specific customer; 

2.  The customer and the affiliated corporation shall use the same trade ordering system; 

and 

3. The member shall verify whether the registration requirements stated in [§104-3(1)] of 
the Regulation are met for all of the multiple customers. 

[December 22, 2022] 

112 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§52-6. High-speed Algorithmic Trading through Multiple Members 

In case where a member intends to receiver orders for high-speed algorithmic trading from 
a  customer  who  has  completed  the  registration  as  a  high-speed  algorithmic  trader,  the 
member  shall  apply  for  the  right  to  use  the  trader  registration  number  of  the  relevant 
customer to the Exchange. In such case, the latter part of [§50-3(1)] of the Regulation and 
[§52-4(1) (excluding subparagraph 3) through (4)] of these Enforcement Rules shall apply 
mutatis mutandis to the relevant application.   

[December 21, 2022] 

§52-7. Member’s Obligation to Manage High-speed Algorithmic Trading 

(1) Pursuant  to  [§50-4(1)] of the Regulation, a  member shall inspect  electronic system  in 
order  to  verify  whether  the  electronic  systems  including  ordering  system,  etc.  used  by  a 
customer has sufficient stability and adequacy to carry out high-speed algorithmic trading 
as specified in each of the following subparagraphs: 

    1.  Matters  concerning  inspection  of  electronic  system,  etc.  related  to  the  registration 
stated in [§50-3] of the Regulation; A member shall prepare the standards and procedures 
for  electronic  system  inspection,  conduct  the  inspection  of  the  electronic  system 
thoroughly through the linkage tests with trade ordering system by the customer before 
applying for the registration, and file the results with the Exchange; 

    2. Matters concerning regular inspection: A member shall inspect the connection with the 
customer’s electronic system on a regular basis every year. Provided that, if the member 
conducted the inspection on a timely basis due to  the change of  electronic system,  etc. 
during  the  relevant  year,  it  shall  be  deemed  that  the  inspection  pursuant  to  the  main 
clause is completed and   

    3.  Other  matters  that  the  Exchange  deems  necessary  for  the  stable  operation  of  the 

electronic system, etc. 

(2) Pursuant to [§50-4(1)] of the Regulation, a member shall establish appropriate internal 
control  mechanism for the management of  risks and the prevention of  financial accidents 
related to the high-speed algorithmic trading of customers as specified in each of following 
subparagraphs: 

    1. Matters concerning the granting of order limits: A member shall grant an appropriate 
order limit by evaluating the financial stability, credit rating, etc. and check the adequacy 
of the relevant limit on the regular basis; 

    2. Matters concerning the monitoring of trades: A member shall monitor and supervise 

113 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
whether  a  customer  complies  with  relevant  regulations  and  internal  control  standards 
through the monitoring of high-speed algorithmic trading; and 

    3.  Matters  concerning  the  response  to  accidents  and  failures:  A  member  shall  prepare 
appropriate  control  and  response  system  including  manuals  to  effectively  cope  with 
accidents or failures related to high-speed algorithmic trading of customers and minimize 
damage.   

(3)  With  respect  to  the  request  for  submitting  materials  pursuant  to  [§50-4(2)]  of  the 
Regulation, A member shall record and maintain the following materials for ten (10) years 
and submit them if the Exchange requests for the market management, etc. 

    1. Materials on the registration of high-speed algorithmic traders and their trades; and 

    2.  Results  of  inspection  and  supervision  conducted  pursuant  to  paragraphs  (1)  and  (2) 

and related materials. 

[December 21, 2022] 

§53. Date of Action for Ex-dividends, etc.   

(1) The date of action for ex-dividends, ex-rights or ex-distribution, etc. pursuant to [§51] 
of the Regulation shall be each of the following dates: (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

1. It shall be, except the cases mentioned in subparagraph 2, the day before the record 
date. Provided that, if the record date is a market holiday or in the middle of the closing 
period  of  the  shareholder  register,  the  record  date  shall  be  deemed  the  trading  day 
immediately preceding  the first  day of market  holidays or the commencement  date of 
closing of the shareholder register; and   

2.  It  shall be the day on which trading  halt is  called  off if the record date falls in  the 
middle of the trading halt (excluding the first day of trading halt).   

(2)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1),  when  it  is  deemed  necessary  for  the  market 
management,  the  Exchange  may  determine  the  action  date  differently.  (Amended  on 
February 3, 2009) 

§54. [Deleted on August 16, 2007]   

§55. [Deleted on August 16, 2007] 

114 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§56. Public Opinion Gathering   

Public opinion gathering pursuant to [§55-2] of the Regulation shall be governed by the 
provisions of [§5] of the Internal Regulations Management Regulation and [§6] of the 
Regulations Management Regulation. 

ADDENDA 
(January 24, 2005)   

§1. Effective Date   

These  Enforcement  Rules  shall  become  effective  on  the  date  when  the  Exchange  is 
incorporated.  Provided  that  [§19]  through  [§22]  shall  become  effective  on  the  date  when 
the Exchange determines.   

§2. Abolition of Previous Enforcement Rules and Interim Measures Thereafter 

Beginning with the date when these Enforcement Rules became effective, the Enforcement 
Rules of the Regulation on KOSDAQ Market Business of the KSDA shall be abolished on 
the  date  when  these  Enforcement  Rules  became  effective.  Provided  that  the  relevant 
provisions  of  the  Enforcement  Rules  of  the  Regulation  on  KOSDAQ  Market  Business  of 
the KSDA shall apply to the call auction until the effective date of provisions specified in 
the proviso of [§1] of Addendum.   

§3. Interim Measures for Trading, etc.   

The  trading,  suspension  of  trading,  trade  settlement,  etc.  conducted  and  implemented 
pursuant to the Regulation on KOSDAQ Market Business of the KSDA before the effective 
date  of  these  Enforcement  Rules  shall  be  construed  as  those  conducted  pursuant  to  these 
Enforcement Rules.   

§4. Interim Measures for Opening the Trading Account, etc.   

Opening of trading account, notification of the guidelines for collection of customer margin, 
designation of substitute securities  and calculation of substitute price, etc. pursuant  to  the 
Regulation on KOSDAQ Market Business of the KSDA before the effective date of these 
Enforcement Rules shall be construed as those accomplished pursuant to these Enforcement 
Rules.   

§5. Interim Measures for Agreement on Use of Market Information   

The agreement for the use  of market  information, which  was entered into pursuant  to  the 
Regulation on KOSDAQ Market Business of the KSDA before the effective date of these 

115 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Enforcement Rules, shall be construed as those entered into pursuant to these Enforcement 
Rules.   

§6.  Example  of  Application  to  the  Stocks  of  Securities  Investment  Companies  and 
Beneficiary Certificates of Securities Investment Trust Companies   

In  applying  these  Enforcement  Rules,  the  stocks  of  securities  investment  companies  and 
beneficiary certificates  of securities investment  trust  companies that were issued pursuant 
to  the  abolished  Securities  Investment  Company  Act  and  the  Securities  Investment  Trust 
Business  Act  shall  be  construed  as  those  issued  pursuant  to  the  Act  on  Business  of 
Operating Indirect Investment Assets.   

§7. Interim Measures for Surveillance Issues   

The issues designated as surveillance issue, before the effective date of these Enforcement 
Rules,  pursuant  to  the  Regulation  on  KOSDAQ  Market  Business  of  the  KSDA  shall  be 
construed as the issues designated as abnormally rising issue pursuant to these Enforcement 
Rules.   

ADDENDA 
  (March 25, 2005)   

§1. Effective Date   

These Enforcement Rules shall become effective on March 28, 2005.   

§2. Interim Measures for Designation as Abnormally Rising Issues   

In the case of the issues that fell under the criteria for the designation as abnormally rising 
issue pursuant to the provisions before the effective date of these Enforcement Rules shall 
be construed that they came under the criteria for the designation as abnormally rising issue 
pursuant to these Enforcement Rules.

  (October 14, 2005)   

§1. Effective Date   

These Enforcement Rules shall become effective on November 7, 2005.   

§2. Interim Measures for Guidelines for Calculation of Base Price for the First Trading   

Listed shares for which the base price has not yet been established at the time of effective 
date of these Enforcement Rules shall be construed that they are listed on the effective date 
of these Enforcement Rules. In such cases, in the case of the issues for which the trading 
has  been  suspended,  it  shall  be  construed  that  they  are  listed  on  the  day  the  trading  is 
resumed.   

§3. Interim Measures for Program Trading   

The trade that falls under the program trading pursuant to the previous Enforcement Rules 
shall  be  construed  as  the  program  trading,  even  after  these  Enforcement  Rules  became 
effective, until the futures or options contracts pursuant to the previous Enforcement Rules 
are delisted.

§1. Effective Date

separately. 

(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), the amended provisions of [§10] shall become effective 
on  the  enforcement  date  of  the  amended  provisions  on  the  price  range  for  placing  bids 
specified  in  [§5-5(1)1(a)&(b)]  of  the  Regulation  on  Issuance,  Public  Disclosure,  etc.  of 
Securities of the Financial Services Commission. 

§2. Enforcement Date, etc. of the KOSDAQ Market Business Regulation 

“The date specified by the Enforcement Rules” in Addenda of KOSDAQ Market Business 
Regulation  (amended  on  April  29,  2015)  shall  refer  to  the  enforcement  date  pursuant  to 
[§1(1)] of the Addenda.  Provided that the enforcement date of the amended provisions of 
[§10]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Business  Regulation  (amended  on  April  29,  2015)  shall 
refer to the enforcement date falling under [§1(2)] of the Addenda. 

§3. Exception to Applying Provisions on Designation as Substitute Securities       

The  amended  provisions  of  [§44]  shall  apply  to  the  issue  that  was  designated  as  an 
investment alert issue first since its enforcement date.

§3. Exceptions in Applying Provisions on Designation of Temporary Overheated Issues, 
etc. 

(1)  Notwithstanding  [§23-2(1)2]  of  the  former  version  of  the  Regulation,  the  issues  that 
were requested to be suspended from trading by the Market Oversight Commission on the 
trading day immediately preceding the enforcement date specified in [§2] of this Addenda 
shall not be designated as temporary overheated issues. 

(2) The amended provisions of [§28-4] shall apply starting with the temporary overheated 
issue that is designated first after the enforcement date of these Enforcement Rules.

For  the  issues  that  were  designated  as  temporary  overheated  issues  as  of  the  trading  day 
immediately  preceding  the  enforcement  date  specified  in  [§2]  of  this  Addenda,  the 
suspension of trading pursuant to [§25(1)5-2] of the former version of the Regulation may 
not apply.

ADDENDA 
(March 25, 2016) 

§1. Effective Date 

These  Enforcement  Rules  shall  become  effective  on  March  28,  2016.  Provided  that  the 
amended provisions of [§28-5], [§28-7] and [§3 of Annex 5] shall become effective on the 
date determined by the Exchange separately by taking into consideration the time required 
to develop computer system, etc. 

§2. Effective Date of the KOSDAQ Market Business Regulation, etc. 

The  “date  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  Addenda  of  the  Regulation  (No.1247, 
amended on November 4, 2015) shall refer to the date specified in each of the followings: 

132 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. For the amended provisions of [§9-3] and [§12-7] through [§12-9] of the Regulation, 
March 28, 2016; and 

2.  For  the  amended  provisions  of  [§23-4]  of  the  Regulation,  the  effective  date  as 
stipulated in the proviso to [§1] of this Addenda. 

§3. Exception to the Term of Market Making Agreement 

Notwithstanding the amended provisions of [§12-14(3)], the effective period of the market 
making  agreement  that  is  entered  into  for  the  first  time  after  the  effective  date  of  these 
Enforcement  Rules  shall  be  the  period  from  the  effective  date  noted  in  the  main  body  of 
[§1] of this Addenda to the last trading day of the year to which the effective date belongs. 

§4. Interim Measures related to Market Makers 

Based  on  the  effective  date  of  these  Enforcement  Rules,  selection  of  issues  for  market 
making,  reception  of  applications  for  market  makers,  conclusion  of  market  making 
agreements  and  other  actions  taken  by  the  Exchange  beforehand  with  respect  to  market 
makers for the purpose of implementation of the market maker system shall be deemed to 
have been conducted in accordance with the amended provisions. 

§5. Exception to the Effective Period of Low Liquidity Issue subject to Call Auction 

Notwithstanding the amended provision of [§3 of Annex 5], the effective period of the low 
liquidity issue subject to call auction that was selected for the first time after the effective 
date of this Enforcement shall be the period from the effective date noted in the proviso to 
[§1] of this Addenda to the last trading day of the year to which the effective date belongs. 

§6.  Interim  Measures  related  to  the  Selection  of  Low  Liquidity  Issue  subject  to  Call 
Auction, etc. 

Notwithstanding the effective dates noted in the proviso to [§1] and [§2(2)] of this Addenda, 
selection of low  liquidity  issues for call  auction  and other actions taken  by the Exchange 
beforehand for the purpose of changing the trading method of the low liquidity issues into 
the call auction shall be deemed to have been conducted in accordance with the amended 
provisions.

§3. Exceptions in Applying Provisions on Assessment of Liquidity of SPACs 

In applying the amended provisions of [Annex 5], in the case of a stock issued by a SPAC 
that is applied with the call auction as having been designated  as the low liquidity issue 
subject to call auction pursuant to the previous version of these Enforcement Rules when 
these Enforcement Rules is put into effect, the relevant stock shall be released from such 
designation on the effective date of these Enforcement Rules and the call auction shall not 
apply thereto.

ADDENDA 
(September 19, 2017 / Regulation No. 1490) 

§1. Effective Date 

These Enforcement Rules shall become effective on September 25, 2017.   

§2. Exemptions to the Timing for Calculating and Applying Assessment Rates 

Notwithstanding  the  amended  provisions  of  [§47(4)],  [§47-3(1)]  and  [§47-4]  of  these 
Enforcement  Rules,  the  assessment  rates  of  the  quarter  in  which  the  effective  date  falls 

135 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
shall be calculated on the day preceding  the  effective  date and  applied from  the effective 
date to the end of the quarter following the quarter in which the effective date falls. 

§3.  Exceptions  concerning  Invalidation  of  Substitute  Securities  Ineligible  for  Member 
Margins 

Notwithstanding  the  amended  provisions  of  [§35-36(1)]  of  these  Enforcement  Rules,  the 
substitute prices for the substitute securities ineligible for member margin shall be adjusted 
as follows:   

1. The adjustment rate shall be 25% from the effective date of these Enforcement Rules 
to September 24, 2018; and   

2. The adjustment rate shall be 50% from September 25, 2018 to September 24, 2019. 

§4. Exceptions concerning Deposit Limits per Issue of Substitute Securities 

Notwithstanding  the  amended  provisions  of  [§35-37(1)]  of  these  Enforcement  Rules,  the 
rates  applied  for  calculation  of  deposit  limits  per  issue  of  substitute  securities  shall  be  as 
follows:   

1. In the case of subparagraph 1 of [§35-37(1)]: 100/100 from the effective date of these 
Enforcement  Rules  to  September  24,  2018;  and  75/100  from  September  25,  2018  to 
September 24, 2019. Provided that, in the case of a security falling under subparagraph 
1(b) of [§44-2], it shall be 200/100 and 150/100, respectively; and   

2. In the case of subparagraphs 3 and 4 of [§35-37(1)]: 20/100 from the effective date of 
these Enforcement Rules to September 24, 2018; and 15/100 from September 25, 2018 to 
September 24, 2019.

142 

 
 
 
 
 
   
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
selected  as  a  different  classes  of  stock  subject  to  call  auction  from  the  Effective  Date  of 
these  Enforcement  Rules  to  the  end  of  the  next  quarter.  In  this  case,  it  is  deemed  that 
September 25, 2020 is the date of the evaluation of the listed stocks on the last transaction 
date of the quarter where the Effective Date of these Enforcement Rules belongs.

(Regulation No. 2000 / November 25, 2021) 

§1. Effective Date   

These Enforcement Rules shall become effective on November 29, 2021. Provided that, the 
amended  provisions  of  paragraphs  2  and  3  under  [Annex  6]  shall  apply  from  January  3, 
2022.

149 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex  1]  Guidelines  for  Calculation  of  Lowest  and  Highest  Quotation  Prices  for 
Determining First Trading Price of Issue Using First Price as Base Price 
(Amended on June 28, 2005; October 14, 2005; August 16, 2007; December 4, 2007; February 3, 2009; July 31, 2009; 
July 29, 2010; Total revision on December 30, 2010; April 20, 2012; March 25, 2013; May 23, 2014; June 16, 2014; 
September 30, 2014; April 22, 2016; December 27, 2018; October 27, 2021; April 12, 2023; February 27, 2025) 

Guidelines for Calculation of Lowest and Highest Quotation Prices for   
Determining First Trading Price of Issue Using First Trading Price as Base Price 
(Pertaining to [§8], [§17], [§20], [§27], and [§48] of the Enforcement Rules) 

1. The lowest and highest quotation prices used for the determination of first trading price 
of the issue  using the first  trading  price as a base price  shall be the prices (the amount 
less  than  KRW  1  shall  be  rounded  down  and  if  the  prices  do  not  match  the  quotation 
price  unit,  each  price  shall  be  the  closest  prices  to  those  prices  among  prices  that  are 
higher than those prices and that match the quotation price units; the same    hereinafter) 
calculated  by  multiplying  the  appraisal  price  (the  amount  less  than  KRW  1  shall  be 
rounded down and if the price does not match the quotation price unit, the price shall be 
the closest price to that price among prices that are higher than that price and that match 
the quotation price units: the same hereinafter) by the applicable ratio noted in paragraph 
(3), except for the cases defined otherwise: 

2. The appraisal price noted in paragraph (1) shall be each of the following subparagraphs. 
In  such  cases,  when  the  company  subject  to  preparation  of  consolidated  financial 
statement pursuant to the Act on External Audit of Stock Companies shall be based on 
the consolidated financial statement and audit report thereon, and for issues falling under 
at least two (2) among issues using the first trading price as the base price, the appraisal 
prices are calculated by applying the relevant calculation method in consecutive order on 
the basis of respective effective date. 

A. Re-listed issues and issues with listing change (including a class of stocks) 

(1)  Case  where  stocks  of  the  corporations  established  subsequent  to  a  split-off  or  a 
merger  after  split-off  of  listed  corporations  are  re-listed  and  the  listing  status  of 
stocks of the surviving corporations is changed 

(a) In cases where the net asset amount [net asset amount is calculated by adding the 
amount of treasury stocks to the total capital (excluding non-controlling interests), 
and  in  the  case  of  issues  with  listing  change,  the  net  asset  amount  stated  in  the 
statement  of  financial  position  made  public  recently  may  be  used  and  the 
statement  of  financial  position  used  for  the  first  listed  issue  between  a  re-listed 
issue and an issue with listing change shall also be used for the issue listed later: 
the same hereinafter in this  paragraph] of re-listed issues and issues with listing 

150 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
change as of the date of listing application is “positive”, the price determined by 
issue  according  to  the  following  method.  In  such  cases,  as  a  case  where  new 
stocks are delivered to a specific person before the listing date (if the listing date 
is the day of trading suspension, it shall be the day when the suspension is lifted; 
the  same  hereinafter  in  paragraphs  2A  and  2B  as  a  result  of  paid-in  capital 
increase by way of the third party allotment, merger, stock swap or business/asset 
takeover  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “paid-in  capital  increase  by  way  of  the 
third party allotment, etc.), if the number of stocks issued at the issuing price less 
than  50/100  of  the  appraisal  price  exceeds  the  number  of  stocks  before  the 
relevant  paid-in  capital  increase  by  way  of  the  third  party  allotment,  etc.,  the 
lowest price among the quotation price units shall be the lowest quotation price.     

1) Appraisal price at the time of split-off = (Sum of market capitalization per class 
of stocks on the last trading day of company before split-off x Net asset split-
off ratio) / Sum of shares per class of stocks after split-off 

2)  Appraisal  price  at  the  time  of  merger  after  split-off  =  (Sum  of  market 
capitalization  per  class  of  stocks  on  the  last  trading  day  of  company  before 
merger  after  split-off  x  Net  asset  split-off  ratio)  /  Sum  of  shares  per  class  of 
stocks after merger after split-off 

3) The net asset split-off ratio noted in 1) and 2) shall refer to the split-off ratio of 
net  asset  value  of  a  company  before  the  split-off  stated  in  the  report  on 
completion of split-off or the post-issuance report submitted with respect to the 
split-off or merger after split-off. Provided that, if it has been confirmed that the 
net asset values of re-listed issue and issue with listing change as of the date of 
listing application are different from those stated in the report on completion of 
split-off  or  the  post-issuance  report  submitted  with  respect  to  the  split-off  or 
merger after split-off according to the balance sheet in the CPA audit report (or 
review), the net asset split-off ratio may be determined differently.   

4) In cases where the number of companies before merger after split-off is two (2) 
or more, “(Total market capitalization per class of stocks on the last trading day 
of company before merger after split-off x Net asset split-off ratio)” noted in (b) 
above shall be determined by adding the amount calculated per company before 
merger after split-off. 

(b) In cases where the net asset value of issue with listing change as of the date of 
listing application is not ‘positive’, the price per issue determined according to 
following method   

1) Case of issues with listing change 

151 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
The lowest quotation price shall be the lowest price among the quotation price 
units  and  the  highest  quotation  price  shall  be  the  closing  price  (if  there  is  no 
closing price, it shall be the base price: the same hereinafter in paragraph 3) on 
the last trading day before spit-off.   

2) Case of re-listed issues 

i) If the net asset value is ‘positive’, the net asset value per share. In such cases, 
the latter part of the part other than provisions  of subitems (a)1) through 4) 
above shall apply mutatis mutandis. 

ii) If the net asset value is not ‘positive’, the lowest quotation price shall be the 
lowest price among the quotation price units and the highest quotation price 
unit shall be the amount (the amount less than KRW 1 shall be rounded down 
and if the prices do not match the quotation price unit, each price shall be the 
closest prices to those price among prices that are higher than those price and 
that  match  the  quotation  price  units)  determined  by  dividing  the  market 
capitalization of company before split-off per class on the last trading day by 
the number of shares per class of newly established company. In such cases, 
in  cases  where  the  stocks  of  which  the  class  is  different  from  the  class  of 
company before split-off is allotted to the new company, the calculation shall 
take such factor into consideration. 

(2)  Case  of  re-listing  the  new  company  established  subsequent  to  the  merger  of 

listed companies 

The  price  calculated  by  dividing  the  sum  of  market  capitalizations  per  class  of 
stocks on the last trading day of the companies before merger by the number of 
shares per class of stocks of the company after merger.   

B. Issues undergone paid-in capital reduction 

(1) Case of capital reduction without consideration 

The amount (in the case where stock splits or ex-rights occurred before the listing, 
the amount shall be determined by taking into account such factor) determined by 
multiplying  the  merger  or  write-down  ratio  applicable  to  the  minority 
shareholders by the closing price on the last trading day before the reverse stock 
split  or  write-down.  In  such  cases,  if  the  new  stocks  are  delivered  to  a  specific 
person as a result of the paid-in capital increase by way of third party allotment, 
etc.  conducted  before  the  listing  date  and  if  the  number  of  stocks  issued  at  the 
price less than 50/100 of the issue price exceeds the number of stocks excluding 
the number of stocks before the relevant paid-in capital increase by way of third 

152 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
party allotment, etc., the lowest price among the quotation price units shall be the 
lowest quotation price.     

(2) Case of reduction of capital stock by payment in cash 

The  price  determined  according  to  the  following  formula.  In  such  cases,  if  the 
amount  obtained  by  multiplying  150/100  by  the  amount  pursuant  to  following 
formula is less than the closing price (in the case where stock splits or ex-rights 
occur before the listing, it shall be the amount determined by taking into account 
such factor: the same hereinafter in this item) on the last trading day before the 
trade  suspension,  the  relevant  closing  price  shall  be  the  highest  quotation  price 
and if, as a case where subsequent to the paid-in capital increase by way of third 
party allotment, etc., the new stocks are delivered to a specific person before the 
listing date, the number of stocks issued at the issuing price less than 50/100 of 
appraisal  price exceeds the number of stocks before  the relevant paid-in  capital 
increase  by  way  of  third  party  allotment,  etc.,  the  lowest  price  among  the 
quotation price units shall be the lowest quotation price, and the amount pursuant 
to the following formula is not ‘positive’, the lowest quotation price shall be the 
lowest price among the quotation price units and the highest quotation price shall 
be the closing price of the last trading before trade suspension.   

(a) Appraisal price = [(Closing price on the last trading day before paid-in capital 
reduction  x  Number  of  shares  before  paid-in  capital  reduction)  –  (Payment 
amount per share x Number of shares reduced)] / Number of shares after paid-
in capital reduction 

(b) In calculating the appraisal price noted in  (i), if the stock split, reverse stock 
split,  or  ex-rights  occurs  before  the  listing,  such  factor  shall  be  taken  into 
consideration, and ‘payment per share’ shall refers to the amount paid for one 
(1) share to minority shareholders and ‘number of shares reduced’ shall refer 
to the number of shares reduced for all shareholders. 

(3)  Notwithstanding  the  provisions  of  items  (a)  and  (b)  and  subparagraph  (3),  in 
cases where new stocks are delivered to a specific person as a result of a paid-in 
capital  increase  by  way  of  the  third  party  allocation,  etc.  conducted  before  the 
date  of  listing  (referring  to  the  date  of  supplementary  listing  as  a  result  of  the 
paid-in capital increase by way of the third party allocation, etc. and the date of 
listing change due to the capital reduction, and including the date of release from 
trading  suspension  in  the  case  of  an  issue  under  trading  suspension;  the  same 
hereinafter in this item) and after the capital reduction, and the number of stocks 
issued at the price less than 20% of the appraisal price stipulated in item (1) or 
(2) exceeds the number of stocks before the aforesaid paid-in capital increase by 
way  of  third  party  allocation,  etc.,  the  appraisal  prices  shall  be  as  follows.  In 
such  cases,  the  appraisal  price  shall  be  calculated  on  the  date  of  listing 

153 

 
 
 
 
 
 
concerned,  and  the  lowest  price  among  the  quotation  price  units  shall  be  the 
minimum  quotation  price,  and  when  calculating  the  maximum  quotation  price, 
the applicable ratio shall be 300%. 

(a)  In  the  case  of  capital  reduction  without  consideration:  the  price  obtained 

through weighted calculation by the following formula 

 Appraisal price = [(Closing price of the last trading day before the capital 
reduction    Number  of  stocks  before  the  capital  reduction)  +  Sum  of 
issuance amounts of new stocks resulting from the paid-in capital increase 
by  way  of  third-party  allocation,  etc.]  /  Number  of  stocks  on  the  date  of 
listing concerned 

(b)  In  the  case  of  capital  reduction  with  consideration:  the  price  calculated 
through weighted calculation by the following formula. In such cases, if the 
price calculated by multiplying the following appraisal price by 300/100 is 
lower  than  the  closing  price  of  the  last  trading  day  before  the  capital 
reduction, the closing price of previous day shall be the maximum quotation 
price,  and  if  the  appraisal  price  is  not  “positive”,  the  closing  price  of 
previous day shall be the maximum quotation price. 

 Appraisal price = [(Closing price of the last trading day before the capital 
reduction    Number  of  stocks  before  the  capital  reduction)  +  Sum  of 
issuance amounts of new stocks resulting from the capital increase by way 
of  third-party  allocation,  etc.  –  Sum  of  payments  to  the  shareholders  for 
capital reduction] / Number of stocks on the date of listing concerned 

        (c) In calculating the appraisal price in (a) and (b) above, if there has been stock 
split, reverse stock split, or ex-rights occurs before the date of listing, it shall 
be calculated by taking into account such factor.   

C. In the case of issues resuming trading after halt or suspension for at least thirty (30) 
trading  days,  appraisal  price  shall  be  the  closing  price  of  the  last  trading  day. 
Provided  that,  in  the  case  where  there  has  been  stock  split,  ex-rights,  etc.  occurs 
before  the  resumption  of  trading,  it  shall  be  calculated  by  taking  into  account  such 
factor  and  the  latter  part  of  the  part  other  than  items  (1)(a)1)  through  4)  of 
subparagraph A above shall apply mutatis mutandis (if only the capital increase with 
consideration by way of the third-party allocation occurs, the listing date in the latter 
part shall be deemed as the release date from the trading suspension).   

3. The applicable rate shall be as follows. In such cases, in applying paragraphs 1 and 2, the 
lowest applicable rate among the relevant applicable rates shall be applied to the issues 

154 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
falling under both of them.   

A. Applicable rate for the calculation of the lowest quotation price: 50% 

B. Applicable rate for the calculation of highest quotation price 

(1) In the case of issues undergone capital reduction or ETNs undergone a split or a 

reverse split: 150% 

      (2) Other issues: 200% 

4.  In  cases  where  it  is  deemed  that  the  appraisal  price,  the  lowest  quotation  price,  or  the 
highest quotation price calculated pursuant to paragraphs (1) through (3) are significantly 
unreasonable or it is difficult to apply them, the Exchange may set them differently. 

155 

 
       
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex  1-2]  Guidelines  for  Calculation  of  the  Base  Price  for  the  Date  of  Quotation 
Placement for the Calculation of Quotation Quantity Limits 
[September 12, 2018] 

Guidelines for Calculation of the Base Price for the Date of Quotation Placement for 
the Calculation of Quotation Quantity Limits 
(Pertaining to [§8(4)] of the Enforcement Rules) 

(1)  For  the  issues  other  than  those  under  paragraphs  (2)  through  (4);  the  base  prices 

calculated in accordance with [§17]. 

(2)  For  the  issues  using  the  first  trading  price  as  the  base  price;  the  appraisal  prices 

determined in [Annex 1]. 

(3)  For the issues scheduled to be delisted; the closing price on the date the transaction was 
last made. Provided that, in cases where an issue scheduled to be delisted has undergone 
ex-dividends, ex-rights, stock split or reverse stock split, the price shall be calculated by 
taking such event into account.   

(4)  For subscription warrants and subscription right certificates; the closing price on the date 
the transaction was last made. Provided that, in cases where there is not the closing price 
on  the  date  the  transaction  was  last  made,  it  shall  be  the  price  under  each  of  the 
following subparagraphs: 

1.  For subscription warrants; the price calculated by deducting the exercise price from 
the  base  price  for  the  date  of  quotation  placement  of  the  stocks  of  the  company 
issuing  the  relevant  warrants  under  [§16-2]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Listing 
Regulation. Provided that, if the price calculated is not positive, the base price for the 
date  of  quotation  placement  shall  not  be  calculated.  In  such  cases,  the  quotation 
quantity  limits  noted  in  [§8(4)]  shall  apply  with  the  quantity  determined  in 
subparagraph  4  of  the  same  paragraph.  The  same  shall  apply  hereinafter  to 
subscription right certificates. 

2.  For  subscription  right  certificates;  the  price  calculated  by  subtracting  the  issuing 
price  from  the  base  price  for  the  date  of  quotation  placement  of  the  stocks  of  the 
company  issuing  the  relevant  certificates  under  [§16-3]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market 
Listing Regulation.
