157 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex  1-4]  Base  Price  for  Trading  of  Initially  Listed  Stocks  and  DRs  of  Foreign 
Stocks 
[December 21, 2022] (Amended on August 8, 2023; February 27, 2025) 

Base Price for Trading of Initially Listed Stocks and DRs of Foreign Stocks 
(Pertaining to [§17] and [§27] of the Enforcement Rules) 

1. Initially Listed Issue (limited to issues falling under [§17(1)2a]) 

A.  In the case of listing only one (1) issue of common stocks 

(1) In the case of stocks that have been offered through an initial public offering or a 
secondary  distribution  after  the  date  of  application  for  the  preliminary  listing 
review pursuant to [§25] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation, the issuing 
price at the time of the initial public offering or the secondary distribution. 

(2) In cases other than the case in item (1) above, net asset value per share calculated 

according to the followings:         

(a)  The net asset value per share is calculated by dividing the net asset amount by 

the total number of shares issued as of the date of listing application. 

(b) The  net  asset  amount  in  subitem  (a)  above  shall  be  calculated  by  adding  the 
treasury stock value to  the total  assets (excluding  non-controlling  interests). In 
this case, if there has been a capital increase or decrease for the period from the 
base date of the statement of financial position submitted to the Exchange as of 
the date of new listing to the date of new listing, such amount shall be added or 
subtracted. 

        (3)  Notwithstanding  subitems  (a)  and  (b),  for  issues  listed  by  transferring  from  the 

KONEX market, the price calculated according to the followings: 

(a)  In  the  case  where  there  has  been  no  initial  public  offering  or  secondary 
distribution  after  the  date  of  application  for  the  preliminary  listing  review 
pursuant  to  [§25]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Listing  Regulation:  The  price 
whichever  is  lower  between  the  arithmetic  average  of  closing  prices  (in  cases 
where stock split, reverse stock split, ex-rights, etc. occurs, the prices adjusted 
by  considering  such  factors)  for  the  last  thirty  (30)  trading  days  (hereinafter 
referred to as the “trade execution day” in this paragraph) on which trades are 

158 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
executed  among  the  trade  execution  days  on  the  KONEX  market  and  the 
closing  price  of  the  last  trade  execution  day.  Provided  that,  if  the  number  of 
trade  execution  day  is  less  than  thirty  (30),  the  price  whichever  is  lower 
between the arithmetic average of the closing prices for all trade execution days 
and the closing price of the last trade execution day. 

(b)  In  the  case  where  there  has  been  an  initial  public  offering  or  secondary 
distribution  after  the  date  of  application  for  the  preliminary  listing  review 
pursuant to [§25] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation: 

The price = [(Price on the KONEX market  X Number of stocks (excluding the 
number of stocks sold through the secondary distribution if there is a secondary 
distribution)  before  the  initial  public  offering  or  the  secondary  distribution 
(including  stocks  acquired  by  a  listing  sponsor  pursuant  to  [§13(5)]  of  the 
KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation; the same hereinafter) + Amount of initial 
public offering or secondary distribution) / Number of stocks after initial public 
offering or secondary distribution 

                1) Case where the number of trade execution day is less than thirty (3) days; 

                2) Case where the issue is designated as investment caution issue or investment 
risk  issue  pursuant  to  [§5-3]  of  the  Market  Oversight  Regulation  for  one  (1) 
year prior to the date of listing on the KOSDAQ market; and 

                3) Case where the price on the KONEX market is higher or lower than 10/100 of               
the price at the time of the initial public offering or the secondary distribution. 

B.  In the case of initially listing both common stocks and a class of stocks at the same 

time 

(1)   In the  case  of  common  stocks,  the  price  calculated  according  to  the  method  in 

subparagraph A 

(2)   In  the  case  of  a  class  of  stocks,  the  price  calculated  according  to  the  following 

method: 

            (a) For a class of stocks that have been sold through an initial public offering or the 
secondary distribution within six (6) months before the date of listing, the price 
at  the  time  of  the  initial  public  offering  or  secondary  distribution  close  to  the 
date of listing 

            (b) For a class of stocks that has no initial public offering or secondary distribution 
within six (6) months before the date of listing application, the price calculated 
by simple arithmetic average of the base prices of the same class of stocks that 

159 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
have  been  sold  through  an  initial  public  offering  or  the  secondary  distribution 
within  six  (6)  months  before  the  date  of  listing  application.  Provided  that,  if 
there  is  no  same  class  of  stocks  that  have  been  sold  through  an  initial  public 
offering  or  the  secondary  distribution  within  six  (6)  months,  the  base  price  of 
common stocks 

    C. In the case of initially listing foreign stocks or DRs of foreign stocks 

The price at the time of an initial public offering or a secondary distribution after the                         
date  of  application  for  the  preliminary  listing  review  pursuant  to  [§60]  of  the 
KOSDAQ  Market  Listing  Regulation.  Provided  that,  if  the  price  (referred  to  as  the 
“converted  price”  in  this  subparagraph)  converted  by  applying  the  basic  rate  of 
exchange  designated  and  announced  in  accordance  with  the  Foreign  Exchange 
Transaction  Regulation  to  the  closing  price  (limited  to  the  closing  price  confirmed 
before 17:00 on the day immediately before the listing date) on the latest trading day 
on  a  foreign  stock  exchange  before  listing  is  lower  than  the  price  obtained  by 
multiplying  the  price  at  the  time  of  an  initial  public  offering  or  a  secondary 
distribution to the rate specified below, it shall be converted price. 

        (1) For common stocks (including DRs whose underlying stocks are common stocks): 

90%; and 

        (2)  For  a  class  of  stocks  (including  DRs  whose  underlying  stocks  are  a  class  of 

stocks): 50% 

2. Listing of a class of stocks for the first time after initial listing of common stocks, and 
listing of a class of stocks whose rights are different from those of other class of stocks 
already listed   

    A.  In  the  case  of  a  class  of  stocks  that  are  listed  for  the  first  time  after  the  listing  of 
common stocks, the price at  the time of  the  initial  public offering or the secondary 
distribution within six (6) months before the date of listing application. Provided that, 
if there is no initial public offering or secondary distribution, it shall be the base price 
of common stocks on the listing date. 

    B. In the case  of  a  class  of stocks listed whose rights  are different  from  those of other 
class of stocks already listed, the price at the time of the initial public offering or the 
secondary  distribution  within  six  (6)  months  before  the  date  of  listing  application. 
Provided that, if there is no initial public offering or secondary distribution, it shall 
be the following price: 

(1)   Case  where  the  same  type  of  classes  of  stocks  are  already  listed,  the  price 

160 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
calculated by simple arithmetic average of the base prices; or 

        (2)  Case  where  the  same  type  of  a  class  of  stocks  are  not  listed,  the  base  price  of     

common stocks on the listing date. 

3. Listing of DRs of foreign stocks whose rights are different from those of DRs of foreign 

stocks already listed 

    The price at the time of the initial public offering or the secondary distribution within six 
(6) months before the date of listing application. Provided that, if there is no initial public 
offering  or  secondary  distribution,  it  shall  be  the  price  calculated  by  simple  arithmetic 
average of the base prices of DRs of foreign stocks already listed. 

4. If the base price calculated in accordance with subparagraphs 1 through 3 (amount less 
than  KRW  1  is  rounded  off)  does  not  match  the  quotation  price  unit,  it  shall  be  the 
closest  price  to  that  price  among  prices  that  are  higher  than  that  price  and  match  the 
quotation  price  unit.,  and  in  the  case  where  it  is  recognized  that  the  base  price  is 
significantly  unreasonable  or  the  application  of  the  relevant  regulations  is  difficult,  the 
Exchange may set them differently. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

161 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
162 

 
 
 
[Annex 2] Method of Calculating Base Price of Issus gone Ex-dividend and Ex-right 
(Amended on October 14, 2005; August 16, 2007; December 4, 2007; February 3, 2009; July 31, 2009; Total revision on 
December 30, 2010; April 20, 2012) 

Method of Calculating Base Price of Issus gone Ex-dividend and Ex-right   
(Pertaining to [§17(1)6] of the Enforcement Rules) 

(1) Case of ex-dividends   

1.  Case  of  paying  dividend  with  the  stocks  whose  class  is  the  same  as  the  class  of 
already-listed stocks   

a. Base price of common stocks = (Closing price of cum dividend common stocks × 
Number  of  common  stocks  before  dividends)  /  (Number  of  common  stocks  before 
dividends + Number of common stocks allotted to shareholders of common stocks)   

b. Base price of preferred stocks = (Closing price of cum dividend preferred stocks × 
Number  of  preferred  stocks  before  dividends)  /  (Number  of  preferred  stocks  before 
dividends + Number of preferred shares paid as dividends to shareholders of preferred 
stocks) 

2. Case of paying dividend with either the common stocks or different classes of stock 
to the already listed common stocks and different classes of stock   

a. Case of paying dividend with common stocks   

i. Base price of common stocks = (Closing price of cum dividend common stocks × 
Number of common stocks before dividend payment) / (Number of common stocks 
before  dividend  payment  +  Number  of  common  shares  paid  as  dividends  to 
shareholders of common stocks)   

ii.  Base  price  of  different  classes  of  stock  =  [(Closing  price  of  cum  dividend 
different classes of stock × Number of different classes of stock before dividends) - 
(Base price of common stocks x Number of common shares paid as dividends to the 
shareholders  of  different  classes  of  stock)]  /  Number  of  different  classes  of  stock 
before dividends   

b. Case of paying dividend with different classes of stock   

i. Base price of common stocks = [(Closing price of cum dividend common stocks × 
Number  of  common  stocks  before  dividend)  -  (Issue  price  of  different  classes  of 

163 

 
   
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
stock  x  Number  of  different  classes  of  shares  paid  as  dividend  to  shareholders  of 
common stocks)] / Number of common stocks before dividends   

ii. Base price of different classes of stock = (Closing price of cum dividend different 
classes of stock × Number of different classes of stock before dividends) / (Number 
of different classes of stock before dividend + Number of different classes of stock 
paid as dividends to shareholders of different classes of stock)   

(2) Case of ex-rights   

1. Case of allotting stocks whose class is the same as that of stocks already listed   

a.  Base price of common shares =  (Closing  price of  cum  rights  common  stocks × 
Number of common stocks before right offering) + (Issue price of common stocks x 
Number of common shares  allotted to  shareholders of common stocks) /  (Number 
of  common  stocks  before  right  offering  +  Number  of  common  shares  allotted  to 
shareholders of common stocks)   

b. Base price of different classes of stock = [(Closing price of cum rights different 
classes  of  stock  ×  Number  of  different  classes  of  stock  before  right  offering)  + 
(Issue  price  of  different  classes  of  stock  x  Number  of  different  classes  of  stock 
allotted to shareholders of different classes of stock)] / (Number of different classes 
of  stock  before  right  offering  +  Number  of  different  classes  of  shares  allotted  to 
shareholders of different classes of stock)   

2. Case of allotting either the common stocks or different classes of stock to the already 
listed common stocks and different classes of stock   

a. Case of allotting common stocks   

i) Base price of common stocks = [(Closing price of cum rights common stocks × 
Number  of  common  stocks  before  right  offering)  +  (Issue  price  of  common 
stocks x Number of common shares allotted to shareholders of common stocks)] / 
(Number  of  common  stocks  before  right  offering  +  Number  of  common  shares 
allotted to shareholders of common stocks)   

ii)  Base  price  of  different  classes  of  stock  =  [(Closing  price  of  cum  rights 
different  classes  of  stock  ×  Number  of  different  classes  of  stock  before  right 
offering)  +  {(Issue  price  of  common  stocks  –  Base  price  of  common  stocks)  x 
Number of common shares allotted to shareholders of different classes of stock}] 
/ Number of different classes of stock before right offering   

b. Case of allotting different classes of stock   

164 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
i) Base price of common stocks = [(Closing price of cum rights common stocks × 
Number of common stocks before right offering) + {(Issue price of different classes 
of stock – Base price of different classes of stock) x Number of different classes of 
stock  allotted  to  shareholders  of  common  stocks}]  /  Number  of  common  stocks 
before right offering   

ii) Base price of different classes of stock = [(Closing price of cum rights different 
classes of stock × Number of different classes of stock before right offering + (Issue 
price of different classes of stock x Number of different classes of stock allotted to 
shareholders of  different  classes of stock)) /  (Number of  different  classes of stock 
before right offering + Number of different classes of stock allotted to shareholders 
of different classes of stock)   

iii)    In the case of allotting different classes of stock to the already listed different 
classes of stock, the method of calculating the base price of common stock noted in 
i) shall apply mutatis mutandis thereto.   

Notes:   

1. In the case of paying dividend with or allocating the stocks whose class is different from that of 
already-listed stocks, it shall be deemed that among the already-listed stocks, the stocks whose class 
is most similar to that already-listed are paid as dividend or allocated.   

2. "Closing price of cum dividend" or "closing price of cum rights" refers to the closing price on the 
day immediately before the action date of ex-rights or ex-dividend. Provided that, in the case of the 
first ex-dividend for an initially-listed issue, the closing price of cum dividend shall be the closing 
price  of an issue  whose trading volume  during  the  period  until  one (1)  month  prior to the end  of 
concerned listing year is the largest, from among the listed issues of concerned companies; in cases 
where such company is listed during the last month of the fiscal year, it shall be the closing price of 
an issue whose trading volume during such month is the largest.   

3. “Issue price” shall be the price falling under any of the followings and in the case of the capital 
increase without consideration, the issue price shall deem to be “zero.”   

(a) Of the prices that the applicant company calculated and published before the action day of ex-
rights (referring to the expected issuing prices or final issuing price), the most recent price; and   

(b) In cases where there is no price falling under the ones noted in (a) above, the price that the 
Exchange  calculated  using  the  following  formula  (in  cases  where  the  applicant  company  has 
made public the formula for calculating the issuing price, such formula shall be used: the same 
hereinafter) while taking into account such parameters as the base stock price and discount rate. 
In such cases, if the first day of calculation for the base stock price is after the action day of ex-
right  and  the  capital  increase  is  made  by  way  of  right  offering,  the  base  stock  price  shall  be 
calculated by setting the first day of calculation as “three (3) days before the record day of new 
stock distribution”, and if the capital increase is made by way of standby right offering, the base 

165 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
stock price shall be calculated by setting the first day of calculation as “three (3) day before the 
day the shareholder’s list was finalized”.   

Issue price = [Base stock price x (1 - Discount rate)]/ [1+ Ratio of bonus issue + (Ratio of paid-in 
capital increase x Discount rate)] 

4. “Number of stocks paid as dividend or allocated to the shareholders of common stocks (different 
classes of stock)” refers the number of shares calculated by multiplying the ratio of the number of 
common stocks (different classes of stock) to the total number of stock issued on the day before the 
action  date  of  ex-rights  or  ex-dividend  to  the  total  number  of  stocks  to  be  issued  as  a  result  of 
dividend or right offering.   

166 

 
 
 
[Annex 3] [Deleted on September 13, 2013] 

[Annex 4] [Deleted on September 13, 2013] 

167 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex 5] Criteria for Liquidity Assessment and Selection of Low-liquidity Issues 
(Amended on March 25, 2016; June 21, 2016; February 28, 2017; September 19, 2017; September 12, 2018; 
December 7, 2018; November 28, 2019; November 26, 2020; March 12, 2021; November 23, 2023) 

Criteria for Liquidity Assessment and Selection of Low-liquidity Issues 
(Pertaining to [§12-10, §12-12, §12-15 and §28-7] of the Enforcement Rules) 

(1) The criteria for liquidity assessment shall be as follows: 

1. The assessment target period and issue shall be as follows: 

(a) Assessment target period: From October of the year preceding the year which includes the 
selection date to September of the relevant year 

        (b) Issues subject to assessment: Stocks and DRs of foreign stocks (excluding the stocks issued 
by  SPACs  stipulated  in  [§2(30)]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Listing  Regulation,  the  issues 
scheduled to be delisted and the issues with fewer than 60 trading days during the assessment 
target period) 

2. Parameters for liquidity assessment are calculated by arithmetically averaging the daily figures 
of each of the following parameters over the number of trading days during the assessment target 
period excluding the days of trading suspension. 

(a) Turnover ratios 

The turnover ratio is calculated based on the value obtained by dividing the volume of trades 
{limited to the volume of trades concluded during the trading hours of regular sessions by the 
methods of individual auction under [§18(1)3 through 5] of the Regulation and [§19] of the 
Regulation; the same hereinafter in this Annex} by the number of listed shares. 

(b) Effective spreads 

An effective spread is the spread that reflects the average executed prices during the trading 
hours of call auction in regular sessions when the market-taking quotations in average size of 
each  issue  during  the  assessment  period  are  submitted,  and  calculated  by  the  following 
formula: 

  Effective  spread  =  (Effective  bid  spread  ÷  Quotation  price  unit)  +  (Effective  offer  spread  ÷ 

Quotation price unit), where 

 Effective bid spread = Average purchasing price – Average of the best bid and offer quotations, and 
 Effective offer spread = Average of the best bid and offer quotations – Average selling price 

        (c) Trading cycle 

168 

 
 
 
 
 
 
         
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
A trading cycle refers to the time interval between executed trades during regular sessions and 
it is calculated by the following formula. The number of trades in the formula shall be based 
on  the  number  of  trades  by  call  auctions,  and  in  the  case  of  those  issues  of  which  trading 
methods are stipulated differently pursuant to [§23] and [§23-4] of the Regulation, it refers to 
the  number  of  trades  during  the  trading  hours  of  regular  sessions  (excluding  the  number  of 
trades  executed  with  extended  scope  of  participating  quotations  as  a  result  of  the  change  in 
trading methods pursuant to [§23-3] of the Regulation): 

 Trading cycle = Regular trading hours  ÷  Number of trades 

(2) The criteria for selection of market making target issues shall be as follows: 

1. The market making target issue shall be  an issue that falls under any of the following items 
based on the result of the liquidity assessment conducted pursuant to paragraph (1): Provided that 
the  Exchange  may  select  stocks  that  are  newly  listed  or  re-listed  during  the  period  subject  to 
liquidity assessment and whose the number of trading days is less than 60 days or stocks that are 
newly listed or re-listed after the period subject to liquidity assessment as target issues subject to 
market making by a method that it determines separately. 

(a) An issue meeting all of the following criteria 

Assessment index 

Criteria for selection 

Turnover ratios 

Effective spreads 

Within  top  50%  in  the  order  of  largest  volume  among  total  issues 
subject to assessment 

Below  top  50%  in  the  order  of  smallest  spreads  among  total  issues 
subject to assessment 

Trading cycle 

Within 600 seconds (10 minutes) 

(b) An issue meeting all of the following criteria 

Assessment index 

Criteria for selection 

Turnover ratios 

Effective spreads 

Below  top  50%  in  the  order  of  largest  volume  among  total  issues 
subject to assessment 

Within  top  50%  in  the  order  of  smallest  spreads  among  total  issues 
subject to assessment 

Trading cycle 

Within 600 seconds (10 minutes) 

(c) An issue meeting all of the following criteria 

Assessment index 

Criteria for selection 

Turnover ratios 

Effective spreads 

Within  top  50%  in  the  order  of  largest  volume  among  total  issues 
subject to assessment 

Within  top  50%  in  the  order  of  smallest  spreads  among  total  issues 
subject to assessment 

Trading cycle 

Within 600 seconds (10 minutes) 

169 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2. Notwithstanding subparagraph 1, an issue that falls under any of the following criteria shall be 
excluded from the list of market making target issues: 

(a) An issue with a liquidity provision agreement in force as of the last day of the assessment 
target period;   

(b) An issue with a market capitalization of KRW 10 trillion or more as of the last trading day 
of the liquidity assessment target period; and   

(c) Other issues that the Exchange deems to be excluded from the list of market making target 
issues for the purpose of market administration.   

3. Timing of selection 

The selection and the public announcement of the result thereof shall be made by December  of 
the year in which the end date of the assessment target period falls. 

4. Effective period 

The  selection  shall  be  effective  from  January  to  December  of  the  year  following  the  year  in 
which the selection date falls. 

5.  Notwithstanding  subparagraphs  (c)  and  (d),  in  cases  where  it  is  deemed  necessary  for  the 
market management, the Exchange may determine the timing of selection, the timing of public 
announcement, and the effective period for market making target issues differently. 

(3) The selection criteria of low liquidity issues subject to call auction shall be as follows: 

1. The low liquidity issues subject to call auction shall be the issues of which the trading cycle 
exceeds 600 seconds or 10 minutes, according to the result of the liquidity assessment conducted 
pursuant to paragraph (1). 

    2. Notwithstanding subparagraph 1, an issue that falls under any of the following items during the 
period from the assessment period to the trading day immediately before the first trading day of 
the effective period shall be excluded from the list of low liquidity issues subject to call auction. 

(a) [Deleted on September 12, 2018] 

(b) An issue with a liquidity provision agreement in force; and 

(c) An issue of which average trading cycle for the 3 months immediately preceding the first 
trading  day  of  the  effective  period  (the  last  trading  day  of  the  latest  3  months  shall  be 
excluded;  the  same  hereinafter in this  Paragraph) is 60  seconds  or shorter  shall  be  excluded 
from the list of low liquidity issues subject to call auction. 

170 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
   
 
 
 
 
3. Timing of selection 

The selection and the public announcement of the result thereof shall be made by December of 
the year in which the end date of the assessment target period falls. 

4. Effective period 

The  selection  shall  be  effective  from  January  to  December  of  the  year  following  the  year  in 
which the selection date falls.   

5.  Notwithstanding  subparagraphs  3  and  4,  in  the  case  of  an  issue  falling  under  any  of  the 
following cases after the effective period may be excluded from or additionally included to the 
list of low liquidity issues subject to call auction in accordance with the manner specified in each 
of  such  cases.  In  such  cases,  the  effective  period  shall  be  from  the  relevant  month  to  the  last 
trading day of the month in which the period under subparagraph 4 ends. 

(a) [Deleted on September 12, 2018] 

(b)  In  the  case  of  an  issue  for  which  a  liquidity  provision  agreement  was  entered  into:  the 
exclusion  begins  from  the  month  following  the  month  to  which  the  effective  date  of  the 
agreement belongs; 

(c) In the case of an issue of which average trading cycle for the latest three (3) months is sixty 
(60) seconds or shorter: the exclusion begins from the month following the month when the 
average trading cycle was calculated; 

(d) In the case of an issue of which liquidity provision agreement was terminated or expired 
during  the  effective  period  after  the  assessment period:  the  additional  inclusion begins  from 
the month following the month to which the next day of the effective date of termination or 
the expiry date of the agreement belongs; and 

(e)  In  the  case  of  an  issue  of  which  average  trading  cycle  for  the  latest  three  (3)  months 
exceeds  sixty  (60)  seconds:  the  additional  inclusion  begins  from  the  month  following  the 
month when the average trading cycle was calculated. 

171 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
         
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex 5-2] Criteria for Selection of Market Makers and Issues for Market Making 
[March 25, 2016] (Amended on February 28, 2017; December 7, 2018; July 13, 2022) 

Criteria for Selection of Market Makers and Issues for Market Making 
(Pertaining to [§12-13] of the Enforcement Rules) 

(1)  The  Exchange  shall  select  a  market  maker  based  on  its  basic  capabilities  for  market 
making and its performance, etc.   

(2) A market maker may choose the issue subject to market making in accordance with the 
criterion specified in each the following subparagraphs: 

1. Priority: The priority in selecting market making issues shall be given in the order of 
the assessment scores on eligibility of each market maker. 

2. Method of selection: Each market maker sequentially picks market making issues, the 
number  of  which  shall  not  exceed  the  number    determined  by  the  Exchange  in 
consideration of the priority stated in Subparagraph (a) and the total  number of market 
making issues. 

172 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex 5-3] Guidelines for Assessment of Market Makers and Making Payments for 
Market Making, etc. 
[March 25, 2016] (Amended on February 28, 2017; September 19, 2017; December 7, 2018; December 27, 
2018;    March 12, 2021; August 2, 2022; November 23, 2023) 

Guidelines for Assessment of Market Makers and Making Payments for   
Market Making, etc. 
(Pertaining to [§12-14, §12-16, §12-18, §12-19 and §12-20] of the Enforcement Rules) 

(1) The criteria for assessment of daily fulfillment of market making obligations shall be as 
follows:   

    1. The period subject to assessment and the subjects to be assessed shall be as follows: 

(a) Assessment period: All the trading days when the market making obligations have 
occurred  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “number  of  market  making  days”).  Provided 
that, if the occurrence time of quotation obligation for a day is less than one hour (or 
3,600 seconds), such day shall be excluded. 

(b) Subjects to be assessed: All of the market making issues for each market maker 

2.  Criteria  for  assessment  of  daily  obligations:  When  the  ratio  of  daily  fulfillment  of 
obligations  of  a  trading  day,  which  is  calculated  in  accordance  with  the  following 
formula,  is  80%  or  higher,  such  day  shall  be  deemed  a  day  for  which  daily  market 
making obligation is fulfilled (hereinafter referred to as a “obligation-fulfilled day”). 

Ratio of daily 
fulfillment of 
obligations =   

Maintaining time of market making quotation that fulfilled the obligation (the 
time  period  during  which  market  making  quotations  have  been  maintained  at 
the level of both the obligatory spread and the minimum amount for quotation 
maintenance stipulated in the market making agreement) 

Occurrence time of quotation obligation (the time period during which the 
quotation obligations have occurred) 

    (a) Occurrence time of quotation obligation: The quotation-receiving time during the 
time  period  from  the  market  opening  to  the  time  before  the  commencement  of  call 
auction  to  determine  the  closing  price  under  [§18(1)2]  of  the  Regulation,  excluding 
each of the followings (in seconds) 

(i) The time falling under each of the subparagraphs under [§12-15(2)]; and 

173 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(ii) In cases where an issue falls under causes for suspension or termination of 
market making pursuant to the market making agreement, such time period of 
suspension or termination. 

(b) Maintaining time for obligatory quotations: The time (in seconds) during which the 
market making quotations that were submitted for market making issues according to 
each of the subparagraphs under [§12-15(1)] have been maintained. Provided that the 
time  during  which  the  obligation  to  maintain  market  making  quotations  is  exempted 
pursuant to [§12-16] shall be excluded. In such cases, the minimum quotation quantity 
shall be calculated as follows: 

  (i) Offer quotations 

      a) In cases where the best bid quotation exists: 

Minimum amount for quotation maintenance 
Best bid quotation + 1 tick 

      b) In cases where the best bid quotation does not exist: 

Minimum amount for quotation maintenance 
Best offer quotation 

c) In cases where either the best bid or the best offer quotation does not exist: 

Minimum amount for quotation maintenance 
Immediately preceding price 

    (ii) Bid quotations 

a) In cases where the best bid quotation exists: 

Minimum amount for quotation maintenance 

Best offer quotation - 1 tick 

b) In cases where the best offer quotation does not exist: 

Minimum amount for quotation maintenance 

Best bid quotation 

c) In cases where either the best bid or the best offer quotation does not exist: 

174 

 
 
 
 
       
 
                     
 
           
   
 
             
 
 
 
Minimum amount for quotation maintenance 

Immediately preceding price 

(2)  The  criteria  for  assessment  of  final  fulfillment  of  obligations  and  the  activeness 
(hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “activeness  in  fulfillment  of  obligations”)  in  fulfilling 
obligations shall be as follows:   

1. The criteria for assessment of final fulfillment of obligations shall be as specified  in 
each of the following items and an issue of which assessment indicator specified in item 
(b) is 90% or higher shall be deemed an “obligation-fulfilled issue”: 

(a) Assessment period: Each quarter during the term of market making agreement; and 

(b) Assessment indicator: Ratio of obligation fulfillment calculated in accordance with 
the following formula on a quarterly basis. 

Ratio of obligation fulfillment 
= 

Number of days for which the obligation was fulfilled 
during the quarter 

Number of days for market making during the quarter 

2.  The  scores  of  assessment  of  activeness  shall  be  calculated  by  adding  up  the  daily 
average  of  each  of  the  following  indicators  during  the  days  for  market  making  of  a 
quarter.  Provided  that  an  issue  that  is  assessed  not  to  be  an  obligation-fulfilled  issue 
pursuant to subparagraph 1 shall be excluded from those subject to assessment.   

(a) The ratio of daily fulfillment of obligations noted in subparagraph 2 of paragraph 
(1); and 

(b) The ratio of maintaining the best quotations that is calculated in accordance with 
the following formula: 

Ratio of maintaining best 
quotations = 

The time of a trading day during which the market 
making quotations were maintained with the best 
quotations (sum of offers and bids) 

The time of a trading day during which the market 
making quotations fulfilling the daily quotation 
obligation were maintained. 

(3)  In  cases  where,  as  a  result  of  the  assessment  of  the  final  fulfillment  of  obligations 
pursuant  to  subparagraph  1  of  paragraph  (2),  a  market  maker  has  failed  to  fulfill  the 

175 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
obligations,  the  Exchange  may  take  measures  of  imposition  of  demerit  points  and/or 
suspension  of  qualification  against  the  marker  make  concerned,  pursuant  to  the  criteria 
specified in each of following subparagraphs:   

1. The criteria for imposing demerit points: In cases where the number of days obtained 
by subtracting the minimum number of days with fulfilled obligations [referring to 70% 
of  the  total  number  of  market  making  days  during  a  quarter  (the  decimal  places  are 
rounded  off)]  from  the  number  of  obligation-fulfilled  days  during  the  quarter  for  each 
market making issue falls under any of following items, the demerit points specified in 
the relevant item. 

(a) Fewer than 5 days: 1 point; 
(b) 5 or more but less than 10 days: 2 points;     
(c) 10 or more but less than 20 days: 3 points   
(d) 20 or more but less than 30 days: 4 points; and 
(e) 30 days or more: 5 points 

2. Criteria for suspension of qualification and effect thereof: In cases where accumulated 
demerit points for total market making issues of a market maker in the relevant year is 
more  than  the  point  set  forth  in  each  of  the  following  items,  the  qualification  of  the 
market maker shall be suspended, and the suspension of qualification shall be effective 
for the period set forth in [§12-19(2)], terminating the agreement for market making. 

(a) In cases where the number of market making issues (shall be based on the number 
of market making issues that have market making agreements in force as of the end of 
the assessment quarter; the same hereinafter in this Subparagraph) is less than 50: 50 
points 

(b)  In  cases  where  the  number  of  market  making  issues  is  50  or  more  but  less  than 
100: 100 points 

(c) In cases  where the number of market making issues is  100 or more but less than 
200: (No. of issues×1.5) points 

(d) In cases where the number of market making issues is 200 or more: (No. of 
issues×2) point 

(4)  The  Exchange  may  make  payments  for  market  making  of  market  makers  for  each 
market making issue pursuant to the criteria specified in each of following subparagraphs:   

1. Issues subject to payment: The obligation-fulfilled issues according to the result of the 
quarterly assessment noted in subparagraph 1 under paragraph (2) (hereinafter referred to 
as the “issues subject to payment”) 

176 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2.  Criteria  for  calculation  of  payments  for  market  making:  The  amount  calculated  by 
multiplying all of the following indicators for each of the issues subject to payment. 

(a)  Fee  revenue:  The  fee  revenue  of  the  Exchange  earned  from  the  issues  subject  to 
payment, which is the sum of trading fees and clearing fees. 

(b)  Trading  share  of  issues  subject  to  payment:  The  figure  obtained  by  dividing  a 
market  maker’s trading  volume of the issues subject  to  payment  during  a quarter by 
the total trading volume of the issues subject to payment during the quarter, pursuant 
to the following criteria. 

(i)  Total  quarterly  trading  volume  of  the  issues  subject  to  payment:  Accumulated 
quarterly  trading  volume  which  is  the  sum  of  purchasing  and  selling  trading 
volumes. 

(ii)  A  market  maker’s  quarterly  trading  volume  of  the  issues  subject  to  payment: 
The trading volume that has been executed by a market maker out of accumulated 
trading volume of an issue subject to payment during a quarter. Provided that cross 
transactions,  trading  volume  executed  by  other  quotations  or  the  quotations  that 
were  not  submitted  in  accordance  with  the  submission  methods  of  market  making 
quotations noted in [§12-10] shall be excluded. 

(c)  Payment  rates:  The  payment  rates  are  determined  by  dividing  the  assessment 
scores on the activeness  in fulfilling obligations for the issues  subject to payment by 
“200”. 

3. Payment of fixed amount of compensation 

The  amounts  pre-determined  in  the  market  making  agreement  shall  be  paid  to  the 
issues specified in the agreement, from among the issues subject to payment. 

4. Timing of payments: Payments shall be made within three (3) months after the end of 
each quarter. Provided that, when the Exchange deems it necessary due to changes in the 
contents  of  market  making  agreements,  the  timing  of  payment  may  be  determined 
differently.   

(5)  The  Exchange  shall  terminate  the  market  making  agreement  for  the  relevant  issue  in 
cases where the  average daily turnover ratio (excluding the last seven (7) trading  days of 
each quarter) assessed every quarter pursuant to the following subparagraph 1 exceeds the 
ratio in subparagraph 2 for two (2) consecutive quarters: 

177 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
     
 
 
 
 
 
1.  Turnover  ratio:  The  turnover  ratio  is  calculated  based  on  the  volume  of  trades 
{limited to the volume of trades concluded during the trading hours of regular sessions 
by the methods  of individual  auction under  [§18(1)3 through 5] of the Regulation and 
[§19] of the Regulation; the same hereinafter in this Annex} divided by the number of 
listed shares. 

2.  Ratio: 15% 

178

[Annex: Form No. 6-5] Standard Agreement for Market Making in KOSDAQ Market 
(Amended  on  March  25,  2016)  (Amended  on  February  28,  2017;  September  19,  2017;  March  12,  2021; 
August 2, 2022; December 21, 2022; November 23, 2023) 

Standard Agreement for Market Making in KOSDAQ Market 

The  Korea  Exchange  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  Exchange”)  and  xxx  Securities 
Company (hereinafter referred to as “the market maker”) hereby enter into a market making 
agreement  pursuant  to  [§12-7]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Business  Regulation  (hereinafter 
referred  to  as  “the  Regulation”)  and  [§12-14]  of  the  Enforcement  Rules  of  KOSDAQ 
Market Business Regulation (hereinafter referred to as “the Enforcement Rules”). 

Article 1. Purpose of agreement 
The  market  maker  shall  submit  quotations  or  execute  trades  to  improve  the  liquidity  of 
stocks or DRs that were designated by the Exchange (hereinafter referred to as the “market 
making”)  and  the  Exchange  shall  make  payments  for  the  market  making  of  the  market 
maker (hereinafter referred to as the “payments for market making”). 

Article 2. Term of agreement 
(1) This  agreement shall remain valid and in full effect  during the period specified in the 
separate statement (hereinafter referred to as “the statement”). 
(2)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1),  in  cases  where  the  market  making  is  terminated 
pursuant to the provisions of Article 9 hereof for each market making issue stated in Article 
3 hereof, the term shall end on the date of termination. 

Article 3. Market making issue 
The market making issue shall be a stock or DR for which the market maker shall make the 
market  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  market  making  issue”)  and  the  starting  date  of 
market making shall be as specified in the statement. 

Article 4. Obligations of market maker 
(1) The market maker shall report one (1) account that is exclusively for market making to 
the  Exchange  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “market  making  account”)  according  to  the 
method  stipulated  by  the  Regulation,  etc.,  and  the  market  making  shall  be  carried  out 
through  this  account.  In  such  case,  when  a  market  maker  submits  quotations  through  the 
relevant  account,  it  shall  not  input  anything  other  than  matters  in  each  of  the  following 
Subparagraphs: 

1. Type of account: [11] Market making account 

2. Type of market making quotation: 2 

189 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) The market maker shall designate two (2) or more officers and employees who will be 
responsible for market making and report it to the Exchange. 
(3)  The  market  maker  shall  continuously  submit  and  maintain  market  making  quotations 
that  satisfy  the  conditions  specified  in  [§12-10]  of  the  Enforcement  Rules  for  the  market 
making issues throughout the term of agreement. In such cases, the method of submission 
of  quotations  for  the  fulfillment  of  obligations  -  the  obligatory  spreads,  the  minimum 
quotation size, etc. - shall be as stipulated in the statement. 
(4) If the market maker intends to submit the quotations for covered short sales under [§9-
2(2)] of the Regulation, the market maker shall have an internal control device that allows 
to submit quotations only if the relevant listed stocks are borrowed. 
(5)  The  market  maker  shall  report  to  the  Exchange  as  a  high-speed  algorithmic  trader  in 
advance. In the case where the market maker submits the quotations for the fulfillment of 
obligations,  it  shall  affix  the  self-match  prevention  condition  under  [§18-3]  of  the 
Enforcement Rules to the quotations, except in unavoidable cases. 
(6)  The  market  maker  shall  complete  the  training  programs  on  the  prevention  of  unfair 
trading provided by the Exchange after entering into the market making agreement. 
(7)  The  market  maker  may  not  transfer  or  entrust  the  rights  and  obligations  under  the 
market making agreement to a third party without the prior written consent of the Exchange.   

Article 5. Assessment of market making performance 
The  Exchange  shall  make  assessment  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “market  making 
assessment”) of whether or not the market maker has fulfilled the market making obligation 
stated in Article 4  hereof during the quarter  for  assessment (hereinafter referred to as the 
“assessment  quarter”)  on  a  quarterly  basis  and  notify  the  market  maker  of  the  result  in 
written form by the time for making the payments for market making specified in Article 7 
hereof  after  the  end  of  assessment  quarter.    Provided  that,  in  cases  where  the  number  of 
market  making  days  during  the  assessment  quarter  (referring  to  the  number  of  market 
making  days  specified  in  the  “guidelines  for  assessment  of  market  makers  and  making 
payments for market making, etc.”; the same shall apply hereinafter) is fewer than five (5) 
days, the market making assessment may not take place. 

Article 6. Suspension of qualification of market maker 
In cases where the market maker, according to the result of assessment of market making 
performance conducted pursuant Article 5 hereof, has failed to perform its market making 
obligations faithfully and consequently falls under the criteria specified in  [§12-19] of the 
Enforcement Rules, the Exchange shall suspend the qualification of the market maker. 

Article 7. Payments for market making 
(1)  Based  on  the  result  of  the  assessment  of  market  making  performance  of  the  market 
maker  conducted  pursuant  to  Article  5  hereof,  the  Exchange  may  make  a  payment  for 
market  making  for  the  market  making  issue  for  which  market  making  obligation  was 
faithfully fulfilled.   

190 

 
 
 
 
 
(2)  The  guidelines  for  payment,  calculation  of  amount  and  time  for  making,  etc.  of  the 
payments  for  market  making  mentioned  in  paragraph  (1)  shall  be  as  specified  in  the 
“guidelines  for  assessment  of  market  makers  and  making  payments  for  market  making, 
etc.” that are set by the Exchange, unless otherwise stipulated in this Agreement. 

Article 8. Exception to payment for market making   
(1) Notwithstanding Article 7 hereof, the Exchange may not pay all or a part of payments 
for market making for the relevant quarter to the market maker in the case of falling under 
any of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Where  the  market  making  assessment  stipulated  in  Article  5  hereof  has  not  been 
conducted; 
2. Case of falling under any of subparagraphs 2 through 5 of paragraph (1) of Article 11; 
and 
3.  Where  the  market  maker  who  intends  to  terminate  the  market  making  agreement 
pursuant  to  paragraph  (2)  of  Article  11  hereof  has  not  fully  performed  the  explanation 
obligations. 

(2) In cases when the Exchange has decided not to make the payments for market making 
wholly or partially pursuant to paragraph (1) hereof, the Exchange shall notify the market 
maker in writing of the decision on and the reasons for the non-payment. 

Article 9. Termination of market making   
(1) In cases where a market making issue falls under any of the following subparagraphs, 
the market making by the market maker for the relevant issue shall be terminated. 

1.  Where  the  average  daily  turnover  ratio  (excluding  the  last  seven  (7)  trading  days  of 
each  quarter)  is  assessed  every  quarter  pursuant  to  [§12-14(6)1]  of  the  Enforcement 
Rules  and  it  exceeds  15%  for  two  (2)  consecutive  quarters.  In  such  case,  the  market 
making for the relevant issue shall terminate at the end of the concerned quarter; 
2. Where the relevant issue is delisted; 
3.  Where  the  liquidity  provision  agreement  pursuant  to  [§12-3]  of  the  Regulation  was 
concluded and is in force; and 
4. Other cases that the Exchange deems necessary for market management. 

(2)  In  cases  where  any  of  the  causes  specified  in  each  of  followings  has  occurred  to  a 
market  making  issue,  the  market  maker  may  request  the  Exchange  for  the  termination  of 
market making for the relevant issue: 

1. Where a resolution on being merged into another corporation or delisting was made; 
2. Where a resolution on spin-off was made; 
3.  Where  a  resolution  on  merger,  stock  swap,  business  takeover,  asset  takeover, 
investment-in-kind, etc. noted in [§18-4(1)] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation 
was made; 
4. Where the cause for review on listing maintenance eligibility has occurred; and 
5.  Other  reasons  equivalent  to  subparagraphs  1  through  4  hereof  that  may  cause  a 
significant  change  in  the  corporate  entity  of  the  market  making  issue  or  a  significant 
effect on the sustainability of listing have occurred. 

191 

 
 
 
(3)  When  requesting  for  the  termination  of  market  making  pursuant  to  paragraph  (2),  the 
market  maker  shall  make  a  written  notice  which  states  the  cause  of  termination  to  the 
Exchange, and the date of termination shall be the day immediately following the day when 
the Exchange has made the decision on the termination of the market making. 

Article 10. Suspension of market making   
In cases where a market making issue falls under any of the followings, the market making 
of the relevant issue by the market maker in charge shall be suspended during the periods 
specified in each of the followings: 

1.  The  period  from  the  time  when  the  cause  for  delisting  occurred  to  the  time  of 
delisting; 
2. The period of time during which the issue remain designated as an administrative issue 
or an investment caution issue; and 
3. [Deleted on March 12, 2021] 

Article 11. Termination of agreement, etc. 
(1)  The  Exchange  may  terminate  the  market  making  agreement  with  the  market  maker  if 
any of the following subparagraphs occurs: 

1.  In  cases  where  it  becomes  impossible  to  perform  the  market  making  or  securities 
trading  due  to  the  bankruptcy,  business  suspension,  revoked  authorization,  withdrawal 
from membership, etc. of the market maker; 
2. In cases where the market maker significantly undermines legal order by such acts as 
breaching the laws and regulations relating to the payment of securities transaction taxes 
by intention or gross negligence and commits the acts falling under any of the following 
cases: 

(a)  Where  the  market  maker  trades  non-market  making  issues  through  the  market 
making accounts; and 
(b) Where the market maker has been subject to sanctions from the tax authorities due 
to any untruthful reports on market making. 

3.  In  cases  where  market  maker  has  been  subject  to  sanctions  equivalent  to  or  heavier 
than penalty surcharge from the Financial Services Commission or member fine (limited 
to a fine amounting to KRW 10 million or more) from the Exchange for unfair trading, 
etc.  with  respect  to  market  making  tasks  related  to  stocks  (referring  to  market  making 
tasks  for  stocks  in  the  KOSPI  and  KOSDAQ  markets  and  equity  derivatives  in  the 
derivatives market); 
4. In cases where the market maker has violated the confidentiality obligation stipulated 
in  Article  14  hereof.  Provided  that  this  provision  shall  not  apply  to  the  case  when  the 
market maker provides documents to the tax authorities to obtain the exemption from the 
securities  transaction  tax  in  accordance  with  subparagraph  3  of  paragraph  (1)  under 
Article 117 of the Restriction of Special Taxation Act; 
5. In cases where the market maker has refused or made a false, delayed or understated 
reports with respect to the request or demand made by the Exchange pursuant to Article 
15 hereof or the matters to be reported, without any extraordinary circumstances; 

192 

 
 
 
6.  In  cases  where  the  market  maker  falls  under  the  causes  for  the  suspension  of 
qualification noted in Article 6 hereof;   
7. In cases where the market maker transfers or entrusts the rights and obligations under 
the  market  making  agreement  to  a  third  party  without  the  written  consent  of  the 
Exchange; and 
8. In cases where the market maker has continuously failed to respond to or made a false 
or  understated  report  with  respect  to  any  request,  demand  or  report  made  by  the 
Exchange in relation to the market maker’s violation of obligations under Paragraph 4 ; 
9.  Other  cases  where  it  is  deemed  inappropriate  to  maintain  the  market  marking 
agreement with the market maker. 

(2)  In  cases  where  it  is  deemed  difficult  to  perform  the  market  making  tasks  due  to  a 
significant change in the contents of the agreement, internal affairs, etc., the market maker 
may terminate this agreement in consultation with the Exchange. In such cases, the market 
maker shall explain faithfully the reasons why it is difficult to conduct the market making 
to the Exchange. 
(3)  When  intending  to  terminate  this  agreement  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1),  the  Exchange 
shall notify the market maker of the cause of termination, termination date, etc. in writing 
no later than five (5) trading days before the termination date. 
(4)  When  intending  to  terminate  this  agreement  pursuant  to  paragraph  (2),  the  market 
maker shall notify the Exchange of the cause of termination in writing no later than the last 
trading day of the first month of a quarter. In such cases, the termination of agreement shall 
be effective from the first day of the quarter following the quarter to which the notification 
date belongs. 
(5)  The  market  maker  shall  inform  the  Exchange  without  delay  when  any  of  the  causes 
noted in subparagraphs 1 through 3 of paragraph (1) occurs. 

Article 12. Change in agreement etc. 
The  Exchange  and  the  market  maker  may  change  the  contents  of  the  market  making 
agreement by mutual consultation even during the term of agreement. 

Article 13. Disclosure of market making details 
The Exchange may disclose all market makers’ trading volume, covered short sale volume 
and  the  individual  market  maker’s  performance  of  implementing  obligations  pursuant  to 
Article 4 hereof on a quarterly basis on the website of the Exchange, etc. 

Article 14. Confidentiality obligation, etc. 
The market maker shall not disclose the material contents of this agreement to any party or 
to the public without prior consent from the Exchange. 

Article 15. Request for change of market making staff 
(1)  In  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  is  inappropriate  for  a  market  making  staff 
designated by the market maker, taking the expertise, morality, etc. into account, to perform 
the market making tasks, the Exchange may request the market maker for the change of the 

193 

 
 
 
 
 
 
relevant  market  making  staff  pursuant  to  the  regulation,  and  the  market  maker  shall 
faithfully  comply  with  such  request  for  the  change  of  staff-in-charge  unless  there  exist 
extraordinary circumstances otherwise.   
(2)  The  Exchange  may  request  for  documents  or  demand  cooperation  in  business  to  the 
market  maker  in  case  when  it  is  necessary  for  the  effective  implementation  of  this 
agreement,  and  the  market  maker  shall  faithfully  comply  with  such  request  or  demand 
unless there exist extraordinary circumstances otherwise. 
(3)  The  market  maker  shall  take  necessary  actions  for  the  Exchange  in  making  inquiries 
into  details  of  trades  through  the  market  making  account  in  order  to  conduct  businesses 
relating to the market making or the exemption from securities transaction tax. 
(4)  In  the  case  of  having  been  sanctioned  by  the  tax  authorities  in  relation  with  the 
payments of securities transaction tax, the market maker shall make a report on such fact to 
the Exchange without delay. 

Article 16. Exemption from liability 
The  market  maker  has  no  right  to  make  an  objection  or  claim  damages  against  the 
Exchange  in  cases  where  the  Exchange  makes  changes  to  the  market  making  system  and 
takes  other  related  actions  in  accordance  with  the  Act,  Enforcement  Decree,  Regulations 
and Enforcement Rules relating to the securities trade. 

Article 17. Application of Regulation 
Other matters which are not stipulated in this agreement shall comply with the Regulations 
and Enforcement Rules of the Exchange. 

We, the Exchange and the Company, hereby sign and affix our seals on two copies of the 
Agreement and keep one copy each as a proof of entering into the Agreement. 

Date: mm/dd/yyyy 

For and on behalf of the Korea Exchange:    _________________________   

President & CEO 
KOSDAQ Market Division   

For and on behalf of the Company:    _________________________   

Representative director 
xxxx Securities Company 

194 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex:  Form  No.  6-6]  Written  Report  on  Changes  in  Quantity  of  Stocks  held  in

General  Borrowed  Total 

Notes:   
1.  In  the  “on-exchange”  changes  in  quantity  held,  the  quantity  purchased  in  the  regular  sessions  less  the 
quantity sold shall be stated. 
2.  In  the  “borrowed”  and  “others”  changes  in  quantity  held,  the  incoming  quantity  (based  on  the  incoming 
date) less the outgoing quantity (based on the outgoing date) shall be stated.   

Attachment: Evidential document for OTC trades 

Date: mm/dd/yyyy 
Name of company: xxxx Co., Ltd. 
Name and seal of representative: 
(Staff-in-charge: Name                Contact number              )

[Annex: Form No. 9] Agreement on Correction of Transaction Errors 
(Amended on February 3, 2009) 

Agreement on Correction of Transaction Errors 

The  Korea  Exchange  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  "the  Exchange")  and  xxx  Securities 
Company,  Ltd.,  who  is  a  member  of  the  Exchange  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  "the 
Company")  agree  on  the  following  terms  and  conditions  for  the  correction  of  transaction 
errors  occurred  in  the  course  of  execution  of  trades  on  the  KOSDAQ  Market  by  the 
Exchange  and  the  errors  occurred  due  to  the  failures  of  the  Exchange  computer  system 
(hereinafter referred to as "transaction errors").   

Article  1.  In  cases  where  any  transaction  error  has  occurred  during  the  course  of  trade 
execution  by  the  Exchange,  the  Company  shall  assume  such  transaction  error  as  an  own 
account transaction upon receiving the request from the Exchange (see [Annex: Form No. 
10]: Request for correction of transaction errors).   

Article 2. The Company shall trade the issues assumed upon receipt of the request from the 
Exchange by the way of reverse trade whose quotation participates in the determination of 
the  opening  price  on  the  following  day.  Provided  that,  when,  due  to  the  unavoidable 
reasons  such  as  the  failure  of  the  Exchange  computer  system,  placing  quotations 
participating  in  the  determination  of  the  opening  price  was  not  possible,  the  assumed 
securities  shall  be  traded  by  way  of  reverse  trade  (except  in  the  case  of  bonds)  whose 
quotations participate in the determination of the closing price. The results of such reverse 
trade (see [Annex: Form No. 11]: Notification of Correction of Transaction Errors) shall be 
reported to the Exchange without delay. In cases where the assumed transaction error is not 
cleared by the reverse trade on the following day, it shall be traded by the same method on 
the next trading day in succession.   

Article  3.  The  Exchange  shall  settle  the  profits  and  losses  incurred  to  the  Company 
(includes  transaction  tax,  all  expenses  incidental  to  such  transactions  and  the  dues  of 
concerned member; the same hereinafter) resulting from the assuming and trading the issue 
with transaction error as requested (see [Annex: Form No. 12]: Request for Settlement for 
Handling  Transaction  Errors)  without  delay.  Provided  that  any  profits  and  losses  resulted 
from  the  errors  made  by  the  Company  in  the  course  of  handling  the  assumed  transaction 
error, shall be settled after the fact according to the request by the Exchange (see [Annex: 
Form No. 13]: Request for Settlement Adjustment for Handling Transaction Errors).   

Article  4.  If  there  is  any  difference  of  opinions  on  the  methods  of  clearing  the  profits  or 
losses  incurred,  including  the  method  of  settling  profits  and  loss  when  ex-rights  or  ex-
dividend occurs to  the issue assumed and any other matters that  are not  stipulated in  this 

198 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
agreement,  such  differences  shall  be  resolved  through  the  consultation  and  mutual 
agreement between the Exchange and the Company.   

Article  5.  This  agreement  shall  be  valid  for  one  (1)  year  from  the  date  of  signing,  and 
unless  any  objection  on  the  terms  and  conditions  of  this  agreement  is  expressed  at  least 
thirty (30) days prior to the expiry date, it shall be deemed that an agreement with the same 
terms and conditions as the one expired has been signed on its expiry date.   

We,  the  Exchange  and  the  Company,  hereby  agree  the  above-mentioned  terms  and 
conditions, and sign and seal two (2) copies of the Agreement and keep one (1) copy each 
as a proof of agreement.   

mm/dd/yyyy 

For and on behalf of the Korea Exchange _________________________   
Chairman of the Korea Exchange   

For and on behalf of the Company _________________________   
Chief Executive Officer   
xxx Securities Company

stable market management, etc.

    - Personal (credit) information is destroyed after 6 months after the cancellation of high-speed 

algorithmic trader registration
